Mile bliadan & CCCC & secht mbliadna agus cethra aís in Tigerna in bliadain roscribad in lebar-sa, & isin bliadain cetna testa O Raighilligh id_est Toirrdhelbach mac Seain, & isin bliadain cetna domarbad clann I Ruairc id_est Tigernan & Brian ruadh id_est Tigernan domarbad le clainn Mic Diarmada & le Muinntir-Eolais a fell & Brian domarbad le mac I Ruairc id_est re hEogan mac Feidhlimthe mic Donnchaid mic Tigernain; & isin bliadain cetna domarbad Tigernan dubh mac Donnchaidh caech Tigernain le O Domnaill id_est re hAedh ruadh O Domnaill, & isin bliadain cetna dobrissedh caislen I Ruairc id_est Feidlimid mac Donnchaid le O Domnaill & le clainn I Ruairc & isin bliadain cetna dogabudh Cloch Locha-huachtair le slicht Domnaill Bain I Raighilligh & me fein Diarmaid.
Ba Cathal mac Parthalain doscribh in leabar-sa id_est mac Fingin mic Foirithe mic Fergail mic Partalain & a tigh Fingin doscribad leth in lebair-sa id_est a Doire Casain & a tigh mic Briain Tellaigh-Echach dos-cribad in cuid ele de id_est a tigh arosa id_est Feidhlimid mac Taidhg oig mic Taidhg moir & ar iniss Eocinain docrichnuighedh e i n-Dardain re feil Catrina; & G is litir Domnaig annsa bliadain sin, & Sis nuimiroir, & feile mic Tomais mic Ferguis mic Tomais udh Tigerna a Tellach-Echach re linn in lebair-sia dosgribad; & isin n-aimsir cetna dobi da espoc a n-espoicdeachd Cille Moire id_est Cormac mac in espuic Megsamradhain, & Tomás mac Ainntriu Meg-bradaigh, & gach fer dibh 'ga rada gur-b e fen is espoc and; & Felim mac Donnchaidh mic Tigernain is O Ruairc re linn na n-espoc sin, & Sean mac Toirrdelbhaigh mic Seain is O Raighilligh annsan aimsir sin; & annsa bliadain chetna domarbad O Mailshechlainn id_est Laighnech O Mailshechlainn le Conn mac Airt I Mailsheachlainn.
Et bennchd De ar anmain innti dosgribh in lebar-sa.
Et dobi cogad idir Magsamradhain & O Raigailligh id_est Sean O Raighilligh isin bliadain cetna sin, & cogad ele idir slicht Taidhg I Ruairc etc.
Aroile righ uasal oirmuidnech onorach rogabh forlamhus & ferandus ar an ardcathraigh n-aibind n-alaind id_est Teibh isin n-Greic dar-ua comainm Laius, & is do-sidhe robo mac Eidhip, & is on Eidhip sin rocindset na da mac aildi oiregda id_est Polinices & Etioccles, & is iat na braithrIsin romarb a chele isin cathugud mor na Tiabhanta & na n-Grec ic cosnum righe na hardcathrach na Teibhe do cechtar leithi.
Acht cena is andsin tainic ar menmain do Stait don airdfilid Frangcach sochinelach bunadh-indruim na Tiabanta, indus rocinset o Caithim, mac Aghenoir, & is e ant Aighenoir sin rop airdrigh na Tirde & na Sidoindoine, & is aice roui in ingen sochinelach dar-ua comainm Eoropa, & is di tuc Iob in gradh ndermair, co rob hecin do tiachtain a richt tairbh da breith leis tar muinchind mara & morfaircce.
Et o rosiacht dar in muir sin cu Cred, dochuaidh 'na richt fen, & rouai in ingen sin aige co morgradhach, & is don ingin sin tuc Iop in tirfochraicc n-adhbul id_est tres primrand in betha do ainimniugud uaithi id_est Eoraip.
Agenoir immorro rogabh fercc & londus adhhul & toirrsi mor o fuair esbaid a ingine Eoropa morgradhaich.
Is i immorro comairle dorinne andsin Aghenoir, a mac morgradhach do chur ar fud mara & tire do iarraidh a sheathar uan domun, & is ed adbert ris, muna faghbad a shiair, can tiachtain aris, & gan a fhaicsin dosum.
Is andsin immorro rosirastar Caithim dingnada in domain & oilena ingantacha na haibheisi moraidhbhle thimchellas in bith, & fuair mor do dhuad & do dochar & do ghaibthith mora & tire sechnon in domain iter muir & tir, & ni fuair in ingin risin ré sin, ge r-ces mor d'imnedh, & is ed uadera sin nar-fédedh taidhecht i n-aigid Ioip mic Shatuirnd, cend na ndee, a ghradh goiti d'fis fair.
Ocus o nach fuair-sium a shiair, is i comairle dos-rat ina menmain trena ghais, dul co tempall Apaild, dei na faistine, d'iarraidh fhessa & eolais uadha cuith a roiphi in ingen.
Et is ed adbert Apaill ris, gan a sirthain, uair ni bfuighbedh, acht eirghedh amach amarach isin magh minscothach maigh-reidh moradhbul amach, & taeceradh bó bendach bithalaind duit isin magh minalaind sin, & len-sa hi nocon-luighe, & in baile a luighfea, cumdaigther letsa cathair caomcumdachta co muraib moraibhle, & co tigibh righdha rofarsenga, & co griananaib seimidhi solusglana, co mad cathair ordain & oirechtais na n-Grec in cathair sin, & co mad e a hainm id_est Boetia no Tebae tre nertudh & tre forgill in dei Apaill.
Roan-sum andsin, & rogabh itaidh, & rocuirther techtaire tairisi uadha ar cend dighe, co sithil alaind umaidhé co n-imdenum oir & airgit umpi, co huamaidh adbul imdorcha uai a comfogus do, ar lar fualascaigh coirneacdai, & tobar firalaind fondfuar ar a lar.
O rosiacht an techtaire dochum na tibra, & tuc a sithil uan usci, as andsin tainic in naithir nemhnach a hiarthar na huama, co ceithri cendaibh moraidhbhle fuirri, & co tri linaibh fiacul in cach cend fo leth, & co ndeilbh torathair o hiarthar co hoirther.
O dochonairc in techtaire os cind na tibraid, tuc beim da glomraib a n-aenfhecht cuige, go rofagadh can anmain andsin.
O ropo fada iarum le Caithim, mac Aghenoir, roui a fer muinntire, rofaidhestar fer eli da muinntir dochum na huama & dochum in usque, & tuc in naithir in aradhain cetna fair.
Cidh tra acht coica oclach torchair da muinntir amlaidh sin.
Is andsin roeirigh Caithim, mac Aghenoir, & roghabh a edegh & rotrealaim a arma, co mbruth miled, co feirg leoman, co neimh nathrach co dorus na huama da digail ar an ti romarbh a mhuinntir.
Et o rainic, adconnairc an nathraigh ndigfrecra ndimoir, & dorinne sduagh luib moir di o iarthar co hoirther, amal seolcrand lunga lanaidhbhle.
O 'tchonnairc in fer mor da hindsaigidh, rocathaighset araen andsin co foilech guinech crechtach crolinntech andsin, & torchuir an naithir fadheoidh, & dochuaidh a neimh ar nemhfni.
Tainic-sium roime iartain co tempoll Apaill, & roraidhset na dei ris ar do denum isin moigh a r-marbad an nathair; & a silad in air sin o fhiaclaib na nathrach, roeirgetar fir fon armghaisced arin tulaigh.
Rothreabh in n-uir roime, & docathaighsit co feg, feochair, fercach; & romarbh cach dibh a chéle acht aen coicer nammá; & is lesin coicer sin rochumdaighedh in Teibh, maraen re Caithim, mac Aghenoir.
Ba he oenta oiregdha in cuiger sin id_est Echion, rouoi ac cumdach na Teibhe maraen re Caithim, mac Aghenoir.
tra acht rochumdaighedh in Teith amlaidh sin re Caithim mac Aghenoir, & rouoi co soinmech setach innte re ré foda, co fhuair doinmed e uadheoidh. Uair rosoad e fen & a shetigh a ndelbaibh nathrach co cend secht mbliadan, noco tainic craidhi na ndei forro uadeoidh, & co roighsit inna corpaib fen iar sin, & is do shil innd fhir sin rochinsead na rig tromglana Thiabanda uile, & is da sil Eidip mic Lai, & robai in Lai hisin i forlamus & i fearandas na Teibe fri re fate, & is do rothirchansatar faidi & druidi, intan atchifead neach da chlaind, gu nach biad a shoegal ni bud fhaiti; conid imIsin donithea gach duine claindi roberthea do, do mudugud Is andsin darala oenda feacht Edip mac Lai do breith don morrigain Iochasta, & rucad he iarna breith co coill commoir comfhaccais, & roaithin a mathair gan a malairt na a mudugud, acht a thocbhail i crand comard comreid isinn fhidbaid, & rafacbad Eidip amlaid sin, & o rafacad he a aenur, rogab a chuideran noeidean.
Atchualaig immorro araile mac rig, robai ar fogail & ar dibeirg, in geran sin na noidean arna cengul isin chrund dar-ba comainm Polipus ainm in gilla sin.
Tanic in fer sin remi d'indsaigid na naidean, & adchondairc in naidin isinn eceandail i rroibe.
Tucastair grad ndermair do, & ruc leis e da aileamain & da altrom amal mac mbunaid do fen.
Is andsin rogabastair Polius rigi a thiri & a thalman fen, & tucastar rigdamnacht a fheraind don mac roleasaiged aicci id_est do Eidip mac Lai.
Is andsin dorala don Eidip sin tecmaill co hanbuinidi anurlum for feachtus ina deagaid sin i cend a athar Lai, & ni fhitir Lai comad he Eidip tecmad do, & ni fhitir immorro Eidip commad he a athair Lai tachrad do.
Et bai cach dib ac iarraid a sloindti uar a chele, & ni dearnaid neach dib a slondud da chele.
Rofhearadar comlond feochair feargach andsin, & torchair a athair Lai la hEidip tre ainbfhis & aneolus.
Et rogob Eidip fhearand a athar, & tucastair a mathair do chaemchele chomadais ar ngabail rigi do, & ni fhitir-sium sin cein noco tarla menma na rigna Iochassta ar cosaibh comnochta in rig id_est Eidip, uair is amlaid robadar & toll tre ceachtarde dib.
Iarfaiges in rigan:
‘Cid rotreththoll do troichthi?’ arsi andsin.
‘Ni ansa,’ ar se.
‘Is amlaid frith me ar lar na fidbaide i crund roard isin choill, & clo a cechtar adam chois acom-congbail isin chrund, & nad fetar cia nom-coraig ind ban samla sin.
Acht romailead & rom-altromad ac Polipus amal mac do fen, & nad fetar-sa nar-ba head cen no gor-hathisiged and me, & co n-ebrad rim mo bith im thurcaire thuilighi can fis m'athar no mo mathar.
D' fiarfaigus do Pholipus nar-fidir sin indissi dam mar fuair me; & as e ni doronnus, dul chom Apaill, dea na faistine, & a iarfaigid de cait a bfuigbind m'athairthir.
Raidis Apaill rimsa gan mo slondud do denam do enduine, & in cetfher tecemad dam and, comlond do chur ris, & bage-baind fis m'athar & fis mo mhathar thrit sin.
Et is e cetfer dorala cucum asa haithlIsin id_est Laius ar sechron no sechran selga acon chathraig ac Potchis, & darochair limsa é mar adchualabair sib.’
‘Truag am sin,’ ar si Iochosta, ‘robe tra in Laius sin th' athair-siu, & is misi do mathair, & is me roaithin do chengul isin chrund gan da marbad ar met do grada, & is me ruc in cethrur cloindi-sea dit id_est Eothiocles & Polenitces, Andtigone & Ismene an da ingin.’
‘Dur son damsa,’ ar Eidip, ‘geneamain, & na mignima sin do denam dam, gid tre anfhis & aneolus dorala iat.’
Is andsin immorro tuc Eidip da da laim i n-oenfheacht ceachtar a da shul, & robean asa chind iat, arbithin gu nnaran-aiced-sum neach ar met a naire a haithli na morchol sin do denam do, cona faictis sluaig na sochaide he.
Imthusa immorro da mac Eidip id_est Eothiocles & Polenices, roeirig tnuth & trenchosnum eturu im rigi na Tebe, gu narfhaem neach dib comroind na cathrach na in chiniuda d'aroile d'eis dallta a n-athar.
Ni thucsad onoir na huaisli da n-athair, acht robadar fein co diumsach drochaicentach ac caithim a n-atharda & ind fheraind, & adar le gach mac dib ba he fen bid ri and.
Dala immorro Eidip ar sin, robai co dubach domenmnach i n-uamthig thalman gan rigi gan roflaithus arna malairt & arna mudugud do fhen.
Is andsin dorigne Eidip lamchomairt moir & toirsi ndofholachta cosna deib aduathmaraib iffernaide, & co Teissifone cussin mbandea ndeamnaig ndasachtaig do sonrud, & is ed so adrubairt:
‘Roailis misi, & roaltrumais co ndernes ulca imda ilerda tre t'aslach & tre t'adanugud, co romarbus m'athair crin cianaesta acin chathraig dianaid comainm Foiccida, & rothuaslucus tre t'fhortacht-su cesta doilgi dithuaslaicthi in torathair diar-ba comainm Spinx, & is e in torathar sin robai i tír na Tiabanda, & is e rofiarfaigead do gach oen tecmad da indsaigid:
‘Cade int anmanda cetharchosta, dechosta, trerchosta?’
Et in te na tabrad tuaslucud arin ceist do, romarbad sin uile iad, cein nogo ranac-sa da indsaigid, intan roba ac iarraid m'athar, & rofhiarfaig in torathar na ceasta cetna damsa, & adrubart-sa ris cor-be in duine sin, uair ceatharchosach he ina naideanntacht id_est cona da chois & cona da laim i n-enfheacht ac imluad dho: dechosta immorro é inna ocuataid id_est & ina ferdacht id_est a da chois amain aicci ac imtheacht, trechosta immorro é ina seanntacht & ina sheanordacht id_est a da chois & a lorg aicci ac imthecht.
Et o rothaimniges in chesta sin, rofersum comlond feig fuireochair fearamail, & torchair in torathar de sin fadeoid.’
Is andsin immorro adrubaid Eidip:
‘Is tre t'fhortacht-su & tre t'fhoirithin dorignius na gnima sin, & romarbus m'athair, & rothoirrchius mo mathair, & is tre th' adandud-su robeanus mo rosc leathanglas lindfhuar as mo chind & diusigsiu iarum fich feirgi feochraigi iter mo macaib-sea id_est Etiocles & Polinices, co radluiget & co radian-scaileat in flaithius, cona roibi ceandacht no commus ac neach d'araile dib; uair ro-linastair diummus & drochciall iat tresin ndimiad & tresin ndimicin tucsad damsa ar mo beth dall dorcha i n-uamthig thalman’.
O 'tchualaich immorro Tessifone ina briathra-sa Eidip, is andsin roeirig in Fhuir demnach dasachtach cona trillsib do nathrachaib nemnecha ima ceand, ac siangail & ic sibsanaig & ic feadgaire & ac foluaimnigud & ac sugud int shrotha tibrechtaich teindtigi dar-ua comainm Cosidon, daig isinn immelbordaib int shrotha sin robid a hait & a hadba.
Is andsin rolingeastair-si co dian deinmnedach dasachtach on t-sruth amal saignen tincurach teindtigi, no amal retlaind luaith lasamhuin na firmaminti foluaimnigi, & is ead-seo sligi a tanic tresna daescurshluagaib disciri dimaine deamnacda, & tresna haireachtaib aduana etlaide do anmandaib batar in ngrianbrogaib iffrind, co ragabastair grain & ecla adbul iat ic faicsin a dreichi deamnaige duaibsigi na baidbi bruthmaire belldeirgi sin.
Et tanic-si rempi arsin dar dorus n-urbadach n-ifrind amach id_est dar Tenair.
Et o dariacht, tanic fordorchud dar dreich in talman uile amal aidchi corgab uaman & imecla lucht na crich & cendadach rempi; & tanic-si ar sin isin sligid suaichnid saineamail ar fanglendtaib slebemail co toracht co Teib.
Is andsin roeirgedar cet nathrach neimneach naimdidi com mbeandaib & birinib ima cend.
Rosuiged & rosluiged a rosc dathach dubglas in n-imdomain a cind & a ceand mullaich.
Is andsin roeirig & rochraith in nathraig nemnig robai ina laim arna sluagaib, cu clos a fogar & a breasmaidm ua cheathar airdib na Grecci id_est co sliab Barnais ar n-airthiur, & co sruth n-Eorait iar n-iarthur, & co sliab n-alaind Oeten iar ndescert, & co heochairbordaib Ismos iar tuaiscert.
Et dariacht sin co deiligthech derrscaigthech dermar cosin ciniud croda cosnumach tnudhach Tiabannda, & co macaib aidbli ailli Eidip id_est Ethiocles & Polinices co raerig fich marthanach & imfhormad adbul imon flaithius iter na da mac sin tre aslach Tesifone, amal da tharb trena thuathmeara thnuthacha ua chuing adbail imfhulaing, co raleansat & co ralagaigset a cengail & a cuibrigi ac imchosnum & ac imthairring fri araile.
Imthusa immorro na Tiabanda, nir-faelsatar imchosnum na da mac sin immon flaithius, & is i comairli rochindset andsin, rigi gach re mbliadna do gach mac dib, & cert crandchair do denum eturru, cia dib daroised in rigi ar tus, & dorignead amlaid sin.
Et rosiacht do Ethiocles in rigi a cirt chrandchair ri head na bliadna sin, & Polenices ar echtra & ar indarba ri sin.
O rocindead immorro in chomairlIsin acin popul adbul Ecionda, rogab imthnuth & emiltus iat risin rig aca rabatar, & tanic serc & sirinmaine doib innd fir robai ar echtra & ar indarba uaithib id_est Polinices.
Is andsin, immorro, adubairt araile fear soim saidhbir sochenelach don chiniud thromglan Tiabanda gu nar-ba choir don popul tren togaide fechtasugud a flaithiusa iter na rigaib oca utmalla:
‘Oir is e ar samail-ne, mar bis long luchtmar lanadbul occa tuargan o dib gaethaib condtrardaib cona fitir cia gaeth risa rachad, uair is adbul a imned & a eccomnart duind a beith ua rigi & ua rigsmacht in rig ac buileam id_est Ethiocles, & ua tamach & ua tomaitheam in rig araill id_est Polinices.’
Dala immorro Polinces meic Eidip, robai ar sibal ar sechran sechnon na crichi urairde Echionda.
Et o rabai Polinices ac triall & ac tindsceadul ar echtra & ar indarba asa tir & asa talmain, is andsin immorro tangatar imraiti imda ingantacha ar menmain don milid sin, uair ua trom & ua tendius mor leissium a fhat & a ansadaileacht co cend na bliadna sin noco roissead in rigi do.
Ua subach & ua so-menmnach e in darna fecht an tan d'airberead da uidh & da aire an rigi do rochtain do: ua hirnascda udmall a comairle in curad sin, uair ni fitir ca crich no ca cenel isin domuin i cindfedh a coimetecht ri re na bliadna sin a n-ingnais a tire, uair ni rauatar meic rig and no rofhlatha aicci risa cindfedh a comarle.
Ni rabatar didiu in tan sin amus na hoclach re hurgairdiugud seta na sibail acan fhir sin re hed na bliadna sin.
O rocindestar immorro Polinices a atharda alaind aichnid da fhacbail & indsaigid in tire anaichnig aneoil, is ed seo rogabastair roime ar fat na Grecci gartgloine do chathrachaib ingantacha Inaich in rig Grecda sin, & da bruigib dathglasa Dane, & cosin cathraig claincolaig co mac Meicinib, & is andsin rofhacaib-sium da eis na huamanda bruthmara Baichecda & tulcha togaide tondglasa na Tiauanda.
Et asa haithlIsin immorro tanic-sium roime sech in sliab soreid soimthechta Chitheron & sech cairrgib mora michluacha Sciroin & in Sciroin hisin ua latrand lanchalma i n-aroile carraic cocuasta ar caetib na conaire, & is e bes donid, gach duine rodringed isin charraic sin rofuraileadsum poccad a chos arin duine, & intan na bid ac pocad, dobered lua do co cuired ri hed n-imcian uada he, cein noco tanic Teis mac Eig meic Neptuin da indsaig, co roibe ac indmad a chos.
Is andsin tucastar Teis trentairring cuici air, & raathchuir uada é isin muir moradbail.
Dala Polinices immorro, tanic-side reime dar na bruigib sciamhda Scillecda, & seach cathrachaib taebgela insi comaird comreid Corinthon.
Is andsin immorro tanic dered dun lo & tosach don aidchi co roergedar retlanda suaichinti solusta inna haidchi imdorcha acgairbi imman esca n-adfuar n-aigreta.
Et rouatar immorro eoin & ethaide & cethra caithmecha in talman ina suan & ina sirchotlod eo mmidmedon aidchi.
Is andsin rofalchait retla roglana na firmaminti foluamnigi o nellaib imdorchaib imdaib usqidib, & rohoslaicit uamanda aidbli acgarba Éoil, ardrig na ngaeth, in tan sin co rothocaib inn ainbthine garb geimreta a tuasan & a tommaithium os aird tre chomtroit na ngaeth ngarb ngluair mbruthach mbresmadmandach dar bragaid a chele tre chetharairdib na cruindi, uair ua samalta co thaidmigtis & co ngluaisfidis fraigthi fothamla na firmaiminti asa sligthib & asa slaedraigib.
Is andsin roerig in gaeth andeas dianid comainm Auester co hainbthenach aduathmar, co radruit & co radluthaid dorchadu ndermair dar dreich thalman uile, co rachruad-chrithnaigseatar snaitheda saignen tened taidligi tresin ndilind ndifhulaing ndimoir n-ometa roferastair an uair sin, co ma fualraigthi firdoimne na coillti niamda Neimegda, & comdais locha lanaidbli lindfhuara aird & inadha na hErchaidi i crichaib tirmma tart--mara Tenair, co rolinastar tolathuile srotha & sruthana, co mbreisdis leo na feda & fiduada, con tudusstis leo na cairgi cendgarba cruaidi troma tuinidi.
Acht cid tra acht robrisit feada & fidnemeda na Greci gartglaine.
Rodluigid & rodian-scailit na coillti croma craebglasa, comdar moigi reidi roglana a n-inada da n-eis.
Ua hingnad & ua machtnugud mor re Polinices na slebti cendmora cairrgecha ac brisiud & ac breasmandugud risna buindeadaib diana dileand tictis ara trethan & ara tondgail asna sleibtib soineamail sirardaib sin.
Ua hingnad & ua haduath mor leis dano na treba & na tigi & na cethra caithmecha craesacha do lot & da lathrugud tresin fuasnad ndoninde ndermair sin.
Et is andsin tanic remi Polinices co dian & co dasachtach gan sligid & gan lansoillsi & gan laneolus.
Ach cheana ua ferrdi lesseam duibi & dorchacht na haidchi sin, uair ua hecal & ua huruamun les toir & tinol da beith aca brathair ara cind id_est Ethiocles, & dano ua ronar les gan lucht caemsa & coimidechta re hurgairdigud n-imthechta re himguin & re himbualad 'na fharrad.
Ua he immorro samail in trenfhir sin do Tiauandaib do sil calma Chathim mic Agenoir ar setaib na sliged sin amal bis stiuraigi cona luing luchtmair lanmoir ar lar in mara garbfhuair gemreta gan rind & gan retlaind d'fhaiscin re himluad n-imthechta a sin, acht seastan & seiseilbi in lera longaig lanadbail 'ga buaidread & 'ga badbrisiud, cona fitir ca cuan no ca caladport cusa rachad.
Et is andsin tanic remi Polinices, & ua hi tresi & tairpigi na-imtiged-som inn oidchi co cruithed & co cumscaiged na railgi remra roardda ac tairring a sceith moir mileta tresna coilltib clithirdiamraib, & co mbrised na feda & na fualascada da ucht & da urbruindi re hagairbi a imthechta re hingargi na huaire sin, cein noco facaid int soillsi suaichnid solusda.
Et is and bai int soillsIsin isin tur rigda roard isin chathraig dianaid comainm Larisa annsa Greic bic, & ua soillsi arar-silleastair-sium andsin lec logmar lasamuin ua comsolus la & agaid bai i coimecur in tigi roaird rigda sin.
Et is andsin tanic-seom remi 'na rem roretha d'indsaigid na cathrach Larissa, lam cle re templaib uaisli Iunaindi batar isin cathraig uraird aibind id_est Prosinda, & lam deas ri gaethlaigib lethnaib Lerna; & is andsin tanic-sium remi annund dar doirrsib urarda uraibni oslaicthi na cathrach sin, & rofegastair ime urlara fairsingi fiadnacha na cathrach sin.
Et roleceastair a chorp cubaid comfhata co haimneartach adlesc re lar & re lantalmain a haithli atchis na haidchIsin re hursaind in tigi & re hursaind na cathrach rigda sin i cubachail chruaid cumaing, & rochotail and.
Is andsin immorro tarrastair int ardri uasal airegda, Adraist, isin chathraig leathangloin lanalaind i l Larisa.
Et ua he int Adraist cianaesta comaimserda sin ua hairdri uar gasraid glanmoir Grec, uair arbithin is amlaid robai in ri soim socenelach sin, & bunadchenel a mathar & a athar Ioib mac sona saidbir sochenelach Satuirn.
Et ni raibe imsnim aireochais in rig sin acht gan immad cloindi aigi genmotha da ingin namma, & ua fiu maccu firena forglidi na hingeana gleglana geanmnaidi sin, & is ara n-inmaine na n-ingen sin doroindi-sium idbarta aidbli atmara da Apaill, co n-indisead do na fir risi faeidfidis na hingeana sin.
Et adrubairt Appaill risseom tre fhirfhaistine do denam do, commad muc adbul eccendais allaid & commad leoman leatarthach lanfergach uad cleamnada do.
Et nir-thuic Adraist in fhaistine sin, & ni mo rothuicsetar a fhilid nachu fhir eolaig.
As sIsin immorro oes & fhuair tanic Tid trom trentachrach mac Oenís id_est mac rig cuanda cathbuadach Calidone, & as ead roimluaid-side asa thir & asa thalam cusin cathraig cuanda comdaingin cetna.
Feacht n-aen dodeachaid d'fhiadach & d'fhianchoscur ria derbrathair uoden id_est ri mac murnech morgradach Ioeinius id_est re Meliager.
Et darala doib torc adbul allaid robai ac inrad in tire & in talman do marbad.
Et as e rocet-gonastair he id_est Tid mac Oenius, & is leis rate a choscur & a chomaideam re Meliager.
Et tuc a chroiceand in tuirc allaid sin da bannleannan bangaiscedaig robai isint selca sin id_est da Aithseannda no Aithleannda, & adchonnaic immorro Tid sin.
Rofhiarfaig da brathair id_est da Meliager:
‘Cid ma tucais croiceand in tuirc isa cetguine rocommaidius dat leandan?’
‘Me da marbad & da mudugud, & is aire sin thucus di.’
Asa haithlIsin immorro roerich Tid do chosnum in chroicind risin n-ingin, & rofher-sum comlund n-athlum re hAthalannda, & roclaeidead inn ingin andsin, & ruc Tid in croicend leis.
O 'dchualaig immorro Meleger in gnim sin, rogab fearg & fuasnad mor é, & tanig remi da digail sin ar Thid, & rothoit Meliager ra brathair amlaid sin id_est re Tid, conid indsin rohechtrad & rohindarbad e sin.
Et darala e isinn aidchi gairb gemreta cetna d'indsaigid na cathrach Larissa, & ua toirrseach Tid re himnead na haidchi sin; uair ua píseda fuarda oigreta a etach 'na imthimchell, & na-shildis tromchetha falcmara fleochaid asa fholt & asa edgud.
Et tanic reme annund d'indsaigid inn inaid i rroibe Polinices, & rotriall-som anad annsan inad sin.
arsin roairig Polinices sin, & adrubairt:
‘Cia dobeir in n-eicin & in n-imluad-sa orumsa adrasta?’ Is andsin adubairt Tid:
‘Erig,’ ar se, ‘& facaib damsa in n-ait & in n-adua i n-atai, co ndernaind-sea suan & sirchotlad and.’ tra acht rogabastar confad co tnuthach cosnumach, & fearga firmora fiadnacha na milead sin, cona dernsad coibnius na coicele inn ait nach a n-eninad inn aidchi sin, & ua cumair comraid & imacallma iat inn uair sin.
Is andsin rogabsatar bruth & borrfad, brig & barand, att & annini na curadu sin re chele, co rachuirset na cuingeada calma comlaind sin a n-etaigi i nn-enfhecht & a n-enaball dib dochum in comraic sin.
Polinices, immorro, ua hairddi & ua hairegda, ua rigdu & ua rochalma, ua datu & ua denmaigi é ana gach duine, & ua trichtach in trenfer sin in tan sin.
Tid, immorro, mac Oenius in trenfear calma Calidonda, fear bec bailc beoda bruthmar borrfadach alaind eccendais aninneach mermurnech mormenmnach.
Is andsin rogabastair in tuir thalchar Tiauanda id_est Polonices, sleig lethanglais lanmoir co crund datta deigremur isin dara laim do re sadud & re srainiud a escarat uad, & cloideb leathan lanfhada lanadbul re hairlech & re himbualad isin laim araill.
Tid immorro, mac Oenius, rogab a catharm catha & comraic & comlaind inn uair sin; & ger-ba lugu d'ais & do airddi in gilla sin, ua bailci & ua bunata e anda cach fear.
tra acht ba setrech sirchalma serig na tresa troma trenbemeand doberead cach dib uar a chele, cumma samalta ri tenid tricheamruaid laindrigda lasamnachta na n-arm & na n-fhilfaebar re frasugud na fola fordeirgi re corpaib & cendaib na milead moradbul sin, & ba tend in tuargain dobertis ara n-indib & ara n-ochtaib da ngluinib comnarta comfhillti i cliabaib & i compur a chele, comdais salcha sleamna na sraiteada sin re siliud & re snigi na fola a crechtaib na curad sin, & ro shinset-sum a llama adannta aindsclecha do chrechtnugud & da chruad-chascrad chuirp a chele. Acht ata ni chena.
Robad aicmeil eisinill don fhir thuathchell Tiauanda sin in comruc sin id_est do Polinices, acht mine chluinead in ri uasal Adraist in n-nuall n-anuail n-anaichnid sin na curad comrumach a comruc, a sitgal & a setfeadach na trenfher sin ac tachar.
O 'tcholaig immorro in ri sonmech senorda id_est Adraist sin, rohadandait lochranda loindearrda loindreacha lasamna & sutrolla suaichinti solusta, & tanic reime asin grianan glansolus i rroibi, & atchondairc na firu aduathmara agarba anachinti, & a gnuis letarthach landerg co mbraenaib fola fordeirgi forro.
Is andsin adrubairt Adraist riu gen drochciall do denam, & dofhiarfaig:
‘Ca dasacht ar atathai, a occu ailli echtarda?
ga difhoillsigud dermair dobeir oraib comruc & comlond do denam 'sinn aidchi? on?’ arse.
‘In ar girra in lae lib dober oraib troit & tachar do denam adrasta?
Et indisid dun can as tangauar, no cuich sib fein, & ca iret tegthi, & ca fath bar ndebtha; & rofheadar-sa,’ ar se, ‘is daine suarca sochenel sib.’
Is andsin rofhregradar i n-oenfhecht & in n-oenaball do:
‘A dei da n-adramaid,’ ar siad, ‘cadai-siu duind?’
Et ar sin rolobair Tid:
‘Tanac-sa, immorro,’ ar se, ‘a crichaib na Calidone, & tuc an agaid mi conigi seo, & rob ail lim ait & inat ar teichead na doinindi do fhagbail sund, & ni fhetar cia an duine seo,’ ar se, ‘nar-leic dam in n-inad inar-triallas anad, uair is e fen tanic ar tus and, & rofhindfa tussu,’ ar se, ‘in ua sonairt sochenelach misi trem gnimradaib goili & gaiscid; & dano,’ ar se Tid, ‘is e Oenius ri na Calidone m'athair.’
Et ar sin rolobair Polinices mac Edip:
‘Is lor lim fen mo shochenelaigi,’ ar se, ‘& met mo menman.’
Et is ed uadera dosom gen ainm a athar d'indsin na d'aisnes ar met a chuil & a chorbaid, uair ua nar leis-seom a indisin in chuil hi sin.
Is andsin rolobair in ri cendais cianaesta Adraist:
‘Leigid as uar feirg & uar fuasait, & tait limsa dom thig,’ ar se, ‘co comsnaidmmer uar comand & bar comluge & uar caridrad, & is doig comma fearrdi beias uar comand deued do denam daib, uair is iad seo da fher dec rop ferr comaltus & comand isin bith id_est Achilles & Patrocolus & Orestis & Pilades & Nisus & Eorialus & Castur & Pullux & Tesisius & Pirathous & Polinices & Tid.’
Tangadar-som aroen re hAdraist andsin arna n-etarscarad da comruc & da comlond d'indsaigid in tigi rigda roaird; & robai Adraist ac fegad na fer sin ar sin, & adchondairc craicend leomain barrgloin buidimongaich mirmoir mirathmair mallachtaich im Polinices.
Tid immorro mac Oenius is amlaid robai-side, & chroicend tuirc adbail allaid immi, & a fhiacla cruaidi croma i lleanmain in croicind sin.
Et o 'tchondairc Adraist sin, rothuigestair in fhirinde fhaistine doroigne Apaill do, comad muc adbul allaid, & comad leoman fond letarthach lanadbul uad cleamnada do; & ruc Adraist a altugud buidi dona deib, comad iat na curaid sin uad cleamnada do, arbithin na croiceand rouatar umpu.
Is andsin rogabastair-sum a llama deasa na deisi sin, & ruc leis iat isin teach fa diamra & ua derride isin rigdun.
Et is amlaid rouai in tech sin, & dered idbarta dorondad leis-seom and, & adbert-som re muntir:
‘Atdaiter lib tendti lasamna lanmora & athnuithter lib fleda firmesca fina.’
Is andsin roerig seastan & seiselb re himad & re himluad muntiri in rig re freastal & re fritholam na fleidi sin, & roergeadar dream dib re dergud imdad do pellaib cimsacha corcarglana & d'imscingib ailli orda & do chearchaillib caema clumderaithib; & dream aile re freastal & re fursunnud na sudrull solusta co slabradaib ailli ordaib imfulaing eistib; & dream aile dib ac luad & luchtaireacht a feola na fleidi sin; & dream aile dib ac saethar & ac suidigud na mbairgen comshuaiti cruithnechta ar miasaib coimdenmacha cruindi.
Ua hainius & ua haibnius mor re hAdraist bruth & borrfad, teasuach & tindenus a muintiri ac frithaileam in tigi taebalaind sin.
Is andsin rosuidestar in ri diumsach delradach sin ina rigshuidi rodenmach do chnamaib ailli eilfinti.
Roshuidsetar immorro isin leith aile in tigIsin id_est Polinices & Tid ar n-indmad & ar n-asaic doib.
Rouatar in dias sin ac sillead & ac sirsillead uar a chele.
Is andsin adubairt Adraist, in ri sona seanorda sin, buimmi & banchometaid a ingen do thabairt chuci id_est Acheist; & adrubairt Adraist ria Achaist dul ar ceand na n-ingen sin, & tangadar na hingina caema com-cosmailIsin isin tech, & ua deirgither losa liac gnuisi & aichthi na n-ingen sin, & ba baine linscoit lenead arna langlanad in fecht araill ri met na naire rogob iat ac sillead & ac faicsin na fear coem coimthech.
Et is andsin tangatar d'indsaigi a n-athar, & roshuidsetar ina fhiadnaise.
O ratairned & o rotairmiscead a ngeri & a n-accorus, & rochuiread a miasa comchruindi cumtha uaithib, doratastar in taisech cuanda comoil in crandoic coimfhecair cumdachda d'or & d'argad co n-ilbrechtugud delb & torathar in talman inti i llamuib in rig uasail Adraist mic Iasis mic Danaus mic Foreneus.
As andsin adubairt Adraist:
‘A occu,’ ar se, ‘in feadauar-si ca fath 'ma ndenmait-ni na hidbarta-sa gacha bliadna?’
‘Nad fheatamar-ni,’ ar siad.
‘Is ed ua bes ac Grecaib,’ arse, ‘inn uair doberthea ár no imned forro, idbarta do denam 'na aigid; & tabraidsi uar n-airi ris, & indesait-sea daib fatha na n-idbarta-sa id_est nathair suaichnid sechtfhillti granda gnuisgarb gaisidech eitech luaimneach lanneimnech darsa comainm Fitoin robai ac indriud insi delbda Deil.’
Et o'tchualaig Apaill innihi sin, tanic do chathugud risin nathraig, ar ua leis-sium fein int inad coem coiserctha sin, & rothoitestar in nathair sin re hApaill amlaid sin o chreachtaib dearmara diarmide con-tacmaiged & con-timchilled cet laa air in nathair sin ar maigshlebib Sirra.
Et asa haithle sin tanic Apaill remi co tigib saidbri suaichinti soneamla co hairdrig na n-Grec id_est co Crothtopus, & is amlaid robai in ri sin, & soniucar ingine glegloine genmnaide aicci, & tuc in ingen sin grad ndermar do Apaill, & is tairside dochuaid Apaill ua cleith ar bru shrotha niamgloin Neim, & robai inn ingean sin torrach co cend noi mis, airet bis gach bean, & rothuisim-si mac maisech minalaind murneach i clithirdiamraib na coilled cruimne craebaigi.
Et tucastar-si da altrom é d'aroile buachaill isin tshleib ua comneasa di, uair ba hecail le a hathair da thabairt a aithbir Et rohoiled in mac sin i llepthaib feoir & fidnemid & ua dosaib diamraib digaindi darach.
Et is ed ua hadbur cotalta don naidin sin id_est fetana ceolbindi cocuasta do senm do.
Fechtus robai-sium amlaid sin ina chodlud d'eis a oiti, douanic cuanart craesoslaicthi confadach chuici, & aduadar é.
O'tchualaig mathair in mic sin id_est ingen Crotopuis, rolinastar do gul & do golgaire na hinlesa rigda rofhairsinga, & roindis da hathair sin, & ni thanic cridi inn athar uirri, & romarbad aicci hi.
tra acht ua holc re hApaill a bhean do marbad, & rofhaideastar-sum torathar dermar demnech dasachtach d'indred in tire & in talman in ndigail a mna. Et is amlaid bai in torathar sin id_est delb mna o cichaib suas fair sin, co nathrachaib duaibsecha dubglasa ac deligud a dilleachta ima ceand.
Et as e ni donid, teacht isna tigib & macaim & mindaine do breith a hochtaib a maithrech & a muimed, & a n-ithi.
Is andsin, immorro, robai gilla oc aetidach beoda mear mormenmnach do Grecaib id_est Corebus, & nir-fhulaing doside int imnead & int edualang rofhuirim ar lucht in tire & in talman, & tanic remi cu comruc da sliged ar cind na nathrach sin.
Et is amlaid robai in nathair sin, & maccaem ceachtar a da lam & a hingni croma cruadgera ac tarring a n-indi & a n-inathair & a cride da compur a cleb.
Et dorone Corebus cipi comdaingean catha da muintir ina timchull, & rasaideastar in cloideam leatarthach lanmor robai ina laim i compur a cleb & a cridi, co rathoit cen anmain, & atclos uana Grecaib sin.
Et rogab faelti dermar dofholuchta iat, & rothinoilsead uile da hindsaigid, & is e ni donitis, bera athgera iaraind do sadud trena haigeadaib & trena hindib; & robai do met tedma in torathair co na cromdais eoin na hethaiti na coin na cuanarta ara apach.
Et ua móo fear Apaill iman ngnim sin na 'ma gach ni aile da ndernad ris.
Is andsin immorro tucastair Apaill tedmanda imda uruada arna Greccaib uili co coitchend & arin cathraig Larisa do sonrud.
Et ar sin roiarfaig ri Grec do Apaill id_est Crotopus craet rodingebad dib na neoill tened & na tedmanda sin rouatar aca milliud tre fheirg Apaill.
Et adubairt Apaill:
‘Denad in milid romarb in nathraig,’ arse, ‘idbarta damsa.’
Is andsin adrubairt Corebus re hApaill:
‘Dodensa idbarta dit,’ ar se, ‘dum deoin fen, & tabair & dena orumsa in ndigail dobera, & leic oenur na Grecu.’
Et o doronne Corebus idbarta, rosaerad é fen, & rosaerait na Greic ar cheana.
‘Donimit gacha bliadna,’ arse Adraist, ‘na hidbarta sin in n-onoir Apoill.’
Et o tharnic re hAdraist in scel sin do indisin, roiarfaigeastar do Thid & do Polinices:
‘Cuich sibsi,’ ar se, ‘a fhiru?
roindis in darna fer uaib damsa conaid e Tit mac Oeniusa, mac rig na Calidone.
Innisead in fer aile dam cuich he, uair is uair cubaid comraid.’
Et rochromastar in fear trebar Tiauandha sin a cheand id_est Polinices, & rodech secha uar Thid, & adubairt:
‘Is nar limsa, am,’ ar se, ‘a indisin mo bunadceneoil iter na hinataib caema craibthecha cosearctha, & cidead,’ ar se, ‘is do shil croda Caithim, mic Agenoir dam; & is e m'fherand dileas dearrscaigtheach cathach confadach in Teib, & is i mo mathair id_est Iochasta.’
Et is ed uadera dosom gan ainm a athar do rada ara met a nairi leis-seom in chuil sin.
Is andsin immorro adubairt Adraist:
‘Craed 'ma celfidea-su oraindi sin?’ arse, ‘uair ni fuil ua ceatharairdib na cruindi nech nach cualaig col & crodacht in chiniuda thnuthaich Tiauanda.
Et dano ni fuil acaind crich na ciniud cen chol, & dena-su fen maith,’ ar se, ‘& na hindtamlaig na huilc in chinid da’ Et a haithli in chomraid sin re Polinices, adubairt Adraist:
‘Batar na tenti, uair dered don aidchi & urthosach dun lo, & dentar acaind admolta da Apaill co honorach,’ ar se.
Is Isin oes & fuair & aimsear doroindi Ioib, mac sona saidbir Satuirn, conni & comairli risna haireachtaib dimoraib diadaib, ca digail daberad arna Tiauandaib & arna Grecaib isna olcaib doronsad.
Et ua holc am re hIunaind in comairlIsin digail do thobairt arna Grecaib, & robai 'ga thairmeasc.
Is i comairli dorigni andsin Ioib, a mac murnech morgradach Mercuir id_est techtaire na ndei ifreandaide, do chur a n-ifren do thocbail & da thoduscad Laius, athar Eidip, co ndernad & co n-adandad irgail & anindi, cothnud & comchosnum iter a uib id_est Ethiocles & Polinices.
Et o rocinded in comairlIsin re hIoib, mac Satuirn, & risna deib ar cheana, roerig Mercuir, mac Maia, ingine Athlaint, & rogob a oencheandaich luim luaimnig lanalaind imi re himluad & re hetegail os talmain do.
Et rogabastar a chathbarr orecair ilbrechtnaigthi ima cheand, & rogabastair a fleisc ceandchaim cumachtaich ina laim id_est cadruca ainm na fleisci sin.
Et is amlaid robai in fhlesc hisin, rohodiuscfed in dara cend di mairb in domain, & romairbfead firu in domain in cend aile.
Et tanic roime Mercuir ar sin co haireachtaib ichtair ifrin, ait i rraibe Laius i n-inud utmall anoibind ar bru srotha Stig, & roerig Laius la Mercuir ar fuirmed na flesci fair, & tangatar reompo tresna foiscthib fuarda firgranda firdomni ifirnd, & tresna nellaib duba dorchaidi dermara difhulaing, & tre chiachaib bodra brena buaidirthi batar and, cein noco torachtadar co dorus n-imnidach n-uruadach n-ifrind id_est co Tenair, & o roairig in cu acgarb aduathmar craesoslaicthi confadach treitelltachrach trencendach Ceirbeir, cu Oirc, na firu sin chuici, rofhosclastair glomair na chraes crithnaichech coccuasta batar aicci da sreangad & da slugadchacnom na fear sin, uair is e sin ua deoirseoir deamnach dichoindirclech ifrin.
Et rothocaib Mercuir in laim, & rufuirmeastar beim do chind imnedach na flesci robai ina laim arin coin sin, cor-ua suan sircotalta do.
Et tangatar reompu ar sin id_est Mercuir & Laius, dar dorus ifrin amach.
Et tanic immorro Mercuir remi isna sligthib suaichinti solusta ar fat inn aeoir uraird ainbheanaig fhuasnadaig co haitib reidi roailli ragaethacha Ioib.
Laius immorro tanic seic & remi dar sligthib soreidi soimtheachta slebe Cirra, & dar in cathraig fiadnaig fosadgloin dar Foca, ait ar-marbad & armudaiged eseam fen, & doriacht co Teib.
Ua hecal & ua huruath les-seom tocht isin cathraig ara crodacht & ara colaigi.
Et is amlaid rouatar curaid na cathrach inn uair sin, & siat measca mertnecha a haithli idbarta do denam doib do Baith, do dei inn fhina.
Is andsin rogabastar in seonor eclach imnach imnedach id_est Laius, rogabastar delb & denam araile fatha & fisid do Tiauandaib fair fen id_est Tresias a ainm-side.
Et is immi rogab Laius in ndeilb sin fhair, commad moidi rocreitea do, ar ni chreitir-sium físi na hamra na haislingi and, mina bedis persanda uaisli aca imluad.
Et tuargaib Laius ar sin in flesc filead bai 'na laim, & tuc ara ucht Ethiocles mar a rabi 'na collad, & adrubairt ris:
‘Ua cora dit am,’ ar se, ‘duad & domenma do denam na ainius & aibnius, & ua cora dait snim & siregim do denam ina suan & sirchodlud, uair ita do brathair ac tinol & ac tochostol it agaid.
Et dano ita brig & borrfad, uaill & diumus arbithin caradraid & cleamnais in rig uasail Adraist d'fhaguail do.
Et rochindestar commund & caradrad risin fer calma Calidone, re Tid, mac Oenius, do chur id cend-su dat thachur & dat indarba-su as do rigflaithius.
Et rochureastar Ioib, cend na ndei, misi da indisin daitsiu sin, & bid in Teib acut fein, & na leic foirb na fearandus do inti.’
Et asa haithlIsin tanic laa cona lansoillsi, & roleic Laius e ina richt fen ar lebaid & ar lanndergad a ua id_est Ethiocles.
Rafhoillsig & roindis na cneda & na crechta tucastar Eidip air.
Et rolecestar sruth lindti fala foruidri fiadnaige asna crechtaib sin ara ucht & ara agaid do Eithiocles.
Et is andsin roerig Ethiocles co haduathmar aindsclech imeclach asa ait & asa imdaid, & bai ac iarraid a brathar do throit & da thachar ris, amal thiger nemnig naimdigi arna duscad asa suan & asa sirchodlud do murn & do medar lochta na sealga aca sreathad 'na timchell.
tra acht ua hirdered don n-aeichi & ua tosach don lo acna hidbartaib sin aidbli Adraist. Et is andsin tanic Adraist & Polinices & Tid da n-imdadaib & da lepthaib, & rothoit a suan & a sirchotlad ortho a haithli anbthine na hoidchi sin.
Et nir chadail immorro int airdri uasal Adraist, acht rouadar imraiti imda ilerda ar menmain inn fhir sin.
Arna marach tangadar isin rigdai rogloin sin, & tuc cach dib lam a llaim a chele.
Donaisc a chomaind & a caradraid ara chele, & rucastar Adraist leis a tech ar leith iat id_est Tid & Polinices, in nd-inad ndiamuir nderrit, ait a ndenad-son cocur & comairle.
Et is ed seo adubairt riu:
‘A occu ailli érérgna,’ ar se, ‘roimluaidseadar na dei sib dam indsaigi-sea, & fuaribar olc & imnead ac tuidecht.
Atchualabar-si, & adchualadar Greic archena, da ingin choema chruthacha do beith accumsa id_est Argía & Deifílen, & is am toirrsech-sea re tinchur tochmairc na n-ingen sin, uair ni fuil duine sotal sochenelach na fer dearrscaigthech deigfhearaind o nach tangas da n-iarraid na n-ingen sin orumsa, uair tancas iarum a Fair & a hÉobail & a hAchís & a Sparta & a Pissa & a hElis do thochmarc na n-ingen sin.
Ra-eimthius-sa sin Cindnim,’ ar se, ‘a comshnaidm na desIsin daibsi tre chomairli na ndhei, uair is dingbala lim,’ ar se, ‘uar nduchus & uar ndeccenel do chleamnaib accum.’
Et o 'tchualaig Tid & Polinices sin, robai cach dib sel ac sithshilled uar a chele cia dib doberad fairech no frecra no fritholam fair in fher sin ar tus.
tra acht rolabair in fear urlam anacarach id_est Tid dana derscaigthech & adubairt:
‘Is mor, am,’ ar se, ‘ind umla & inn inisli, in cheandsa & in comairli daitsiu aicned mar sin acut umaindi. Uair ni thanic do rigaib tenda togaide in talman ri uad co mor firindi flaithiusa rit-so, a Adraist uasail.
tra acht is urlum ailgiussach sindi im gach ni uas ail letsu, a Adraist,’ ar Tid. Et ar sin ralabair Polinices briathra terca tarbacha, & is ed so roraid:
‘Cuich roopabad cleamnus & caradrad fhir mar thusu?
ge-tamait-ne ar echtra & ar indarba, ni thindeanus & ni toirsi lindIsin acht mad suba & somenma, uair dogabmaid th' ailgine-siu & t'onoir, & is adbal a airfitiud lind beith ac comchaitheam do flaithusa saidbir sochonaig maraen rit fen.’
A haithli in chomraid sin, immorro, roergetar-sum i n-oenfheacht & i n-oenfhuair asan inud sin, & tucsad a llama disli deasa a llam inn airdrig uasail Adraist, & rogell Adraist riu-son co cosenad a fearanda disli digbala duchusa doib, & i ed on rocomailled sin ni as mo nar-gell.
tra acht rohindised sin do lucht na cathrach cuanda comdaíngni id_est Larisa, & adclos clu na cleamnad sin cuanna coimithech sin do beith acin rig, & irnaidm na n-ingen erergna ilchrothaigi. Argia án don fhir ar tus id_est do Polinices, mac Eidip.
Et ua hingnadh delb na hingine, & ua hi ceitgen cloindi rigda Adráist hi.
Et rohindised inn óg digaind dathgel deigdenmach id_est Deifíle do cheangal re cheli comadais di id_est Tid, mac Oenius.
Et adclos ua na crichaib ciana comaidchi in scel sin, & adclos dano co slebtib leathnaib Liac, & cosna fiddromandaib fairsingi primda Partecda, & ua oirechtaib aiblib Isilecdaib, & o Thragia atuaid co Easalia uadeas, & o sruth adbul thondsolus Nem anair co rind mara Adraist siar, & cosna bruigib ailli urarda Eparda, & co treuaib togaidi Tiauanda co romesc & co ramedair in rig n-ocol n-anuarasta id_est Etiocles, in scel sin do cloistecht.
tra acht o thanic la cona lanshoillsi, rohordaiged & ro hurlumaiged bandsi firfina. Rochomlinad & rochumdaigit na hinleasa rigda rofhairsingi d'airechtaib suarca subacha gasraidi Grec.
Ua medugud menman, & ua hindtocuail aiceanta risin rigraid n-arnaid n-aiccendta n-allata id_est fuireochros fegtha & fairgseana arna delbaib rigda rinnta a n-athar & a seanathar badar ar sleasaib suaichinti in tigi cuanna cumdaigthi sin.
Et ua hiat so araill dona rigaib isa delba rorindad and id_est Inachus uasal, cosa mberthea croeba coibniusa na n-Grec uili, & Iasius seanorda sruitheta, & Foroneus sithamail sochreitmeach, & Abas cosnumaid cathbuadach, & Acresius laindech lanmenmnach, & Corebus curata coscurach, & Danaus felltach firmeblach, & dano batar delba dathchaine deigdeinmacha imda aile isin tig sin.
tra acht ua fograch fraigthi na firmaminti re muirn & re mormesci na milead ac ol isin tig sin. Et ua hadual re indisin comrada ciuine cosnomacha na n-ingen n-Grecda ngruadsolus ac ol & aibnius isin tig sin.
Et robid gach bean builid bratchorcra ac bibsugud & bansigud re hingenaib ailli Adraist andsin, comad lugaiti ecla & uruaman na fer cuanda coimithech sin orro.
Et is andsin tangadar reompo na hingena nuaglana narecha glegela gruadcorcra id_est Argía & Déifilen.
Et cosnigtis frasa dermara der dar aichtib na n-ingen sin ri met na naire inn uair sin.
Ua huruath mar, & ua hemeltius, & ua himsnim, & ua huirecla leosom caill a nn-oigi & a n-ingenais dona feraib sin.
Oir ni rabadar ar tuind talman in tan sin da ingin uad indrucu andat sin.
Air is amlaid batar-sum, cendchaema cosmaile sulglasa saineamla gruadchorcra gribglana belchorcra banamla detgela dianim lamgela laichthecha co sliastaib semidib, co colpthaib cumaidib, co traigthib tanaidib, co salaib sarchruindi.
tra acht gid fata robeth fer fiamach firglic ac mideamain na n-ingen sin, ni fhitir ca ragu doberad dib ara caime & ara cosmaili. Is andsin, immorro, ua himchumang maigi & tigi & coillti ac gasradaib gusmara Grec ac idbairt & ac onorugud baindsi na n-ingen sin Adraist.
Et o rauatar-sum amlaid sin, atchualatar buaidread & breasmaidm isna feadaib & isna fidnemedaib umpu, & ua comartha duba & dobroin dona bandsib accu-sum sin artoin.
Asa haili sin, immorro, tangadar mna in tire & in talman i tempull merglan Menerua, uair is ed ua bes aco-sum in tan sin, na hingena oga ra-foetitis re feraib, rotheasctais ni da faltib isin tempull sin Menerba i comartha genmnaideachta.
Et o thangadar-som isin tempoll sin, rothoitestar fadbairm & etig Eoraip, rig na hArcaide, adrochair ri hAdraist fecht riam remi sin, & rothoitsetar airm & ilfhaebair archena batar isin tempull sin, & rochrithnaigseadar riu stocfhograigthi dermar dofholachta as gach aird da n-indsaigid.
Ua derbairdeada demnacha sin, & ua figrad firuilc, & roimpatar-sum ammach dochum in rig o 'tchualatar-sum na hidna uruada sin, & nir-indisetar don rig sin acht rouadar fen ac crithugud comraid eturru fen, & robai airrdi urbada aili andsin, uair is amlaid robai ingen Argía id_est banchele Polinices, mic Eidip, & cumtach alaind orda ima bragait id_est muntorc alaind ingantach Hermione.
Ua feochair firchruthach in frithi sin, ua haindsech & ua hurbadach inn aiscid sin do cech oen ac a mbid.
Uair is e Ulchan uruadach, gaba imneadach ifrin, roairic in gnim sin, & is di dorigni Ulcan in cumdach n-orda sin id_est d'Ermione, d'ingin Mairt, mic Ioib, da dei in chatha, & Uenerech bandei na toili, & is ime tuc-sum sin disi dar ulcaib ria.
Uair ua hi caemchele Ulcan Uenir uanchumachtach, & is tar cend Ulchain doroigne Mairt inn ingin Ermione re Uenir.
Conid immIsin darigni Ulcan in set sirbhuan sonashercach sin re silliud sechtair fair co nemib nathrach, co lingur loiscend, co salchar slama tened & saignen, co mongaib dubglasa duaibsecha dracon, co leccaib lasamna loiscthecha ar medon and.
Comma ruited re duba, & coma fiuchtugud fergi, & coma grendugud galair do gach oen aca mbid.
Et is i cetna nech ara rimir a hairmerta uruada id_est Ermione, banchele chuanda Chathim, mic Agenoir, & is les-side rochumdaiged in Teib ar tus riam.
arrasoed in bean sin i nnathraig ngranda ngeranaig aroen re Cathim, mac Agenoir, co mbitis aroen ac sirfhetgaire isna moigib cuanda caithmecda. Et asa haithlIsin rosiacht in muntorc sin co Semile, ingin Cathim, mic Agenoir, & is di-side tuc Ioib in grad ndermar.
Et ni luaithi ranic in muntorc sin da hindsaigid na thanic Iunaind, ingean Shatuirn id_est bean Ioib, d'indsaigid na hingine i rricht a mumi, & is ed adubairt re Semila:
‘Cundig-siu,’ ar si, ‘comairle & comriachtain rit isin deilb i comraiceand re hIunaind.’
Et rochuindig Samilia amlaid sin ar Ioib comriachtain ria, & rocomroic Ioib ria-si a richt saignen telctech tendtide, amal danid re hIuaind cu raloiscead fochetoir Semile, uair nir-fhaelastar-si dellrud na diadachta doben ria.
Et is tre bithin in muntoirc sin rolot loscend in n-ingen sin, amar fhorglit na faibli guacha gendtligi sin.
Et indister co roibi in cumdach comthnudach colach sin ac Iochasta, mathair Polinices, & is trena bithin sin roui-si acca mac uaden id_est ac Eidip, co ruc da mac do id_est Ethiocles & Polinices.
Et tuc Polinices ar sin he da banchele uadein.
do Argía, da ingin alaind Adraist. Ua dereoil & ua dimicin re siair-si id_est Deifile, a cumdach brigach bandsi ac fegad in muntuirc ingantaich orda sin.
Et o'tchondairc, immorro, Erifile, caemchele Amfíarus, inni sin, tucasdáir saint sirchuindcheda air, co nar-bh fhearrdi le a bethu 'na ingnais.
Et tuc Argía disi in n-aiscid sin, & rochuir sí iar sin Ampiarus ar éigin dochum in chatha araon re hAdraist & re Polinices gusna sluagaibh & gusna secht righaibh do tabairt in chatha i nd-aghaid na Tiabanda & Eitiocleis.
Rocuired iartoin in cath, & romeabhaid for Adraist & for Poilinices, & romarbtha na secht righa and & Poilinices, & ní taineic duine 'na bethaid as acht Adraist a aonar, & robaidhedh Aimpíaras.
Almeon, dono, mac Aimpíarus romarbh seíc a mathair id_est Érifilié; ar as sí fodera a hathair do bhádhud id_est Aimpiarus.
Roghabh iar sin cuthach Almeon a haithli a mathar do marbad dó.
Rotothlaig iar sin a ben for Almeon id_est Cailliore isidhe, in muntorc; ar roba doigh lé co bfuigbed sé sláinte da scarad an mundtorc ris.
Tugad dise hé iar sin in mundtorc, & aráoi ni móite fuair-siom sláinte.
Taineic iar sin athair a mathar go hAlmeon id_est Pleigh, & romarbhustar Almeon id_est mac a ingine, a cinta a ingine, mathar Almeon fén.
Rotothlaig ben Almeon id_est Calloire, ar Ióip co rocoimhetad a da mac bega di co tisadh dhíbh di-ghailt a n-athar, Rén & Soc a n-anmanda-sidhe.
Atrachtatar sidhe iar sin, & rotinólatar-sidhe sluagh mor dermháir dochum Pleighi, & rofuagratar cath fair.
Rotinoil dono Pleigi a muinntir & a mileda.
Aráoi rocuindeigh Pleigi cairde bliadna forna macaibh gan cath do cur ris.
Adubratar-samh dobher-dáois da mbeith a chend-sam aca-samh risin mbliadain sin arná búain da méidhe.
Adubhairt Pleigi nach tibhrad a cend dóibh da dheoin.
Rocuirsit iar sin cath go fichdo feochair fergach leth for leth, & romarbad sluagh dírim diairmhe etorra.
Aráoi romeabaid in cath for Pleigi, & rosiachtatar da mac Almeon chuige, & adubhratar ris:
‘In tucais let,’ ar siat, ‘Almeon?’
‘Ní tucus,’ ar sé, ‘& da mbeith agum atrasta, doberoind.’
Robensat iar sin maca Almeon a cend do Pleigi, & tucsat ár dermháir for a muinntir macaibh mnaibh.
Tancatar iar sin da tigh ar mbreith buada & coscair.
do scel an mundtuirc.
Asa haithle sin immorro rochuir Polinicsés ag cind bliadna techtaire dochum a bhráthor id_est Eitioclés, Tit ainm an techtaire, & adubhairt an techtaire fris in flaithes do leigen da bhráthair.
Roghabh ferg mor Eitiocles, & adubhairt in ní tárraid ní leicfedh uadha, & ní dhénadh cert na dligedh uime acht muna rucadh iomarcrait tsluaigh nó catha uadha é.
‘Ocus nocha denaim-si,’ ar se, ‘fich na formad um airdchendus na Greigi uili tré charadrad an rig Adraist, & leigid dam-sa bruigi cairrgeacha cumga na Teibi tondglaisi.
Et is iris limsa gor-ip e m'athair Eidip, & bid d'aitrebachaib aigi-sim,’ ar se, ‘id_est Pelops mor, mac Tantail, & Ioif, mac sona Saduirnd.
Et is misi,’ ar se, ‘rachleachtsad ant oireacht-sa orra, & ní hail leó,’ arse, ‘fomamugud do choraid chundtabartach acht beith ag aenrig dilis derrscaigtheach, uair cach flaithus na ba feidil, ní choiglend do chíneadaib.
Et nach faiceann tusa ant aduath & in n-egla ata ar m'oiracht-sa ar mo dul-sa dib?
Et dono ni leigfid maithi na treb Tiabarda misi dib itir, na rigi do thabairt dosum.’
Acht trá ní rodamustair do Thid a chloistecht na eistecht risna baithcheileabraib briathar sin Eitiocleis.
Is andsin immorro adubairt Titt:
‘Dobera,’ ar se, ‘an flaithus uaid, & gid trí muir adbalmora iaraind robeidis ad timcheall arna cumtach do Impíon airigda & is eiside cetduine risar-cumdaigead múr na Teibi ar tus, & ni denad acht a chruit cheolbind choguasta do sheinm & ticdis croind & clocha ua cheol a chruiti-sium co teigdis aran múr.
Et cid airm & ilfaebur & teinti an talman, ní dad t'aincfed co rabais marbtha mudaigthi o 'r n-armaib-ni.
Et biaid do mindrig at egmais araen re d'chend.
Et is truaigi lem,’ ar se, ‘an digal doberthar arna ceithernaib croda Caradonda dobera let isin chath ad t'arrad bodein.
Uch tra,’ ar se Tit, ‘bud adbal na háir & na hesraidi ar slesaib sleibi Chitherón, & biaid tuili falcmar fala i sruth alaind Ismén don chomrac sin.
Et ní hingnad lem,’ arse, ‘cach olc dodentái, uair bá croda colach cach cineadh or-geineadbair, & ní fhuil do Tiabandaib uili duine nach indtamlaigend da athair a n-ulc acht mad Poilinicseis.
Et a Eithtiocles, digeltar ortsa,’ ar se, ‘th' ulc féin can rigi na bliadna-sa do thabairt duindi, uair nocha sirmid acht sin.’
Et o ralabair Tid dana derrscaigteach amlaid sin ar tairrseach an tigi rig, tainig roime co dian & co debil amal tanig an torc tren adbal allaidh dochuir Déan d'indrad & do sugad crich na Calidoine, ar ba ferg le can idbairt do denam di do lucht na Cailidoine, co n-eirged a guairi gairblíath gaisideach amal fhidbaid osa cind contaidligidis saignena solusta asa fiaclaib croma cruaidgera ima leiccnib langranda re glondbeimnig a claideam no a clomair an trath contu-indsned ara cheili hé contachlad & contógluaiseadh cairrgi troma tuinidi an talman & fualascada fada na fidbaidi a heochairimlib srotha Achileus antan contuairgidis seal-gaireada sirluatha gasraidi Greg cor-fhagaib an torc sin Talimon taraheis & co ratrascair an coraid curata Ixion co ramarb an milid morchalma Meliagér ua deoid hé.
Ocus is fan samla sin tainig an treinfer calma Cailidonda a hoireacht thnuthach na Teibi, mar bad air fein dobertha era 'ma fhlaithus.
Et ua tindisnach toirbert an fhir sin isna sligthibh soineamlaib soimtheachta, & dodiubraic uad an fleisc n-olachraind robai 'na laim a comartha sída.
Et robatar mna na Tiabanda seal ag sithsilleadh an gilla sin, & dobadar ag eadarguidi cacha huilc do Thid & dobadar ag imdradad uilc ana n-aigentaib dá ríg bodein id_est Eitiocles.
Is andsin, immorro, rabai an fer meblach micomairlech neimdeach naimdigi id_est Eitiocles, ag sgrudad ana menmain indus doberadh inndeall a oideada 'man teachtairi togaidIsin id_est 'ma Thid; & is e ni doroine-sium an fer dichoindircleach diumsach sin id_est fer da chuingeadhaib calma catha & do ogaib talchara tairisi do thoga & do thinol & a chur ar cind urtharrsna Thid ar sligid nach seithénadh, & a marbad doib.
Et ba feramail an fer cosar-cuireadh an coimlin curad sin do chomlann; & tangadar an ceithern sin ar casanaib conairi na coillteag ndriseach ndeilgneach ndiamardluith, & fuaradar inad fiamach farairi a nglind dorcha doimtheachta iter da sliab arda aimreidi co fidnemeadaib fermara fasaigh.
Et dobái carrag ard aduathmar, & is innti-sidhi rabai an torathar tedmandach dar-bo comainm Spínx.
Et is é an torathar nathaidledh & nothímchilleadh na moigi fa coimnesa di o roscaib rogranda ruamanta.
Et cach duine adchidh, & tigead isin sligid sin, roiarfaigeadh sin ceasta doib; & gach duine nach tabradh fregra furri, rosinead-si a dóidi duaibseacha dubglasa, & a hingne urnochta aithgera, & a fiacla garba goinideacha a cend cach duine, co sluigeadh & co sirchagnadh dara craes salach sleímredach, noco taínig an fer og ainíndech Eidip, & co ramarbustair an torathar sin.
Et ní lamdais cethra caithmeagda dul d'ingeltradh feoir an muigIsin na eoin na eathaidi cromad dar craebaib na caillead sin os cind in adbaid sin.
Et tangadar muinter Eitiocleis co tai taithenach co ruigi in inad sin, & rabadar ag urnaidi Tid diumsaig do dalaigh.
tra acht tangadar neoill dorcha dubglasa na haidchi tar dreith thalman uili, & o doriacht Tidd an tan sin a comfogus na caillead a rabadar na fir, adchondaircc uada don tulaig a roibi taitnem na sciath scellbolgda & ruithean na cathbarr n-orda n-ileagair tré thana na cailleadh ré soillsi in esca. Et dotocht ar Tid aga faigsin, & taínig roime da n-indsaigid arapa, & donochd a chlaidim, & dobertaig na fagada bega bega bungera rabai 'na laim, & dofhiarfaig co hainmin ainindeach:
‘Can as tangadar na firu,’ ar se, ‘& cá folach doberthaí?’
Et nir-labair duine dib ris.
Acht is andsin daerig taisech bailcbeoda bunata na buidne sin id_est Croemus curata, & dogab a fhaga suainmeach sodibraicthi ina laim laidir lancalma, & tuc urchar do Tid cor-ben isin croicend an tuirc adbail allaid bái uime da leith chlí, cor-bean crand na sleigi a n-ingnais a hiaraind eter a ucht & a imlínn.
Et ragabustar aduath feochair fergach an gilla sin, co raergestair a fholt caem curchanach amar scaith sciath sciach; & dobai co hudmall anshadail aínindeach ag ínred a aichthi & a édaig ré feochrugud na feirgi bai fair.
Et adraig ar an magh minalaind a coindi na curad, & dogab 'ga n-agallaim & is ed doraid:
‘Anaid ré himbualadh, a oga, uair nocha n-uilím-si acht mé am aenaran ar an mbernaid.’
Et ní roibi a fureach sin acoson, & tangadar da indsaigid.
Et adchondairc sin na firu sin, indus ba lia ina mar doshail.
Tainig roími suas a mullach na cairrgi a mbid Spinxs, & dobai ac brisead na cairrgi comdaingne da lamaib croma curata, noco riacht mullach na cairrgi.
Et o dariacht suas co na roibi eagla fair uilc do denam ris a leith da druim, rathachail & dotarraing carraig ndermair ndofulachta, a roibi feidm seisrigi sonairti do tharraing a tendtaib talman, & rothogaib uasa gualaind co seitreach sírchalma amail an tilcoma tendtachair rodibraic Polus mear mormenmnach aran laechraid Laipiteagda ar bansib Piratous.
Et ba machtnugud reisin mbuidin teind Tiabanda sin Titt do beith isin charraig osa cind.
Et tarlaig Tidd an tan sin an charraicc ua samalta ri sliab, cu rasrain & cu rasrailleastair an furmed fuasnadach sin, naco rathuitseadar gnuisi na gasraidIsin & a n-arm urnochta ar lár a n-aenfeacht & a n-aenuair, & ralenaid a lama na laeich sin.
Rotrascraid & rothuindsnit ochta na n-ánrad sin co bristi buaidirthi concurthi a nuaid maraen a roteilcthi rochuir an curaid sin ar an cloich chruaidh.
tra acht torchair cethrar curata comlaind a n-aenfeacht uan cloich sin, co fuaradar bás leis; & dotheithseadar an dirim croda curata sin focetoir, uair fa derrscaigtheach degcineoil an cethrar fuaradar bás and. Dabai ara reím sin fer rigda romenmnach solusta saignenta dib sin id_est Dorebus, & dathuit andsin an fer suaithnig sochinelach do sil Mairt mic Ioíp & ba talchair ré tachar an trenfer sin id_est Teron; & atorchair andsin an marcach mormenmnach urbadhach imneadach id_est Ilas & ba troigtheach é an tan sin; & adorchair and dono an fer miscneach mordalach do sil primda Penteus id_est Pedimus.
Adchondairc immorro Tid tuitim na treinfer sin, & na sluaig bristi buaidirthi archena do teitheadh; & rachasustair na da fhaga fhirgera bai 'na laim, & dodibraig íad co direach degdaingen.
Et asa haithli rolingastair leim don chruadcharraig a roibi ar an mag mor a mach a ndeagaid theithid na Tiabanda, & ragabsam cruaidsciath cuanda cathbuadach in fhir thalcair Tiabanda id_est Terón, & ragabastair an craiceand aduathmar alltaighi bai aigi fein uma chend.
Asa haithlIsin doronsad na Tiabanda dirim dluith catha comdaingin dib a n-agaid Thid arisi.
Tid, immorro, rathairring seig co talcair tindesnach a claideam mbailc mbeoda mac Bistoneagda asa truaill taebguirm aisgedaig urbaga a athar ainmnig id_est Aeniasa do Thid re trentachar a cuil a chaemduirind.
Ratimairg & dotimchill cach ré feacht na firu sin.
Roscail & roscathastair an feacht araill, & uá farrach anfulang dona feraib sin taidleach na n-arm limtha lasamain ré cheili.
Et ba toirmeasc tachair dona treinferaib a n-imad ag indsaigid aenfhir, contuairgidis & contuinsidis curpo a cheili ag rochtain an rig sin; & fa cumang croda comnaidi Thid iter armaib urnochta na laechraidi lanmarbtha uime anoir & aníar.
Robo neimneach nemthoglaidi & fá fosaid an firlaech sin ag srainead na sochaidi uada amach co cian & ua dermair difoillsiugud an fhir sin ag imirt a sceith, co mbiad ar miri & ar merbeallaig 'ma-cuairt, co na faghad fer creachtach crithnaigthech ris ba teindinus teithead caí na conair can Tid croda Cailidonda do thegmail dó ara chind urtharrsna.
Conteilged-sium & contogluaisid uad na faga fada firgera, nabidis 'na saitheadaib saiti sodibraicthi a sgiath & a cnis an curad sin; & ua lor do gresacht a gaiscid-sium id_est Tid na fiarletharthi fuilidi confertais na fir sin fair.
Et is andsin rabadar cethrar curad comramach ag cirrad chuirp an rig sin, & ba hiad so a n-anmanda:
Deilocus beogda bruthnaigthech; & fer mer do muintir Tiabanda, Plegeus tnuthach tomaithmeach, co tuaig lethain ledarthaig, tuir chatha chomlaind;
Gian gloindmer gaisgedach Tiabanda tairgsenach feramail forlaind;
Lochapanteis ledarthach lanfheachtach.
Ticead a dodranig.
tra acht roroth & rasrain Tit na treinfiru sin contoitidis re tentaib talman uad. Is andsin rabadar ina Tiabanda aga n-airim fein & fa galar leo a dteirci re tachar an tan sin.
Is andsin rofotraicsidar Croimeus Caithmegda dar-bo mathair Driopi Phoiniseagda an mbrathluirg ndruimnig ndaigremair amal ralaig roremair, & adubairt:
‘A firu,’ ar se, ‘an racha ant aenduine imlan uaind ar cur ar n-aír co hArgus?
Et a aes cumtha,’ ar se, ‘ní ferrdi duindi imad ar lam & ar n-arm & a dul-san beó & ní head sin ragells-amair-ni a Chidon & a Lampus don righ id_est do Eitiocles.’
Et an tan rabai-sium aga rada sin, tarlaig Tid trenglondach urchar do sleig seimnig sarfheachtaig do, co tarla 'na bél & 'na braigid cor-tregd a indi & a orclaigi ina cliab & gid mad béo robed balb co brath i ndegaid sin.
Et asa haithlIsin dogabastair Peripas mac Teispis a brathair ledarthi leathmarb leis iter a da laim & dobai ag toirsi & ag truagnemela co mor asa los.
Et is andsin dodibraig Tid id_est faga tromger tulfhaebrach a leith da druim do cur-drebrisastair a asnada cuara curata cor-gab urraindi tré brathair robai iter a da láim & dofhoslaig an brathair a suili ag buain an gai ind & dobai ag fegan brathar osa chind & adubairt Peripas:
‘Co tucthar aigid mar so ar do mac fein, a Tit.’
Et rothuitsead an dana brathair sin amlaid sin ré Tid, & dodun cach dib suili a ceili.
Et is e terna a sin Menetus a aenruc, & rotheith-sium noco rathuit, & rug Tit air, & rothogaib Menetus a dá laim, & dobai ag iarraid anacail ar Thid:
‘Ar na dee da n-adraid riut, leig uait misi d'indsaigi na Teibi cu raindisur do scela innti, amal domarbais-si sinne,’ ar se, ‘& do beith-siu béo.’
Nir-bo trocair, immorro, Tid do Menetus,:
‘Doberim mo breithir ris,’ ar Tid, ‘na geb-sa do dera ina do debrogoid.
Uair is tú dogeall mo chend-sa do breith leat do Eitiocles & cuir uait t'
arm,’ ar se, ‘& gab maithim n-anacail, uair bu gairid bía ad bethaid risna cathaib iartain.’
Is andsin tuc Tid athais n-imagallma & imchainti arna Tiabanda, & tainig athscis mór andsin do Tid, co nar-fhéd a sciath d'imarchur na a chlaidim do chongbail, co nusnigdis srotha fola fiadhnaighi na miled romarbastair asa trillsib troma taitnemacha, amal leoman mer Maisileagda ar gur air almad & indili co nbi scitheach ar caithim an comaid sin.
tra acht is ed fa tend ag Tid dul d'indsaig na Tebi & faidb fhuilidi forderga na fer sin do breith leis do Eitiocles & dona Tiabandaib ar chena noco ndebairt an bandea Menerba ris:
‘A mic’ ‘ríg na Calidone,’ ar si, ‘ca misgais no ca migradh fuil agut fort fen intan tegi dod tinnlacadh do Tiabandaib? Et na mill in coscar rochuiris & na mórgnima doronais, & doghebat Grécaigh uili cathugud o Tiabandaib.’
Ocus rotinntodh Menerbha aicnedh Tit andsin.
Imthusa Beniri banchumachtaigi roinnsaigh seig a lennan id_est Mairt, mac Ioib, & roeigh air, acc iarraidh furtachta do Tiabandaib.
Ocus dofurail ar Tit dul co Teibh do fagbail a oidhedha, & roraidh ris:
‘Da madh e intan tucais in gradh ndermair dam-sa, & mé ac Ulcan, & rochuadhus ad chomdail-si & rochomracais rim ri Beínir.’
Et o racomraic Mairt ré Ueínir andsin, rochruaid-cheangail an slabrad sin iad a n-urd a n-adaltrais, & o'dchondaircc Ulcan iad, rothinoil na huili dee & bandee co fhacadar co fiadnach adaltras na deisi sin.
‘Et da mad hé an lá fuarus-sa ant imdergad-sa as do los-so, a Mairt, dobertha-sa maithim damsa dona Tiabandaib; & is mo doberad Ulcan damsa cach ní do chuingebaind fair anai-siu, a Mairt, gé doronas a aimles.
Et créd mar-leigis dam,’ ar si, 'in ingen rucus duitsi dar cend Ulcain id_est Erimone da thabairt don fir Thirdha Tiabanda id_est do Chaitheam mac Aigenoir, & olc do denam ré lucht na Tebi 'na degaid?
Et is nair duitsi' ar si, 'corob treisi Ulcan re milliud na Tiabanda ina duitsi 'ca n-anacul.
Uair is é Ulcan tre ét umaitsiu tuc forru cach col da ndernatis id_est in muintorc tuc doibh' Nochar-fuilngastair trá an fer cuanda cathbuadach sin id_est Mairt, mac Ioif, briathra Ueiniri do dul co dimain.
Rachuir a arma uadh, & ratoirling asa charpud, & ragab chuigi in ingin a crislacha a sceith, & dogab co hinmain ailgen age hagallaim, & adbert:
‘Is tu duine as docha lium dona dainib & dona deib.
Is taisgi rabaithfind-si me fein isna srothaib adfuaraib ifernda na dorachad do grad-sa & t'inmaine uaim-si & grad lochta na Teibi.
Et chena,’ ar se, ‘ní fhedaim gan teachtaireacht don athair d'Ioib,’ ar se, ‘uair atá a chumachta a nim & a talmain, ar muir & ar tír, & ní fetar teacht a n-agaid chainti an chumachtaigh sin.
Uair docindastar Ioib & na dee ar chena o thosach an domain an cath-sa do chur.
Acht chena,’ arse, ‘an tan beidid na cineada ceachtarda ac cathugud ar faithchí na Teibi id_est na Greig & na Tiabanda, & dober-sa fortacht & foirithín ar na cineadaib tairisi Tiabanda, & dodensa,’ arse, ‘do comairli-si cach indus dofédab.
Uair legaid na dee dunn furtacht ar carad, acht na rab toidecht a n-agaid a toili.’
Et o adubairt-sium sin, rogreseastair a eocha disciri difoillsigtheacha.
Ba deínigtir saignen luath lasamain ré tinchur a diubraicthi a n-aimsir adfuair anbhthenaigh, amal tainig Mairt mac Ioip roime risin teachtairecht sin.
Imtusa Mairt conuigi sin.
Imtusa, immorro, Tit mic Aeniasa, rochind seig a cheim co hegandais adhuathmar tarsna bruigib cairgeacha gartglana Gregda, co facaid uad mullach na cathrach suaithinti suthaigi id_est Prochinna.
Ua salcha sesmacha trillsi an treinfhir an tan sin ré lansalchar an luaithridh a haithli an lanchomaig, & ba salcha fliucha na fiarletairthi badar a cnís an curadh sin tré allus a aistir & imtheachta, & ba ruisti ruamanta ruisc an rig sin can codlad can chumsanadh, & ba mórmenmnach an milid sin a haithli an choscair dochuir.
Uair is amlaid dobai Tit mac Aeniasa andsin amal tarb comthnuthach coscarach ar traethad & ar toirnem chuingida choimfedma, coma lochairthi lanmarb dá eis arna fudbogud.
Et o rasiacht immorro Tit na cathracha sin na Greigi, nir-an ag adandadh feirgi & urbaga & miscaisi na Tiabanda arna cineadaib cosnamachaid_est ota Sefon co hArgus, & dobaí 'ga indisi a chuir fein re teachtairecht dochum Eitiocleis d'iarraid a fhlaithis do Phoilinices & raindis an feall dotriallad air fein tré cheilg in aidchIsin ag Eitiocles & era do thabairt do umon flaithus do Poilinixes.
Et dob urusa do Thid aslach uilc do thabairt iter na poiplib sin Adraist.
Uair dobai an dea croda cathchumachtach id_est Mairt ag urail ana cetna orro.
Is andsin immorro dobaí an rí uasal Adraisd, & maithi a muinntire 'na farrad a coindi & a comairli, antan tainig Tit can fis can aireachad chucu no cor-labair fon dorus ag teacht astech:
‘A firu,’ ar se, ‘gabaid bar n-arma co hoband;, a Adraist,’ ar se, ‘cuimnig,’ ar se, ‘do sochineilchi & mormenma na fer mor or-geinis, & gab t'errad catha & comlaind & comraig umat; uair nocha n-uil comall caradraid ag na Tiabandaib risna deib na risna dainib,’ ar se, ‘& dobad usa liumsa dul re teachtaireacht d'indsaighid cach cineada egendais ainindaig aili 'sin doman na da n-indsaigid-sium.
Et a Gregu,’ ar se, ‘berid mise dochum catha na Tiabanda, co ndiglar orra t-indlead ceilgi tucsad oram isin n-aidchi.
Et ergid co hoband,’ arse, ‘dochum bar namad antan ataid co heaglach anband remaib, & antan ataid trúaig nemelach ag nuallguba a muinntire, & ag adnacal chorp a carad alla muich da cathraig, & domarbus-sa fein id_est treinfer dona Tiabandaib.
Et gid am creachtach crolindteach-sa, is ed is ail lium a n-indsaigid a cetoir doridisi.’
Is andsin doeirgeadar na Greig a n-aenfecht a n-agaid Tit do ferthain fhailti fris, & is e cetfer doriacht da indsaigid an trenfer calma Caithmeagda Polinixes, mac Eidiph, rochrom a chend, & adubairt:
‘Adchim-si do chreachta, a Thid croda, a charagain; & ni tu do creachtnaiged andsin,’ ar se, ‘acht mad misi fein; & do rulcaib rimsa doronad ritsu sin.
Et bid-si an bar tocht,’ ar se, ‘a Gregu, & leigid damsa debaid ma brathar; & is ed dligim-si, a Thid,’ ar se, ‘do creachta-su do digail ar na Tiabanda.’
Et o dorigni-sium an comairlIsin co coitchend re cach, roerig truaignemela toirrsi & tindusa a crideadaib na n-Greg uili, co na roibi d'óg na do shin andsin an aenduine nar-chind aenmenmain a aít & atharda d'fhagbail, & dul d'indsaigid na Teibe da togail re Polinices, mac Eidip.
Et dolabair an comairleach cianaesta id_est athair an oireachais id_est Adraist, & adubairt:
‘Leigid damsa & dona deib bar caingni do chrichnachadh, & denaid teindeanus um thachur risna Tiabandaib.
Uair nocha racha an flaithius a n-aiscidh o Phoilinices can a digail, & bid nua sin antan dogentar.
Acht chena,’ ar se, ‘dentar Tit, mac Aeniasa, do leiges & do lesubugud, & legar codlad & cumsanad do chorp creachtach an curad comba slan.’
O 'dconncadar ceitheirn cuanna coimideachta Thid & a baincheili baillgeal banamail, a cnes ar creachtnubad, robuaidrid & romedraid a menmanda.
Et roiadsadar uili uime 'ma cuairt co dluith & co daingean, & tairastair Tid co fosaid forbailid isin rigda, & a druim risin colamain comdáingin bai for lar an tigi, & doglanustáir an fiseacda fireolach id_est Idmon Epidurda, a creachta an curad sin d'uisqui langlan linnfhuar, & dothesc do scín aithgher faebarguirm iumad an feola atmairi as.
Rachuir luibi cumachtacha cnesaigthi a ledarthaib an laeich sin.
Et dobai immorro Tid, mac Aeniasa, ag fhaisneis & ag indisin a gloir & a chomraith fein & Eitiocles, rí na Teibi; & roindis an t-inad a tugadh in tsleag ceilgi uime, & in uair tugadh an cath, & anmand na toiseach dorochair leis, & an fer-indisin-scel doleig da deoin uada id_est Meón fileata fadamail.
Et ralai socht & snim an rig n-uasal n-Adraist & airig an tiri & an talman badar ag eisteacht risna scelaib sin; & rob adannad menman don lucht sin scela na Tiabanda, & fá togbail fergi & fhuasaidi Poilinices moir mic Eidip sin.
Et asa hailIsin rothoirind & rathain an grian dathglan difhoillsigtheach ar uaitni caema corcurglana dar eocharbordaib in aigeoin aird Iberda siar co fuinead, co raiad & co rainfhogair agaid dorcha doimtheachta crislach comluaimneach choguasta na firmaiminti um tulcaib & trebaib an talman uile, co roibi cach uili ina colladh & ina comsonad, acht mad an ri cendais cianaesta Adraist a cliamain primda Polinices ag sgrudad gaisi can chodladh in aidchi sin.
Et bai immorro Tid leadarthi ina lanchodlad.
Et asa haithlIsin tainig Mairt mac Eoiph con arm-fogrugad adbal in aidchIsin dar crichaib arda na hArcaidi, & dar bruigib níamglana Neim, & dar mullach sleibi tirmglain Tenair & co cathraig uasail Apaill do Tiramnas co ralin grada chatha cosnama crideada crithnaigtheacha curada na Greige uile tré aslach an dei Mairt mic Eoip.
Et dono roscail Fama, ingen Terra, co cluach irdairc scela an dea sin Mairt fo chricha & chendacha na Greigi Et a cind seacht laithi iar sin roerig an senoir snimach uasal, Adraist, & rabai co himsnimach 'ca imradh an cath rocomorfad no an sid rosirfea ar cach.
Et is í comairli rochind-sium a faidhi & a fisidi do thabairt da indsaigi & a iarraid daib seig tre idbartaib ar na deib cid bud choir dona Gregaib do denam.
Et is íad fá fileada an tan sin aigi-sium id_est Aimpiaraus, mac Eitiocleis no Eiclis, an sagart tuaithcill tuigsenach na todochaidi; & an senoir fireolach finnitneach Melampus, mac Amithón.
Et ni roibi a coimré fris neach as mó ara tabradh Apaill firinde fregra inain fer fer sin Melampus.
Et doronsad na faidIsin taiscelta faistine ar tus tré fuil & tre indib na ceathra comloiscthi; & ona fuaradar fis, ba failid leó uaithib sin.
Is andsin rotriallsatar taisceladh ar nellaib nuaglana in aeoir.
Is amlaid rabadar-som, & sliab ard aireda chuanda coimreidh coiseargtha a comfogus doib id_est Aphesannt.
Et is do mullach an sleibIsin rofoluaimnig Peirs mac Ioip do cathugud risin Gorgain.
Et is amlaid robai an Gorgain sin id_est torathar trechendach, & cach duine adchid he, doníth carraig chomdaingean de.
Et o chualaid Pers, mac Eoiph, sin, tainig d'indsaigid Meneirbi, & dosir furtacht furri dochum na Gorgaine.
Tug Menearba a sciath gloinidhi udein dó co faicead-som scath an torathair ag tachur ris trésan sciath sin & co faced in torathar a scath fen conar air fen docuaid ann; & atorchair an Gorgan leis-sium amlaid sin.
Is andsin tangadar na faidi & na fisidi sagart sin id_est Ampiaraus, & Melampus isin sliab n-alaind n-olachranda sin, & a snaitheadha ailli idbarta 'má, cendaib re turggabail na greine suaithinte solusta isin maidin moch-thrath.
Is andsin dolabair Ampiaraus ar tus risna deib id_est re hEoib do sundrad, & rarim a cumachta egsamail in gach inad fair d'iarraid a firindi & a innisin duind ‘tre gothaib, na n-én, a Ioib, an mberam coscur dona Tiabandaib don turus-sa.’
Et o 'dubairt Ampiaraus sin, ralaigastair isin carraig chomdaingin a roibi, & dobaí ag fegad fhaistine ina aignead andsin, & o rafegastar-sum renda & reltanda na firmaiminti & atha in aeoir, ralabair Melampus an filid asa haithlIsin:
‘Adchi-si, a Ampiarauis,’ ar se, ‘conach foillsigend én na eathaidi sosad na saime don ulad sin no so.
Uair adchi-si edaigi duba duaibsecha in aieoir ag troid & ag tachar da n-íningnib croma gcruaidgera ré ceili & comartha duba & broin sin,’ ar se.
Adubairt Ampiaraus ar sin:
‘Darignius-sa co minic, a Melampuis, faistine a n-uair dob óg me antan dochuadus a n-Argo maraen ré hIason & ré hErcail & re rigraid Greg archena co crich na Colcheta.
Et ní rochreid Iason da fisid na da fireolach id_est do Mopsus, amal dochreid damsa.
Et nocha nfuarus riam,’ ar se, ‘derbairdeada moruilc mar so a faistine da ndernus, & tabair-si t'airi, a Melampuis,’ ar se, ‘risna dirmaib diairmidi d'elaib ailli aengela adchím atuaid on sruth adfhuar oigreta id_est o Strimon seachum aneas o sruth niamglan Nil.
Et tuic let,’ ar se, ‘na Tiabanda taetencha i sidh in cathrachaib comdaingnib trésna helaib nemluaimneacha,’ ar se, ‘& ag siud buidean as chalma inaid fein da n-indsaigid id_est secht n-aquili aduathmara, & is íad sin,’ ar se, ‘secht rig na n-Greg ag indreadh & ag argain na Tiabanda.
Et ag siud,’ ar se, ‘aquil dib ag dul a n-airdi co raloisceadh & co raloitteadh hí; & is é sin,’ ar se, ‘an ri diumsach drochaigentach id_est Capeneus an sechtmad ri do rigaib Greg.
Loiscfid saignen teindtigi hé ar an cathuchad mór na Teibi.
Et dofhédar,’ ar se, ‘in aquil so rothuit ar scis eteagaili, is é an mac baeth buaidealta Partanapeus, & ant en-sa dono rothuit ar braigid a cheli Polinices mor, mac Eidip sin; & a brathair Eitiocles, rí na Tiabanda.
Et ann acil raimig imshlán id_est Adraist uasal a aenur.
Et ant én so adchí do bathadh,’ ar se, ‘id_est Ipimedón, & ant en-sa adchí ac cognam chind aroili id_est Tid mac Aeniusa sin & Menailispus.’
Is andsin domebaid a chai ar Ampiaraus, & rafiarfacht Melampus:
‘Cid ma cidii, a chumthaig, a trasta?’ ar Melampus.
‘Truag am sin, a uasail airmidnig, a Melampuis,’ ar Ampiaraus.
‘Doberim-si,’ ar se, ‘aithne ar an én úd rothuit can ait & can inad d'fagbail, conid mé fein tuitfes tresin talmain sis ar cathachad mor na Teibi.’ tra acht ragabastair critheagla mor na faidi & na fisid sin, & rob faiteach leo fegad na fisi sin, & dochuir an sagart Ampiaraus a edach uasal idbarta de, & táinic isin sliab co dubach domenmnach, connach cuiread asa airi cathuchud na Tebhi mar bad in uair sin nobedh.
Et ni deachaid a teach an rig Adraist, na do comrad re huaislib na hoirechta, acht dofhalcastair hé a nduama aineolaig anaithnid can fis do duine.
Melampus immorro dobái fein isin tsleib chedna co cend se lá & se n-aidchi can labra ré duine.
Et o nar-labradar na faidi firindi fesa risna Gregaib, rogresistar Eoip mor, mac Saduirn, cend cumachtach coitchend caich, gasraid Greg dochum na Teibi do togail, comdais fasaighthi na feranda & duine & dingnada na Gregi ré leiri & lanméd tinoil na treinfer sin, cona fagadhais a mna & mic & mindaine ag nuallguba da n-eis.
Is andsin roglanaid & radaingnigid carpaid craeslethna comora.
Ralimaid & rolondraigid slega suainmeacha sodibraicthi a meirgi & a migne leo-sium.
Raslibaid & roslemnaigid cloidmi aithghera urnochta aco-sam ré har & ré hoirleach a n-escarad.
Raníamaid & ronuaglanaid cathbarra cruinne cumdachta & luireacha drolmanacha dubglasa leó.
Rochumaid & rochoimsigid inair chaema cruadchomraig fa chneasaib na curad sin, & tucad leo fedmanda fillti for bogadaib caema cornectaib.
Ralegaid & raluathchumaid a n-iarrnaigi athcnaiti arathair, a corrana coimremra & a rastail troma treuairi, comdais airm aithgera urlama a n-agaid irgaili.
Radidnid & radaingnigid a sceith chaidi cathbuadacha do seitidaib gorma glaedecair tiuga togaidhi tarb.
Et raergedar uili a n-aenfecht co haenmenmnach na Greig co hArgas & co teach an righ uasail Adraist con craitheadh feigi na firmaimindti gair gasraidi Greg ag tinnscedal tachair re lucht na Teibi coma coma samalta in nuall sin & tulborb fogragad na cruinni comairdi ac athcumsgugad don choraid curata id_est Encheladus, da sleibtib sarmora na Sigili srotaidi.
Et is amlaid innister co rugad an corad sin fa sleibtib na Sigili id_est daine mera mileata badar an tus na haimsiri & is i comairli rochindsed, tocht do togail nime & rigi do gabail.
Et o 'dchualadar na dee sin id_est Ioip & Apaill & na dei ar chena, dochuirsedar cath risna coradaib sin & ríu seig aderthái mic an talman ara truma & ara talmaigeacht.
Ramebaid orra an cath sin, & rochenglaid & rachuibrigid risna deib iad, & dochuiread fer dib fa shliab Athna.
Et is ed innister an trath chuireas cor no culscal de, conseideann sruth casracha teinead a taeb ant sleibi, & roceanglaid andsin Enceladus bá tri sleibtib na Sigili id_est Lilbeus & Pacinnus & Pilorus, & antan concumscaigenn an coraid sin, crithfograigid cruinne na firmaiminnti uili, & ba cosmail rissin nuallgair na n-Greg ag iarraid thachair risna Tiabanda.
Et asa haithlIsin rochomerig fer brigach borrfadach soichsinach sotal sochinelach id_est Capaneus, an sechtmad rí an toicheastail sin na n-Greg, & is é an fer egennais inniriseach sin nach denad ni ar deib na ar dainib, & rolabair Capaneus:
‘Is dillsiugud & is dimigin duind,’ ar se, ‘a Aimpiarauis, an coimlin curad cumtaig, atai-si ag urnaidi fhaistine aenduine 'sin doman.
Et mad misi chena,’ ar se, ‘nocha bíu ag urnaidi ris, uair is and ata mo chumachta comlaind am chlaidim, & doden-sa faistine daib, a Gregu, muna derna Ampiaraus.’
Et o raiadsadair na Greig fan ngilla sin, raerig Ampiaraus, & adubairt:
‘Nocha n-ar glor ogal ainindeach Capaneuis, na re hegla dodenaind-si faistine daib, acht ar bar ngrád fein.
Acht ata ni chena, a thruaga, ca dasacht & ca drochciall imluaigis sib?
Et ca miscais doberthai daib fein, & dá bar cathraig, do Argus, antan teigthi d'indsaigi na Tiabanda, & créd ma tucsabair orm faistine duib?
Uair adchondarcus derbairdida digla dermairi daib, a Gregu, & rothescad snaitheada bar saegail ag na Parchip iferndaigi.’
Uair tri mna aderar do beith i n-ifern, & fairchi aderar ríu, & cuigeal gona cuigeallach aca a triur a chuma shaegail cach duine id_est bean dib ag imarchur na cuigili id_est Clotha, & bean ag snim ant snaithi id_est Lacesis id_est in tres ben ic tescad int snaithi Atropus.
