‘Et, a thruaga, a Ghregu,’ ar se, Ampiarus, ‘ca hailleas daib treba na Teibi do thuar d'apaigib bar corp arna marbad ar moigib cathrach Caithim & ge-tu-sa 'ca bar toirmesc?’ ar sé, ‘uair is cinnti co racham uili and.’
Et rabai an sagart ana thast Ampiaraus andsin, & dorad Capaneus athis aridisi ar Ampiaraus, & adubairt:
‘Bi-siu co timteitheadach isin Greig, & cach aen ara n-urailfi tú eagla tred t'faistine, & na heist-siu risna stoccaib tendgluaire Tirrannda.
Et dogein-sa fein,’ ar se, ‘faistine da gach aen tia leam dochum an cathaigthi.’
Et is uime aderar Tirrannda, risna stoccaib, uair Terenus, ri na Tusceta, brathair Lidh, cetduine risir-sínnedh sdocc riam ar tuss.
Et rofograigsed Greig bresmaidm ndermair tresin seiseilbi sirgloir dorindsead ag comaentaig ré Capaneus, amal fogrugud doní sruth buinni dian dileann a n-aimsir adfuair earrchaidi dar fegaib & dar fanglentaib an talman.
Et o tainic in adaig, rascailsead na curaid sin a comrath; & gid sochaidi dochodail, no cha n-í Argia, ingen Adraist, ben Poilinixeis, rochodail ré himsnim & ré hudmailli menman a los a fir, uair ní fagad sí caemthachas na comrath in fhir sin ré snim & ré sirimrad cíndus dodenad ré brathair ima chuid don rigi & don fhlaithus.
Et tainig, derid aidchi, roimpi co teach rigda roard a hathar & a mac fein & a meic bicc ina laim id_est Tesanndrus, mac Poilinicseis; & adubairt si ré hathair:
‘Rafider tusa, a athair ínmain, a Adraist,’ ar si, ‘an toisc 'ma tanag-sa an tech-sa, Adraist, cen co hindusar dit.
Et ni hé Poilinixes adrubairt rim teacht, acht mad duba & domeanma, eccumsunad & etfualang dom-buaidread o thucais-siu mi do Polinices.
Et, a ri, adeir ritsu, tabair furtacht ar in fear sin, commor catha les do chosnum na Tebi, & a athair inmain,’ arsi, ‘abair in tibrea, uair rocharas-sa in fer sin, & is coraide ditsiu cungnam les; & ge-tu-sa aniugh ac tendad in tachair, is doig leam biait aris acca thairmesc re hecla uilc daibsi.’
Et asa haithlIsin ropoc Adraist a ingin,:
‘A ingen,’ arse, ‘ni aiscim ort in geran dani & in n-aicine fuacraid.
Cuir dit t'ecla & dena do cheli do chomdidnad, uair atamaid-ne ac fur in chatha sin & is cinti a chur.’
Et o thainic in maten re crichaib in chomraid sin, roerig Adraist.
Tri bliadna tra co haes na haimsire ailli errchaide sin robas ac fur na fingailIsin iter na Tiauandaib & na Grecaib.
Et ergid in badb catha cosnamach & rochraithistair aithindeda adanta uruada uas cathrachaibh na n-Grec & na Tiauanda.
Rogair & rograin uas na longportaib lethna lanfata cora-gabsadar buidne bruthmara & trenfhir talchara a n-armu aithgera ri tenta tindeanais na baidbi beldergi sin.
Et o tanic amser in chatha do chommorad, doronaid idbarta aidbli mora leo, co samlaitis na sacairt maith tresna hidbartaib doib iartain.
Et is andsin roergedar maccaim beca buaigelta, & ingena nuaglana nairecha, & seanoraig crina chrotbolla do celebrad dona fearaib sin, co snigtis frasa diana der dar cathbarraib cocuasta, dar armaib & etaigib na carad cumachta sin ac pocad a cheli re scarad.
Tochastol na n-Grec andso uadeasta.
Is iat so na ciniuda dochuadar dochum in chatha sin, cona rigaib uaisli leo id_est in ri toirrsech taetenach anband anindech snimach sirchelgach Adraist.
Et ni ba setrech re himurchur n-airm in fer sin, acht mad a cloideam nama, & a airm aca muntir 'na degaid.
Rocheangail & rochumdaig a ara a eocho diana deigretha i ndorus na cathrach Larisa, & robai a ech socair soermach id_est Areon, ac doibli & ac daeibili, & ua comartha uilc iartain acco-son sin.
Is andsin roergedar slúaig & sochaidi & sochraideada in rig uasail, Adraist, asa cathrachaib dilsi dathglana uadein.
Et it e andso a n-anmand-side id_est Larisa, & Procinna, & Mída, & Pilos, & Neris ar bru srotha Caradron, & Cleon, & Tilé i crichaib na Lecdomoin; & tangadar na ciniuda comnesta a slebtib cairrgecha Drepain & asan chathraig as Sition iter in sruth lanmor Lanngia & in sruth n-adbul Eleos; & tangas asin chathraig uraird oaibind a hEfir, & a Conrae & asna crichaib uile iter topur primalaind Pegais iar n-iarthur, & in sliab n-aibind Ithmos iar n-airthiur, & in muir n-ard n-Adriadecda iar tuaiscert, & in muir n-ainbtheanach n-Egeta iar ndescert, i sochraide Adraist.
Et ua tri mile lin int sloig sin ac subochus 'ma rig co n-armaib ecsamlaib, uair ni ua cosmail na ciniuda, uair rouadar cesfhagada lethna langera ac forind dona fearaib sin, & lethgai londrecha lasamna ac airiucht aile dib, & taibli taidlecha tulamuis, & boga blaithi beandchruaidi ac drem aile.
Et ua samalta in ri uasal Adraist iter na haireachtaib sin id_est tarb n-ard n-aduathmar co n-imad crecht arna cnesugud ina curp conna fedad ocdaim na n-almad fegad fair ri haduath a adarc tulmael tamnaigthi ri tenta gacha tachair.
Is andsin, immorro, rothocaib in trenfher tend talchar Tiauanda Polinices, mac Eidip, a mergeda ardda aduathmara; & as iad ua cuingid chatha 'man fer sin, na Tiauanda tarrisi tangadar asa tir da n-indsaigid, & cethirna na cathrach ratinnscarnastar Adraist do maroen re a ingin; & at iat so na cathracha id_est Eogeon, & Arenen, & cathair Teis mic Eig mic Nemtuir id_est Toeiste.
Et ua hinund arm & etgud do Polinices inn uair sin & inn adaig tanic riam remi co tech Adraist id_est croicend leomain talchair Teomesecda ime, & slega rindgera roremra ina laim, gu ngonad-som remi & da eis dib sin, & cloideb fate firfaebrach uar a chliu, co ndelb in torathair romarbad la hEidip and id_est Spinx.
tra acht ua fata re Polinices techt in turas sin intan doberead da uid Argía, ingen Adraist, a banchele uadein d'fhácuail da eis & ua tindeanus leis tocht d'indsaigi a flaithiusa a mathar & a muntire in feacht aile; & ua ceithri mili lin na sochraidIsin 'man trenfher sin. Is andsin immorro rochoraig in fer sotal saignenta failid arnaid esadail id_est Tid, a muntir uar aird, & roerig menma in miled sin o 'tchualaich na stuccu 'ca senm, amal eirges nathair oilmir anindech re tinchur na greni i llo samraid solusta, co nthobruchtad tondgar a nemi uar feraib futhremra, cuna lamad duine na ceithri buain ris.
Et ua hiat sluaig inn fhir sin, ciniuda calma Philine, & milid primda Pleuron, & is intIsin robid a brathair-sium id_est Meliager, & cetherna calma Calidone, & aireachta Elenós, & curaid na cathrach Colchis, & aitrebaid int srotha Achilous, cathracha na hEdailli i crichaib na Calidoine sin.
Et is amlaid badar lucht na cathrach sin, & cathcliatha aidbli umaide acco do diden a corp re cathugud, & laigneda lethna ina lamaib re letrad, & cathbairr caema cumdachta ima cendaib; & roiadsad as gach aird inn ocuadatu tend togaide sin 'man milid maisech mormenmnach id_est Tid, mac Oenius.
Ua subach i cathaib in cuingid sin, & ua tendi tomhaitheam Tid arna Tiauandaib na bacur Polinices.
As a haithlIsin roerig in rig ard airegda id_est Ipomedon gasta gruadsolus; & timsaigid a shluaig leis o bruichib srotha lan-alaind Licc, & o imblib srotha Inaich, & o crichaib arda srotha Asterion.
Et tancadar and dano na dirmada doilgi Driopecda & na haireachta aidbli Epecda, & na hilbuidni airrdrici Epedurdá; & tangadar leis fos milid maithi menmnacha na cathrach Dimé, & buidne dluithi degdaingne na cathrach Pilos, & ua hestIsin do Neastoir, mac Taicsis, mic Neleus, do chind gaisi Grec; & ua hoc he in tan sin, & ger-b oc, roop tocht do thogail na Tebe in tan sin.
Acht roimluaid Ipomedón lucht na cathrach leis archeana tre laechdacht a llaime dochum in chatha.
Et is amlaid bai Ipomedon, & cathbarr alaind umaidi co tri ciraib comarda cathbairr, coma samalta re snechta ara sargili ima cend, & ua cengalta corp in curad sin uile o armaib.
Uair is amlaid robai-sium, & crundsciath luchair lasamain fair, co ndelbaib cloindi Dánaus & Beil.
Et is amlaid rouadar sec inda da nderbrathair & fich fergi eturru.
Coica ingen ac Danaus & a comlin sin do maccaib ac Béil; & adrubairt Dánaus re a ingenaib:
‘Dober-sa sib,’ ar se, ‘do maccaib Beil, & marbait-si iat isan oichdi.’
Et is amlaid sin doronad, acht oenbean nama & nir-marb-sein a fer id_est Linus.
Et rauadar delba na dremi sin, & delba ileccair imda aile isin sciath sin arna rindad ind, & ua samalta concrithnigitis na coillti & contairnitis na slebti sainemna soimtheachta ua cosaib in curad sin ac crathad a sceith iter na haireachtaib re tinchur tachuir.
Et cuich in dune da ticfad na ciniuda cosnumacha sin & na cuingid chatha & imad airm na milead mormenmnach sin d'airium?
Acht chena tangadar tri chet do gillib occa athluma a cathraig Ercoil id_est Tirindta; tainic dano and maraen ris Agelleus, mac Ercail, asin chathraig cetna maraen re Hipomedón.
Et ge-r uaiti aittrebaidi na cathrach sin, ua hairdi-side, & ua hairside in n-aimsir irgaile, & ni rohimirchuirit fagada seta suainmecha re dibrucud acin dreim sin, na cloidme cruaide re cathletrad, acht mad fadba leoman letarthach, & tamain troma do giuis arna garbsnoidi, & saigdi saineamla sarechta a bogadaib buidi beandchruaidi.
Concandais admolad Ercoil reompu isin sligid i sochraide Ipomedon.
Et tangadar cethirna comlaind a coilltib Neim, & munter Molorcus asna coilltib craebacha Cloenda i comitecht in marcaig mormenmnaig sin Ipomedon.
Sochraide Ipomedon sin.
Asa haithlIsin roerig in fer taend tarcaisnech id_est Capaneus, & conberad a ormna osna cathaib ceachtarda, & rogabastar a sciath mor mileta arna comcheangul do seichedaib ceithri tarb arna ndeigrindad do ígmaigib nathrach & loiscend & torathar in talman archeana, co ndidned corp in churad sin o bond co bathais; & rogob a luirig snithi-snadmandaig ndualaich ndrolmanaig uachthir diamraib a etaich, & rogab a cathbarr rinta ruithnigthech imma ceand in caithmiled & rogob a sleig crannreamair comthruim ina laim, na fedad dune aile for talmain do tocbail acht mad in ri calma curata id_est Capaneus.
Et tangadar i sochraide in rig sin athtrebaide na cathrach Ámpigánía, & milid menmnacha Mesené, & airsidi irgaili na cathrach Ethoné, & trenfhir thaircseanacha na cathrach Tirón, & aireachta Ephi, & sluaig suaichinti Selos, & fir primda Piléon, & dronga degsluaig a Dorión.
Toicheastol Capeneuis mic Tarsis conigi sin.
Is andsin, immorro, roerig in rigshacart uasal id_est Ampiaraus do thogail na Tebi; & ge dachúaid-sium andsin, robai a fhis aicci gach olc darobi do fen de & do chach archena; & ni da deoin dochuaid-sium and, acht tre aslach eicni; uair rofalaig Amphiaraus é re hecla cathaigthi na Tebi, & ni fhitir duni cait i rroibi acht a banchele uadein.
Et o rabas aca iaraid, adubairt Eriphile re hArgía:
‘Tabair-seo damsa,’ ar si, ‘in muntorc oir fil acut, & braithfet dit mo chele id_est Amphiaraus; uair ni fuil tarba in tachair-sea na Tebi 'na ingnais.’
Et o 'tchualaig Argía sin, roindis da fir id_est do Polinices; & adubairt Polinices in muntorc oir do thabairt do Éripile; & daradad disi sin, & roindis doib int inad i rroibi Ampiaraus, & rohaslaiged fair tocht do thogail na Teibi, & is tresin muntorc sin dorochair Ampiaraus & a bean & a mac iartain.
tra acht rohindled a carbad do Ampiaraus ar echaib caema comretha do shil Shillarus eich Chastoir mic Ioib; & ro--gabastar a barrin aloind oengel ima chend cona chimsaib coema corcarglana fair, & ua crithnaigthech carbad in churad sin risin coill athger iarnaidi d'armaib saiti seasmacha batar immi isin charbad, coma haduath faircsena re gach nduni sleg digaind derrscaigtheach ind fir sin, amail ralaig roremair i fhaicsin os cind a charpait in rig sin, & a sciath rigda roalaind i comfhocus do. Et ba hiat cethirna in churad sin dochum in chatha i tangatar a hindsib Amicclas, & asna cathrachaib id_est a Pilos, & a Pharis, & a Mase; & buidne tenda Tagetí, & milid digaire danarda srotha Eorata; & ua subach somenmnach na sarsloig sin ri tenta tachair; & ua faelid mna & maithreacha na milead sin da marbad ac denam maithiusa, & ar echaib concingtis a catha, & da fhaga ar oensuaineam i llaim gach fhir dib, & ua nochta formna na fer sin, & broit garba gaesidecha o slindenaib sis umpu, & cathbairr coemegair 'ma cendaib na curad sin.
Et dano tangadar la hAmpiaraus airig & urrig a hElis, & a Pisa, & o sruth Ailfeus; & is dar in srutha sin rosnoed Leander d'indsaige a lleannain id_est Era, co rabaided é aenda na n-aidchi andsin 'ca hindsaige.
Sochraidi in primsacairt Ampiarauis moir conigi sin.
Asa haithlIsin rogresestar in gilla oc aededach, Pardonopeus, ri na hArcaidi id_est mac muirnech Meliager, mic Oeniusa, a buidne beoda bagacha a Parrass do togail na Teibi gan fhis da mathair; & rop aneolach arm d'imluad co haes na fuairIsin in maccan sin.
Acht chena rogresestar bedga beodachta e dochum in chatha sin, & is i mathair in meic sin roindarbad alla in tiri in n-enad selga, uair ni ua tualaing tachair hi rena harrsaidecht in tan sin.
Acht chena ni dechaid do thogail Tebi nech uadailli na uad erergnu ina in ri Pardonopeus, & concarad gach duni atchid e, & ua hanrata aicned ind fhir sin ger-b anarrsaid ar n-ais.
Et ua he mian in miled sin stuicc chatha do chloistecht, & airm d'imluad, & catha do chommorad; & ua fata les-seom go nfordergad a shoigdi a curadaib comithi, & ua taitneamach errid inn oig sin d'or re cach isin tinol sin.
Uair is amlaid roba-seom & lend coem corrcorglan immi co slabradaib orda ileccair, & crundsciath cruaid cabradach ara muin, & boga trentairbertach ina llaim cli chosnamaigh, & saigedbolc solusta do craicciund linci arna linecur do lecaib logmara ar comair in rig sin.
Concinged-sum ara echaib srianacha soermacha sin inn uair sin ima n-iaditis airechta agmara na hArcaide coma suaiti achaidi slebe Menail & fidnemid Parteím da n-eis; & tangadar dirma sloig asna cathrachaib id_est a Rirpha, & a Strachta, & a hAnipe, & a Tegea, & a Sillena, & a n-Nonaiccria, & a hAirchimen, & a hAgros, & a Sofid, & a hEremaint, & a Sterefal.
Et at iat so srotha asa tangadar sochraidi la Pardonopeus id_est Clitón, & Pitia, & Lampia, & Penei, & Ason, & taisich Parrais iar tuaiscert na Greci; & ger-b Arceadacda uli in lucht sin, ua hecsamail a n-airm & a n-erred.
Uair is amlaid rouatar dream dona dirmaib sin, & mirti mora ina lamaib arna tarraing a tendtaib talman, & lorga adbulmora oaegurda ac drem aili dib, & bogada bendchaema ac drem aili dib & bera fata firgera d'armaib ac drem aile dib, & cathbairr cocuasta 'ma cendaib.
Et ger-ua comfhocus doib Meiccin and, ni tangadar sochraidi sloig esti aroen risna rigaib sin dochum na Tebi; uair ua 'san aimsir sin dochuaid Tiestes, mac Pelaip, mic Tantail, co mmnai n-Aitir, mic Peloip.
Et o 'tcualaich Aitir sin, romarbastar a dalta fen mac Tiestis, & tuc do Tiestis arna bearbad, co rocaith a richt feola; & indister cor-inta grian fair a rrith, uair nar-u ail le tuidecht os cind na cathrach colaigIsin in la sin; conid imIsin na deachaid sochraidi sloig a Maen & a Meicinib dochum na Tebi, amal indister ar fingail claindi Tantail.
Et o 'tchualaig Athaltanta, mathair Pardonopeuis, a mac do thocht isin sluagad sin, roerig amal tigir tairptig tindesnaig in ndeagaid a mic da fhastud, & tucastar athais & imdercad ara mac & ar lucht na hArcaidi uili bai 'na fharrad, & ni dernad fuirrIsin acht mad taisich na hArcaidi aca nertad leo dochum in chatha, & ni etad in n-ingen alaind Athalanta delugud re a mac ara inmaine.
Et robai aca aichne don airdrig d'Adraist an mac sin Athalanta na banselgaire & Meliager ri cuanna Calidone.
Sochraidi sloig Arcaidi andsin.
Tochastol na n-Grec conigIsin dochum na Tebe.
Acht cheana, ba hiad da chathraig cudruma na n-Grec ar chrodacht id_est in Teib talcharar imad a miled ac srainiud chatha & chomlaind, & in Athain ar leri a hecna & a heolais.
Imthusa immorro na Tiauanda, rogob ecla adbulmor ciniuda cathacha Cathim o 'tcualadar lertinol na n-Grec da n-indsaigi.
Rothochastail iarum Etiocles co hadmall anindech na Tiauanda do chosnum a cathrach risna Grecaib.
Acht chena ni ua subach somenmnach lucht na Tebe re tindscetal in tachair sin, & ni roibi ailgius cathaigti ac duni do Tianandaib in tan sin.
Uair ua senta sothoglaidi muir a cathrach, & batar sníma aile imda orro, do neoch ua mbid a n-imshnim, inna cath do chur.
Et ge ead arabba sin, tanic confad catha 'na crideadaib na Tiauanda do chosnum a ciniuda, & ni do medugud airechtais in rig Etiocles, air ua miscais leo uile e in fer na tocla id_est Polinices.
Et ua he samail Ethiocles, mar bis fael craesach confadach iter ceithrib arna comach.
Anddar les ar teiched conlenfaitis oegaireada na tret trenmarbtha sin e uaden.
Et ua tuillead re hadfuath dona Tianandaib in clu digair dianscelach ac scailiud scel na n-Grec doib; uair roindisfead fear and marcsluag gasraidi Grec do rochtain co bruach srotha Asopis, no co sliab soimtheachta Citeron, no co tolchaib tondglasa Temeson i comfhocus na Tebi.
Et rolinsadar derbairrdeada duaibsecha dírimi in talmain uili confaictis-sium na srotha 'na sruthanaib fala tre thaidbsib n-aislingthi, & conlobraidis torathair balba bruididi ac tairgi trenuilc do Thiauandaib as cach aird, & adclos daibsium tre thaidbsib bansacart dígair dasachtach do muntir Baich, do dei in fhina, ac faistine sechnon na cathrach, co n-ebairt:
‘Is olc a ndenai, a Baich,’ ar si, ‘na heicne-sea do lecun arna Tiabandaib.
Et adchiu-sa da tharb trena tnuacha concindet oencenel & oenatharda ac tachar, & cach dib ac marbad a celi id_est Ethiocles,’ ar si, ‘is olc a ndenai tachar 'man ni nach duthchu dit na dot brathair id_est do Polinices.’
Et robai 'na tast asa haithli sin.
Acht cheana rasir Ethiocles celcgach crithnaigthech faistine do denam do arin fisid, & is airi rofurail air cunnail cianaesta e id_est ar Tiresias; & ge mmad dall in drui sin, ua deigfhisid, & is airi rodallad in duini sin: bliadna robai-sium 'na mnai tre mirbail na ndéi, co tarla imresain iter Ioib & Iunaind, bandei na toili collaidi, ingen do Saturn, inn Iunaind sin caem cumachtach, co n-ebairt Ioib comma mo ailgius sarthoili na mmban na na fer.
Adrubairt, immorro, Iunaind roppa brec, & roaentaigset ua oenfhiadain id_est Tiressias, uair robai-sium sel 'na mnai & sel 'na fhir & adrubairt rabba mo ailgius na mmban na ailgius na fer.
Et ua fergach ri hIunaind sin, & robean a shuili uada-sum, & tucastar Ioib fis faistine dosum 'na aigid sin.
Nocho tre énaib na tre idbartaib ar altoir donid in fer sin faistine, acht tre tuduscad anmand a hifren, uair is mo rocreitea doib.
Et roerig Tiresias & a ingen Manto & Ethiocles aroen ris, & tangadar isin fidnemed fasaig ua comnesa doib, & imun fidnemid sin robai in mag ar-silastair Cathim, mac Agenoir, fiacla na nathrach feacht riam roimi; & conteichit dúine & indili tresin seiselbi ndemnaig n-adfuathmair bis fos isan inat sin.
Et daroindi Tiresias ix clascha comleathna andsin, & rolinaid leis iad do chaerchaib duba dathchaema in n-onoir na ndei n-ifrennaide.
Et ua holc re lucht in tiri a met chaithead da ceithrib risna hidbartaib sin.
Et rodoirtestar Tiresias fleda fina arna clasachaib comlinta sin, & robai ac eadarguidi na ndei n-ifrennaidi n-aduathmar id_est Oirc, & Proserpiana a banchele ind fhir sin, & Tresifoné aslaicthech uruada, & Caroin comthnuthach portimmarchoirthid na n-anmanda dar sruth Stig, co tudusctis anmanna do Tiresias d'indisi firindi do.
Et rogob aduath adbol Ethiocles ri dasacht Tiresias ac iarraid a itgi ar muntir ndemnaig n-ifrind.
Et o raairig Tirisias sin, rofergaiged é re muntir n-ifrind ara fhat leis robai gan nech da chur da indsaigid a hifrind.
Et rolabair in banshacart a ingen id_est Manto:
‘Ac so chucut,’ ar si, ‘anoisi airechta adbana esfhuiligi d'anmandaib i comfhocos duit a hifrend, & rohoslaicit clusala aduamara ifrind anosa, & adchim-sea sosta sirdorcha & aitdeda anaibne ichtir ifrind; & adchim,’ ar si, ‘srotha suaibrenacha sruthglasa ifirnd id_est Acheron & Flegedon & Stix; & adchiu-sa dano Pluton & Prosserpina & breitheamain ecerta ifirnd id_est Minos & Eacus & Rodomantus, tri mic Joib.
Et is amlaid coberaid bretha id_est cilarnd comthromais acco, & lecana finna and & lecana duba.
Et intan ticed in lecan find annis ar tus, ua fir in fuigell; & intan ticed in lecan dub annis, ua hanfhir in breth.
Et is lor indhisim,’ ar si Manto, ‘do thoratharaibh ifirn dit.’
‘Is leor, immorro, a ingen,’ ar se Tiresias, ‘uair cia nach fitir in fian ata arin coraid ar Sissiphus, cloch mulind do chur ana agaid shlebe, & a toitim ina chend dorisi;
Tisius coraid rotriall eiccin for mathair Apaill id_est ar Látona, is i a pian a n-ifirn, sebac aca crem a cridi, & a chridi ac forbairt and.
Gair chucaind, a ingen,’ ar se, ‘na hanmanda Grecda & Tiauanda fuilet and, & indis dam a ndelb & a ndenam, & cuich as neasa dib dam.’
‘Atat and,’ ar si, ‘Cathim, mac Agenoir, & Ermione a banchele, & ceithri hingina Caithim id_est Semile & Autonoe & Inno, & Agabe cona clandaib; & atcim,’ arsi, ‘mairb truaga na Tiauanda andso, & na n-Grec archena.’
Et o darat Manto test & tuariscbail na n-anmand leith ar leth, roerig Tireisias & rochraith a chend, & nir-gab lorg 'na laim ger-bo seanoir e.
‘Bi it tast, a ingen,’ ar se.
‘Dauiccim-sea inni bias do Grecaib & do Tiauandaib uair de sin, & bid mesa do Grecaib,’ ar sa, ‘in tachar-sa na do Tiauandaib; uair is toirrsech,’ ar se, ‘a fuil do rigaib Grec a n-ifirnd ac tairrngiri thoirrsech da fuil beo dib.’
Et as iat so na riga ua toirrsech inn ifirnd in tan sin id_est Appas garb gruganach, & Foraneus cendais cumachtach, & Pelops crechtach cendtescta, & Oenamaus feochair firfheargach, & Protus occal eccendais; & is do-side roba bancheli Stenobe darad grad da lesmac id_est do Belorofons.
Et o roemid in gilla comriachtain ria, rochosait-si re athair e, & adubairt eiccen do thobairt fuirri; & rofergaiged Protus re Pellorofons cor-cuir e d'indsaigid athar Stenobe.
Et robai torathar aicci-side id_est Cimera.
Et rocuired Bellorofons arinn eoch ar Pegais d'fhagbail a oigeda docum Chimera.
Et adrochair in torathar sin les-sium.
Raheaschrad e da eoch fen, & adbath.
Atchondairc Tiresias in caecaid curad romarb Tid do Tiauandaib; & atchondairc-sium Laius mor, athair Eidip, iter na hanmandaib; & robai ac iarraid faistine fair do denam d'aúib id_est do Eithocles, do rig na Tebi, & do Polinices, mac Edip.
Et rolauair Laius:
‘Cid 'ma n-iarthai ormsa,’ a Tiresias, ‘faistine do denum do lucht na Tebi?
uair is adbul d'ulc doronsad rimsa.
Et gid ed,’ ar se, ‘indesait daibsi a n-acuala o deib iffrind ma-dala na Tiauanda.
Is cinti tra,’ ar se, ‘concingit laich luthmara Lerna id_est na Grecci dirma diairmidi do chathaib commora do thogail Tebi.
Et is cinti coscor ac Tiauandaib do thurus gasraide Grec do gairiugud na Tebi, & ni lecfet Tiauanda dona Grecaib aitt na hinad do loscad na d'adlacad do neoch marbfer díb i tír na Tebi.
Et na bid a ecla ortsu,’ arse Laius, ‘a Ethiocles, rigi do gobail dat brathair do Polinices, uair gid feochair fuabartach in fer sin, nocha ua ri arin Teib co brath.’
Et o ralabair Laius sin atrochair in n-ifirind, & rofhac co cumascda cundtabartach scela na n-Grec da eis.
Imtusa immorro na n-Grec doberar os aird andso.
Tangadar reompo co coilltib nuaglasa Ném, & ua dirim difhoillsigud in deagsluaig sin im trascrad & im thogail Tebi leo.
Baich immorro dei inn fhina rotinoil sideic na ciniuda gamschedacha Geittecda o sleb Eim, & o sliab Otris, & o sleb Rodoip dochum na Tebi da forithin; uair ropi Semile, ingen rig na Tebi id_est Chathim, mic Agenoir, mathair Baich.
Uair intan roloisced Semile ac comriachtain do Ioib ria i rricht teined, rothairring Ioib Baich asa broind ar tesbaid mis da hinbaid, & rohailestar Ioib Baich a mbun a sliasta co cend mis, & tuc do lucht na Tebi da haltrom ar sin é, conid imIsin robai Baich ac fortacht na Tebi.
Et is amlaid robai-sium isna longportaib sotla somescda sin & nathracha nemnecha ac imarchur carpait Baith.
Et ua curata lucht carpait Baich & at e andso a n-anmand id_est Nert & Fuasnad, Ferg & Faitcius.
Et o 'tchondairc Baich na cloichtigi cumascda ciach & na neoill landorcha luaitherda re trethan int sluaig os choilltib croebglasa Nem, & dellrad na n-arm sliptha sleamangorm ri ruithnib na greni glanshoillsi, ua socht mor leosum gan tendad a tinoil tachair i n-agaid Grecach, & adubairt Baich re a muntir:
‘Bid bar tast, a oco,’ ar se, ‘& caiscid bar seiselbi.
Rocindsead na Greic,’ ar se, ‘dianscailiud na Tebi iumum-sa,’ arse, & is i mo lesmathair-sea Iunaind chomoras na catha sin chucumsa.
Et darigne ulcu aili rim remi id_est mo mathair Simile do loscud; & ata anosa ac techt co Teib da milliud.
Dobersa immorro' ar se, 'indnell furig ecin arna slogaib' Et tanic-sium remi co dian tindeasnach arin mag in n-agaid int sloig, & ua medon don lo ind n-uair sin, & ua tend tesbach in talam ri taidlanig na greni andsin.
Ragairit dei & bandéi na n-es & na n-aband cuicci, & adubairt riu:
‘Tabraid,’ ar se, ‘fial falaig dar inbearaib uisqui na Greci uili, coma lathraide lantirma a n-inada da n-eis, & dichlid uisqui chollti Nem ar tus, & dobersa a chomain chomadais daibsi aris,’ ar se.
Et ni luaithi adrubairt-sium sin na ratirmaigit lacha & luathaibne, tobair & turlaigi in tiri, coma caeiti conairi inada na n-uisced-sa id_est Lerna & Larceus, Inacus & Caradrus, Erasinus & Asterion.
Acht chena robai oensruth ua clithirdiamruib na coilliudh gan a uisqui do tragad id_est Langia a ainm, & ua huathad eolaig inn usci sin.
tra acht rogabastar ittu adual na Grecu cona fetais a sceith do chongbail, na a luirecha lasamna d'imurchur; & ni faeltais a n-eich a n-imochur na miled sin risin lasud lanitad bai orro iter ech & duni. Et rochuir Adraist taiscelta ar gach leth d'iarraid uisqui id_est co sruth na Memon, & co Síen siblach siruar, & ni fuaradar bandi usqui i n-inud dib.
Et roailsed uar na deib usqui, & nir-sailsed uisqui d'as na d'fherthain ar talmain tre bithu; & ind mar dauadar ar sechran sechnon na cailli, atchoncadar mnai n-alaind n-ilchrothaig co dubach domenmnach id_est Ipsifilé, & dalta derrscaigthech di 'na llaim id_est Achemurus, mac Ligurguis; & Ofeltes ainm aili don mac sin.
Et ua rignaidi rodelb na hingine sin, ger-b olc a hindell & a hetgud, & rosocht Adraist aca faicsinn, & adubairt:
‘A bandei coem cumachtach,’ ar se, ‘uair dar lind nocho daenna do delb acht mad dellrud diada, tobair foirithin eolais uisqui oraind, & ni thobair Ioib fortacht foraind.
Et atamait ac tocht do thogail Tebi, & ni cath marbas sind acht mad oenerti ittad.
Et is lor lindi do Ioib thussu d'fhortacht uisqui oraind.
Et comdaingnigsiu ar curpu-ni dochum in chatha, & dobertar aisceda cruid creichi dit, & dogentar idbairt gacha tuaithi dit.’
Et nir-leic ind n-itu dermár dofholachta labra secha sin don rig d'Adraist, & ba bana buadirthi na Greic uili ri heicin na hitad sin.
Et rocromastar Ipsifile a gnuis, & adbert:
‘Bid bandei daibsi me, a Grecu, & dano,’ ar si, ‘ata mo chairdes risna deib, & ata athair maith & atharda acum ar bunad; & ni lem fen in macan-sa atchithi im laim; & ni biu ni is faiti co bar fuirech, acht ticid lem co hobund co sirsruth soola id_est Langa, na traigend ri tart na re teasbach; & ni rochuindig druidi do thragad ar met is coiserctha é.
‘Et rochuir-si a dalta uaithi ar lar gu na fuirged na firu, & robai ac brecad na naidean sealad co roibi ina thast & tainic reompu 'na deagaid sin.’
In maccoem immorro robi sideic ac brisiud inn fheoir ua chosaib cach re feacht, & robid ac siubal & ac sirium & ac sireigium ag iarraid chithi a muimi in feacht aili.
Et ua haineolach d'imgabail uilc in macan sin na d'iarraid maithiusa an tan sin.’
Na Greic immorro tainic cach ua comair dib-seic ara caethib d'iarraid inn usci ar fat na cailli dluithi doimtheachta.
Et ni tosach sliged roleiged don ingin dochum inn usci.
Et ua samalta coma fochrach firmaimint re nuall subochais int sloig sin ri heas na haband, amal nuall náired aca no-combadud intan concingid calad.
Rothoirnsedar ar in n-usci na Greic gan discrit, cen delugud, gan uaisli, gan onoir do neoch dib da cheili, cu na leigtis a nn-eich na n-arad torlem da tigernaib ri tindenus ola inn usci.
Et ua dirim trethan na tond ri tachim in trensluaig sin ac ibi inn usci, coma bristi na bruaichi, & coma salach sirbuaidirthi inn aband on cind co cheli.
Et ua himda deoch iarmarta acca hol andsin, & ua samalta coma seselbi catha 'ca commorad buredach na buidne sin ac ol inn usci.
Et rolabair ri dona rigaib sin ar larmedon na haband, & robai ac beandochad inn usci & ic taescelad inn inaid i rroibe, & robai 'ga molad co mor, & adrubairt:
‘Ni fhacamar,’ ar se, ‘usci bad fherr ina int usci, na coill uad chaime ina in choill ina uil; & ni coir,’ ar se, ‘sruth do chor 'na cheand.’
Et o rachaisced a n-itaid-sium isint sruth sin, rofhacsad in n-aband.
Et daronsad sruthlecud da n-eachaib & comling da coisidib co subach somenmnach arna bruigib fondglasa fermara gor-gob brig & brogad & borrfad, at & annindi na Grecu amal concuirtis cath inn uair sin.
Et dorindit catha dib dorisi, & cach ina inad uadein do reir uird amal rouadar remi, & roimluaidsed imthecht coma luaithred lansalach na moigi na-imtigdis & contaidlitis ruithni roglana osna cathchoilltib arm batar uastu.
Is andsin immorro rothoris Adraist i mbun chroind, & gai a clemna Polinices acca conguail ina sheasam ar lar int sluaig, & roiarfaid don ingin Ipsifile:
‘Cia th' athair, a ingen,’ ar se, ‘& ca crich is dual dit?’
Rofhrecair inn ingen do-sum co truag & co toirrsech:
‘A uasail, a Adraist,’ arsi, ‘is cruaid na gnima furaile orum d'indisin, mar romarbsad mna indsi Leimin a firu acht misi mo enur,’ ar si, ‘nir-marbus m'athair.
Et is lor sin da indisi, uair ata tindenus orbsi dochum in chatha.
Acht chena is e Toaint, mac Baich, m'athair-sea, & Ipsifile m'ainm fen, & a ndoiri atú ac Ligoric do uar munter-si.’
Tucsadar cach da n-airi hi, & rob onorach ailgiusach leo a scela do cloisteacht.
Atrubairt Adraist ria-si:
‘Innis do scela uili cein no co roithset na daescurshluaig tresin coilli uair is doimtheachta hi.’
Et dochuaid i cend in sceoil d'innisin:
‘Inis Leimin,’ arsi, ‘ata arin muir anbtheanaig Egeta, & sliab n-Ethna do thaib di & sliab Athos don taib aili di, & in Tracia ob ri hob ria, & feda croebglasa comora inti, & imat gacha maithiusa inti do dainib & d'indmasaib, & ni ferr innis Saim na inis Deil na inis daraibi ar muir Eig uili na inn inis sin.
Acht chena ni dearnsamar idbairt da Uenir bandei na toili riam, & ua fergach Uenir de sin, co ra-adand bruth & dasacht ar lucht na hindsi Ni subach somenmach rabid ar sloig i n-aidchi ac lucht na hindsIsin acht mad anindi & esoenta cein no co tanic ar menmain do laechraid landiumsaig tocht do togail tiri na Tragia & ge rauadar a meic & a munter 'ca n-astad nir-ansad aco.
Na mna, immorro, ua toirrsech iat-side don turis inna fer sin uaithib.
Et ua hoc anarsaid misi in tan sein,’ ar si Ipsifile ‘& ni roibi snim ar mo menmain.
Na mna immorro aili robi cach dib ac comdingnad a cheli ac feichim na Traicia uaithib ait i rrauatar a muinter ac cathugud.
Et oenafecht da rauamar-ni and,’ ar si in ingen, ‘a medon lai, atchualamar cethra bresmadmanda bratha isinn aeor os ar cind co rachrithnaigsetar uamanda indsi Lemin & in muir mar bad gaeth congarbad, & ua fidgrad firuilc sin.
Uair is andsin roerig bean uasal Oirphi do mnaib indsi Lemin, & rogob bruth & dasacht hi co roibi ar foluamain ac buaidred in baili ar letred a haigthi da hingnib.
Et rotinoil in baili co haenthech robai a mullach in baili, & adbert:
‘Daingniged uar crideada, & bid aicned fearda fuapartach accaib, & marbaid uar firu uili maccaib, braithrib, aithrib: cuimnigid in miscais tucsad uar fir oraib ri re tri mbliadan anosa.
Et, a thruagu,’ ar si, ‘nach cualabair Brogna bean Tir do marbad a meic fein id_est Ites, & a thabairt i rricht feola aili da athair arbithin eiccni tuc Tir ara derbshiair-si id_est Pilomena a hainm.
Et robean-sum barr a tengad di na hindised air.
Et roscrib ina breit d'fhuil a tengad sin, & rothaisben da siair iartain, conid imIsin romarb Progna a mac.
Et cid daib,’ ar si Polixo, ‘nach mairbfed sib uar mic & uar fir?
Acht mad misi tra, mairbfed mo mhac & m'fher, & ata,’ ar si, ‘Uenir aca rada rind a marbad uili, & dobera-si ni ua ferr duinni anat-som.’
Et ua henmenma ac mnaib insi Lemin uili 'man comairlIsin Polixo do denum, & rochindsetar a firu uili do marbad iter oc & sen.’
‘Is Isin oes & uair doriachtadar laechrad insi Lemin o thogail na Tragia moiri.
Robai immorro fidnemed dorcha doimthechta isint sleb ua comnesa doib, & dachuadar mna insi Lemin d'iarraid fhrecra arna deib, & tangadar badba bellderga ichtair ifirn da mbuaidred-sunt conici sin.
Et rouai Uenir uanchumachtach & Enio urbadach, siur Mairt, dei in chatha, ac furail uilc ar na mnaib sin.
Et is amlaid robai Polixo ben Charoip, & taidbsi a mic 'na farrad andsin.
Et dorindseadar comluigi, co marbfidis a Et rogab adfuath adbul mise,’ arsi Ipsiphile, ‘ac faicsin na mban sin amal aig n-allaid timtechech iter cuanairt croesos--laicthi confadacha do chonaib allta.’
‘Cid tra acht tangadar na fir sin asa longaib, & daronsad idbarta ecsamla imda, & roleicset re hol & re haibnius iad, comdis mescda mertnecha Et o rathoit a suan sirchotalta ar na sluagaib, tangadar a mna fegi furuagra da n-indsaigid da marbad, cunsaeset fuithib amal saga gera gortacha leoman da culenaib ac inred alma & indili.
Et a athair inmain, a Adraist,’ ar si Ipsifile, ‘ni fetar ca holc dib indesaid duid ar tus: acht romarb Górge arnaid aneolach a fer andsin id_est Elemus.
Et is amlaid robai-sium & a da laim impi-si, co rosaid in cloideb ind, cor-gob a rrindi ina chorp fen, & rouai-seom fos aca pocad-si & a lama ima bragaid.
Et ni fhetaim-sea a n-airium uili gach ar-marbad andsin.
Acht chena indesaid becan da maithib uodein id_est Mirmédon.
Romarb immorro Epopéa a mac uadein, & romarb Licáse a derbrathair comaesta uodein id_est Cidomon, & roui ac cui osa cind.
Et romarbad Alcimiden, & robenad a cheand de.
Et o adchondarcas-sa sin, rogab ecla & adfuath me, & tanac-sa im baidb buaidertha co tech m'athar id_est Toaint, & ge-r fata amach on baili in tech i rroibi, robai aca iarfaide:
‘Ca raet in muirn,’ ar se, ‘ar-atcluineam isin baili?’
Et roindis uli da hathair sin:
‘Eirig a athair inmain,’ ar si, ‘uair da mbertar oraind, muirbfer sind aroen.’.’
Et roerig Toaint ar sin & Ipsiphile a ingen, & tangadar ar chaethib diamra in baili amach, conriachtadar conicci in arbach, & robadar co dichealta 'ca descain.
Et atchondcadar na firu foena fiarletarthi ina lepthaib arna marbad da mnaib fen tre aslach Uenire forru, & na cloidmi croderga trena cnesaib & na slega arna sarbrisiud treompo, & consnaetis na copana caema comola arna lintib fala firmora batar and re haidbli in airlig.
Uair batar seanoraig arna sitled andsin, & oic arna n-airlech, & maccaim arna mudugud.
Et adchondairc Ipsiphile taidbsi Baich ua tri ag iarraid a mic Toaint id_est a hathar-si, & tucastar Ipsiphile aichni ar Baith andsin.
Et rolabair Baich riu:
‘Dena imtheacht, a mic,’ ar se, ‘& facaib inis Lemin, & is lor a fhat risna deib ata inis Lemin acut.
Et a ingen,’ ar se, ‘ber let t'athair, & cuir ina curach e baili i teit in mur isin muir moir amach, & dober-sa fortacht fair ar sin.’
Roimthig Baich, & rofhacaib comartha sliged doib, & tangadar-sum reompo 'sin sligid & rochuir in ingen a hathair arin muir, & robadar aroen ac comchui co matin.
Et tanic inn ingen ar culu uada, & rouid ac silliud ara hais co minic ara hathair.
Et o thanic la cona lansoillsi, adchondcadar na mna insi Lemin na huilc sin doronsad fen id_est a fir da marbad, & ua haithrech leosum sin, & rangadar, & rouatar ag gul & ag golgairi uastu.
Acht ua saidbir sochonaig d'erraib & d'armaib & d'indmasaib int olen sin conici sin; & rauadar na mna sin o sen amach nama gan tirecor gan trebaire gan ar gan buain gan fhiru caema 'ga chomditin.
Imthusa immorro Ipsiphile doronni tenid n-idbarta i tig a hathar, & rothocaib airm & etgud a hathar.
Et robai claideb in rig lan d'fhuil ina laim, mar bad ar marbad a hathar robeth & arna adluccun.
Et tucad andsin ferand a hathar di id_est aireochus indse Lemin Ua minic lesi & re Polixo cumnigud in chuil sin, & robidis co tairrsech taetenacha acca tuireom eturru.
Et o rauatar mna insi Lemin amlaidh sin dar eis a fer, adchondcadar in luing luchtmair lanmoir, amal oleán do learaib in mara, no amal sliab lethan lanmor ar met.
Et is i robai and-sin in bennfhata badbluath cetlong in betha id_est Argo, & rigrad glendmer glanarmach Grec inti, intan dochuadar d'iarraid in croicind órda co tir na Colachetta.
Et o rascuirsedar da n-imrud & robai in muir in taeichli, ‘adchualamar,’ ar si Ipsifile, ‘guth oenduni asin luing.
Et is e rouai andsin id_est Oirfeus ceolbind, cruitire, mac Oeaeger, & a gualu risin seolcrand ac airfidiud do lucht na lunga, comad lugaiti snim na saersluag re saethar ind imrama, & ba samalta lindi coma hiat lucht na Tragia do thogail indsi Lemin oraind.’
‘Et roergestar asa haithlIsin sestan & seiseilbi mor i toegib indsi Leimin.
Et dochuamar-ni arsin i toraib roarda romora & i crandócaib comdaingni claraid os cind na cathrach.
Et rotinolsetar mna croda chrithnaigthecha indsi Lemhin cairrgi cruaidhi comamais, & bera fata firgera, & airm troma toirrsecha a fer uadein nomarbsad remi sin, & ragabsad a claidbi forruamanda fuilidi ina lamaib, & rogabsad a lurecha lasamna salcha snadmandacha 'ma corpaib & a cathbairr caema cathaigi 'ma cendaib.
Et ua samalta lindi tra coma torathur firmor for-granda fairrgi rabeth andsin d'aithi & do degail oraind ar n-uilc & ar n-ecorach oraind, & nar-ba long luchtmar lanalaind.
Is andsin tra adracht gaeth gottshnimach glorach, co rasraineastair in luing sin urchur saigti sithguirmi o tir & o tracht amach.
Et rochumaiscseadar andsin neoill comfhliucha ciachmora na firmaminti, cor-ua dorchatu dluith iter muir & tir & co tocuatis na tonda trenmora na longa uar barr aen.
er ar & uar uachtar doib & co leictis dib sis in feacht n-aill co grian & go ganem nglasruad ar n-ichtar.
Et ger-ba tenda talchara tra na trenfir sin rouadar isin luing sin, nir-ba tualaing ursclaidi na hengnoma iad isinn uair sin re met na mor-ainbthine.
Et robai a seolchrand sirfhada sirmor na luingIsin aca dianscailiud & ac adradbrisiud ara met & ara roairdi ac tocuail & toirniub re sitgail na saebgaithIsin in uair sin.
Et dano robamar-ni ac dibrucud & ac dichur uaind na luingIsin do leth aili co telcmais armu aithgere urnochta in n-aigid na miled sin id_est in trenfer thalchair Tailemon, & Pelias mac Aicuis, & Aercail mac Ampitriontis.
Et ua hadual saethar na sarluingIsin re hanfine in mara & re'r cathagad-ni don leth araill.
Et badar drem dona degsluagaib sin ac daingnigud & ac diten a luingi & scellbolga do sciathaib ina timchell, & drem aili ac telad & ac taescad a huisqui asa hichtur, & drem ac cathug-hadh co calmachroda osa cind.
Et rotelcthea atorra?
and-sin,’ arsi, ‘cetha cumasctha cruadarm, coma samalta re frasaib cruaidi clothnechta inn amsir gairb gemridh na bera rindgera romora, & na clocha cruindi comdibhraicthi, & na saighdi snasta sodibraicthi, & na slega lasamna langera trena 'roile isinn uair sin.’
‘Et asa haithlIsin roergedar gathana glanailli greni & ruith-nigud rosoillsi, coma fornell & coma forreill duind na slúaigh robdar isinn luing.
Et o 'dchondcamar iad ban samhla sin, rothuitsetar ar n-airm as ar lamaib, & tainic ar n-aicned boeth banamail uadein duind.
Et adchondcamar-ni amh andsin Peil mac Aicuis, & Tailemon mor mac Aiacuis, & Anatheus tend tomaithmech, & Ifiton data deaglamaig.
Et ba follus osna sluagaib snimacha sin archu eangnuma in domuin id_est Ercoil mac Ampitriontis.
Roclaenad-som andsin cach mbord & cach leth don luing asa ticed re fiuchad na fergi firmoire ac saeighid cusna sluagaib.
Et gid Iason mac Eson immorro ba luthmar leidmech 'sin luing sin, & Oenidies mer mormenmnach, & Idas uallach allata, & Talabus talchar tairisi, & da mac tenda togaidi Tindair id_est Castor & Pullux, & da mac beoda borrfadhecha Boiria id_est Sétiusa & Ealiais, & ba drem do degdainib na lunga sin in lucht sin.’
‘Batar tra fan samla sin ac frasimram in mara & ac dibrucun in muir uaithib.
Et dano rouai in luamairi fosaich fireolach inti id_est Tifis ac stiuradh na lunga sin co na leiced a badbrisiud im chairrgib cendgarba in mara morainbthenaig.
Et rouadar-som isinn eicin sin, cein cor-erig Iason mac Eson & craeb alaind olachraind ina laim i comartha sida, & is i seic robid i llaim Mopsus, taisig da muntir, & robui ag iarraid sida oraindi.’
‘Acht chena nir-ba miad re lucht na luingi in raraid Iason.
Et ni chualamar-ni acht fogur bras a gotha risin ngaith chugaind.
Et is andsin roerigedar in coica trenfher ua tendi & ua tresi isin luing, & rogobsad ruadhramada romora 'na lamaib, & roraeset co fortren feramail in luing sin dochum chuain caladpuirt.
Et ba socharthanacha re silliud isinn uair sin chena gnuisi gruadsoillsi na curad croda re fornert inn imroma & re fiuchud na fergi firmoiri adracht intib.
Ba samail lindi in sluag sin & ba dei uaisli adhartha tiastais do dindgnaib roglana richid uan talmain.’
‘Et is andsin adchoncamar Teis, mac Eig, mic Nephtuin, ac erge asin luing & ua diumsach in deglaech sin a haithli thogla na cathrach id_est Marathon; & adchondcamar dano andsin in rígh uasal Admet, & adchondcamar in cruitire coelbind na Traigia id_est Orfeus; & robui andsin didiu in milid Meleager, mac rig na Calidone, & Pelias mac Aicuis, & Iles mac Ercail & airm 'na laim.’
‘Cid tra acht,’ ar si, ‘rofhoslaicidh lindi doirrsi ar tigead risna damaib sin.
Et ni dernaid idbarta, na suan na sadailli acaind o romarbsamar ar firu co haes na fuairi sin.
Rogobh gach fer dib sin ac toga a thochmairc uaindi in lin robamar.
Acht cheana tuigim-se na dei nar-ua cedugud na comairli dam uadein fes re hIason isinn aidchi sin, ger-ua sochraid socharthanach re mnaib aili é.
Et rouatar-sum co cend mbliadna comlaine acaind isan indsi sin, cen co rucait clanda suarca socenelacha daib.
Et rucus-sa da mac andsin do Iason mac Esoin id_est Toas & Eunios a n-anmanda.
Acht chena ni fhetar a n-ord na a n-aidhid, uair is fichi bliadan co haes na fuairi-sea o rus-facus aca n-aileamain & 'ga n-altrom acin rigain lamgil ac Lichasta.
Et i cind na bliadna sin tra rogob Iason ag gresacht a muntire 'man n-indsi d'fhacuail, o 'dchondairc in muir co tai tegligi.
Et ge ragell-sium.
andsin techt arís dom indsaigi-sea co hindis Lemin, ni racomaill ani sin.’
‘Cid tra acht o raairig Tifis, luamairi na luingi sin, ruithne grene do glansoillsigud, rotrellaim tachar a luingi, & rochomergedar na sluaig, & rogob Iason a armo re cach andsin, & rofacbadar amlaid sin in indsi.
Robamar-ni 'ga feithem & 'ga fegaircsi, cein co ndechaid ar seg asar suilib 'ga sithshellad.’
‘Asa haithlIsin tra adchualadar mna indsi Lemin m'athair-sea do beth i rigi indsi Chio, indsi dearbrathar do id_est Cuuis mic Baich; & ba holc leo-sum sin gan a marbad & gan a mudugud dam-sa, amal romarbsad fein a fir & a n-aithrecha, & rocindead leo mo marbad-sa ind.
O 'tchuala-sa sin immorro,’ ar si, ‘roelus mo enur uaithib re taeb in mara; & o na fuarus nech re setugud sliged dam d'indsaigid m'athar id_est Toaint, tucad me i ndairi & i ndochraidi dochum bar crichi-si, a Grecu.’
Et o rabai Ipsipile amlaidh sin ac comradh risin rig n-uasal re hAdraist & a ni thuc da haire a daltan dathalaind da fhacbail isin choilleigh di heis.
Et intan dachuaidh d'iarraid uisce risna Grecaib, & o rafhacaib-si immorro in mac bec isin, rothuit a suan remcotalta air ar lar ind fheoir & in airthind.
Et in am robai andsin, tanic nathair adhuathmar urbadach da indsaigid.
Is amlaidh robai in nathair sin & ruisc dimora dubglasa 'na ceand co n-uanfad neimi.
Ba glomar a crais co tri tengthaib tendtidi ac taidligud ima carbad & co tri srethaib d'fhiaclaib croma cruadgera ina cind.
Et ua cois-sechartha du Ioib in nathair sin, & is and rocatlad fecht and i timchull na tempall sin caeimchoiserca bidís i comfhochraib di.
Et rogluaiseth-si na railgi romora asa n-ait & asa n-inad & na clacha comthenda a tendtaib talman intan rocomerged.
Et tainic rompi d'iarraidh uisci co dian & co dasachtach & a craes urgranda oslaicthi uirri ag sugud gaithi aidhoir in darna fecht, in feacht aili immorro ac ithi in fheoir & inn airthind do chasc a hithad.
Et rus-bean bem da heirr gan airigud di don maccaem sin, co rus-facaib cen anmain.
O 'tchualaig tra Ipsifile scret in mic aca marbad, roerich da iarraid, & robai 'ga gairm.
O na fuair he & atchondairc in nathraig, roiacht & roeig co cualadar Greic uili golgairi na hingine.
Is andsin rogresestair rig oc na hArcaidi id_est Partanapeus, a eocho fon egiom ar na radh d'Adhraist don airdrig ris.
Et o 'tchualaich fochond in guba, roindis da chach; & o raindis, rogobh Ipomedon ard airegda cairrig comthruim comnert a tendtaib talman & tuc ro n-urchair d'indsaigid na nathrach.
Acht chena ni derna acht scenm disi sin.
Tanic immorro asa haithlIsin Capaneus ar cind conaire di, & gae suainmech sodibraicthi ina laim, & is ed roraid ria:
‘Ni ba hinand,’ ar se, ‘int urchar o chianaib.
Ni fhuil ac deib nime a thairmeasc imam-sa gan du marbad dam.’
Et rodibraic in faga di 'na diaid sin, co roben in craisech di, co rotregdastar a hucht & a hindi, co torchair marb cen anmain.
Ba ferg immorro la hIoib annIsin id_est an nathair do marbad do Chapaneus, & rotriall saegnen tened do lecud da indsaigid andsin, & ged ed rothairmisc gussin cath ar n-uair.
Imthusa Ipsifile intan robui ac iarraid in maccaim, adchondairc in fer frasach forderg d'fuil na naiden & tainic da indsaigid co dubach dian domenmnach, & robui ac pocad in mic.
Acht chena rasaeed a delb & a dath isinn uair sin cu nar-fhurusa aichni a chuirp arna cruadledrad o dhriuch nemi na nathrach.
Et is amlaid robai-si 'na timchell andsin, amal bis ethaid foluaimneach im net ar na choll do nathraig impi; & rogab ina hucht he.
Rochomglan crechta a chnis da fult fhata fhira-laind, & tuc a faid firguil os aird, & is ed roraid:
‘Truag sin, a Arsemaris inmain,’ ar si, ‘is tu ua tocha lium & ba cland dam-sa dar eis mo mac, & ua comdingnad dar eis m'atharda.
Et a mic,’ ar si, ‘caidi in gnuis glan gruadalaind & na briathra gotha-gairechtacha batar let, na tuictis daeini aili acht mad misi re sirchlechtad?
Uch tra is truag in turus dochuadus-sa uait dar a dermaitius tu.
Et, a Grecu,’ ar si, ‘marbaid-si misi, co na faiciur athair in mic-sea id_est Ligurgus, & co na faiciur a mathair id_est Eruididse, uair isam bandama di d'eis a meic do milliud acum; & is taisci tra aidlecar misi na daber a mac ban samlaid-sea 'na hucht.’
Atclos immorro na scela sin ba chetoir co tigib lethna lan-mora Ligurguis id_est athair in meic.
Et is amlaid robai seic edon ar ndenom edport i sleb Peris, & is ed roraided ris andsin, comad da muntir romurfithea in cetduine do Grecaib ar in cathugud Tiauanda.
Is de sin tanic-seom co toirrsech tindesnach dochum na sluag o 'tchualaig na stucu coema comairic aca senm.
Ipsifile immorro o rabui & an mac marb aca imarchor aici, is and dorala a mathair di 'na haigid & airechta cend-caema corp-glana do mnaib 'na farrad & dirmanda degsluaig ac caeiniud in mic sin.
Ligurgus immorro ar ferg & ar fualang dachuaid in scel sin do, & tanic remi co dian dasachtach, & adbert:
‘Caide,’ ar se, ‘in bean i roibi mo mac-sa na laim?
tabraid cucum, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘in colaig confadaig co romarbar hi i cinta mo meic.’
Et is cuma roraid sin & tanic da hindsaigid, & claideb urnocht 'na laim.
Is andsin tuc in trenfer natharda nemlesc id_est Tíd mac Oeniusa in sciath ar scath na hingine, & adbert:
‘A duni dasachtaich,’ ar se, ‘leic a aenur in mignim triallai.’
Et doriachtadar asa haithlIsin Capaneus & Ipamedon & Partonopeus mac Eremandtuis & a claidbi nochta 'na lamaib co roiadsad im Ligurgus da marbad & da mudugud, da saraiged iad 'man ingin.
Is andsin rocomergedar munter Ligurguis do gliaid re Grecaib, & robui int ardrig Adraist 'ga n-astad & 'ga n-irrdegail.
Atbert dono Ampiaruss in sacart:
‘Leicid as, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘uar fich & uar ngliaid, uair is facus uar coibnes & uar cairdeas.’
Nir-ua áil tra re Tid, mac Oeniusa, inn irgail do thairmesc, & is ed roraid:
‘Is dana dit, a Ligurguis,’ ar se, ‘inni triallai id_est in ben do marbad ar ar faesum & ar ar comairci.
Acht is lor dit bith i socra & i sadaili ac cainiud do mic d'ar n-eis-ne cein bem ac tachar risna Tiauandaib.’
Rofhrecair tra Ligurgus dósom, & is ead roraid:
‘Ni fheadar-sa am,’ ar se, ‘comad buidni bidbad do thogail Teibi sib.
Et mas ead as ail lib tra, millid misi, uair ni fhuilim lin tachair daib.’
Et is amlaid roui-sium aca rad sin & mirun & aninni mor aici.
Et robui ac fegad a cathrach uad, cu cualadar comorad catha & irgaili isin cathraig thall.
Is iad rohindised do beth andsin marcsluag gasraidi Grec ac inrud in tigIsin Ligurguis, uair is ed rohindised isin dunad uilc & ecora do denam do Ligurgus i muich risna sluagaib.
Et roergedar de sidi na Greic rouadar thall isin baili & aithindeda luatha lasamna 'na lamaib do loscud tigi Ligurguis & da breith cona n-altoraib ailli adartha leo i ndairi & i ndochur.
Ba buaidirthi tra tegdais in trenfhir sin o gul & o gair ban & mac aca milliud inti.
Is andsin immorro tanic in ri uasal Adraist, & tuargaib Ipsifile i fiadnaisi in tsluaig, & adbert:
‘Traetar uar ferga & uar ficha, a firu,’ ar se, ‘& na dentar lib olc Ligurguis; uair ac seo in bean tuc int uisci daib, & si slan gan crechtnuchud.’
Ba he tra samail in tsluaig Grec in tan sin in muir acgarb anbthenach & na gaetha garba gatsnimacha gatmí 'ga cumasc & 'ca combuaidred gu n-udcith anfad garb gemreta in lear longach lanadbul as cach aird, cein co nn-eirig in ri uasal onorach id_est Nephtuin, co cuireand ina tast & ana teigli hi.
Et antan robadar Greic fan samla sin, is andsin tangadar da mac Ipsiphile & Iasoin mic Esoin o inis Lemin a ndiaid a mathar co tech Ligurguis.
Et rohindised do Ligurgus in dias sin do thorachtain da thig id_est da mac Ipsifile.
Et tangadar ua chetoir i fortacht & i forithin Ligurguis gan fhis & gan aichne doib.
Et o 'tchualadar imrad indsi Lemin & Ipsifile ingine Toaint, rascailset na sluaga sarechtacha, cein co rangadar airm a roibi a mathair, & cor-iadsad a lama luathglasta impi.
O 'tchondairc-si immorro erred & indtsamail a n-athar ina sciathaib coema commora & a airm urnochta ina lamaib, rothoit-si andsin co hanband eserit re romet na failti rogob ac faicsin na mac sin, & rus-snigestar frasa diana der dar gruadib di.
Na Greic immorro roleigsedar a ferga re lar, & rolabair in rigsacart uasal Ampiaraus, & is ed roraid:
‘Eistet rim-sa, a gasrada Grec & Ligurguis, co roindisiur daib a n-ebairt dea na faistine id_est Apaill rium co buigbed sibsi, a Grecu, na hairdi urbada-sa ar cae uar conairi ac techt in turisa, conid airIsin is choir daib uar ferga da thairmesc & uar n-airm do chur uaib & idbarta uaisli imdai & cluicheda suarca subacha i n-onoir in mic mairb-sea id_est Arsemair mic Ligurig co mairet sin co forceand saegail & co dered in domuin.
Uair ni ferr do-sum comshaegul re Neastur cundail cianaesta, no re Laimedon lansaeglach, na haeidid na samla-sa fair; uair airemthar do-som iter deib é da eis.’
Tainic tra ind agaid fae sin, & deisitar ina longportaib isin n-aidchi sin.
Adchlos immorro ua chathrachaib na Greci gartgloni na Greic do commorad cluichi chaintig i n-onoir & in n-airmitin mic Ligurguis.
Et is les dorondad ar tus riam a macsamlai in cluichIsin la hErcail mac Ampitrionis i n-onoir Peloip mic Thantail.
O thainic tra solus tratheirgi do lo arnamarach, & roerig grian glan uallach ina mill crochomderg seach imellbord talman, co roruithnig a gathana glanshoillsi uar tuaithebrachaib in talman, rochomergedar na sluaig iter thall & amuich, comma fograch na fidnemid & feda foithremra coillted Neim re seastan & re seiselbi na sluag sin ac comergi do chommorad na cluiched cainthech sin.
Robui immorro Ligurgus ina rigsuidi & a bancheli Eruididse 'na farrad & bantrochta buaidirthi badbchaintech maraen ria ac cainiud a meic.
Rochomnuallsad leo isinn uair curaid & cathmilid & lathagaili Grec i tigib rigda romora Ligurguis; & ge rachainsed Greic in mac sin, roairigsetar a miscais co mor ac lucht in baile.
Is andsin rogab Adraist, ardri Grec, ac comdingnad Ligurguis do scur a chuma & a thoirrsi.
Ni chualaig-sium sin tra re confad na cumad & re fiuchud na fergi.
Acus asa haithlIsin rocomecrad leosum comrair don mac sin don fhid chuanda chuiprisc & d'fhualascaib ali uraidi & do luibib barrglana bolathmara nach leictis lobud no lochrad dona corpaib ima cuirtis id_est sinomum & ballsam & mirr & tuis.
Et rochoraigid etaigi caema corcorglana thiri na Sithriu taris amuich aneachtair arna n-ilecur do snath alaind orda & do gemaib cruindi carrmogail.
Et roordaig a athair andsin a airm chaema chosmaili in meic beic sin & fadbarm a senathar do thabairt dochum in chuirp sin da n-idbairt & da comloscud leis.
Uair is ed ua bes accusum andsin na cuirp onoracha do loscud & d'edbairt dona deib adartha.
Is andsin roerig in fisid fireolach Ampiaraus & Greic ar cheana don leith ele, acus rocomecrad leo teni taidlech taeblasamna, coma sonairti soimthechta, & coma caeiti comredi na feda dluithi doimthechta da n-eis.
Et o thairnic leosum in teini sin, rosuidigit acu altoiri da deib nuaglana nime & da deib aduathmara ifrind, & rosendit fetana cuasmora ceolbindi do gach leith & da gach thaib dib.
Et rochomergedar secht rig Grec im Ligurgus do chommorud in chainte sin.
Roergedar buidne bithi banamla maroen re mathair in mic id_est Erudidse & dirmanda doescursluaig impi-si id_est a buimmi, & 'ma buimi in mic sin fa Ipsiphile & da mac Iasoin mic Esoin maroen ria a da chomalta.
O dariacht immorro Eruididsi mathair in mic dar dorus in baili amach, rolobair o guth mor, & is ed roraid:
‘A meic,’ ar si, ‘ni hi seo aeidid rofaelius-sa ort.
Et dursan dam t'aithni dot aileamain & dot altrom do mnui meblaig mibriathraig do lucht indsi Lemin!
Et, a Grecu,’ arsi, ‘na cathid uar seoid na bar n-indmasa elaiscib na hidbarta-sa ni as sia acht loiscther lib in bean 'gar-millead in mac id_est Ipsiphile & loiscther misi maroen ria.’
Et o tharnic dissIsin da rad, roerig Ligurgus, & rochuir a erred & a etach uasal idbarta de, & rothesc a fholt, & rochuir isin tenid iat dib linib mar chomarthai mbroin & domenman, & is ed roraid:
‘A Ioib,’ ar se, ‘is mibriathrach rouadais rim ac cetugud mo meic da marbad, uair bam sacart uasal idbarta dit mad gusan ndiu.’
Is andsin roerig fathrand & fidren ruadlasrach romoiri do thenid inna hidbarta, & ba snimach do Grecaib astod Ligurguis & a bancheli gan dul daib da loscud isin tenid sin.
Rob adbul tra in tan sin & ba fograch leca logmara aga loscud inti 'ca loscud & aircet aengel aithlegtha & or ac snigi dar etaigib rigda roailli & fin & fuil ac fiuchud i tulchomaib cuanda comdaingne.
Is andsin roergedar secht ndirmanda do marcsluag Grec 'ma secht rigaib robeoda, & tucsad tri graifni i timchull na tendted sin.
Robuailsetar basa leo, & rothuairgid ochta & urbruindeda andsin, & rohidbraid alma & cethra d'iarraid fhesa & eolais, amal ba bes accu-sum.
Racaithed tra in la sin leosum re comram in cluichi sin, no co-ro luaithred lanmin ar lasad na tenti taeblasamna re hirthosach na haidchi.
Isin maitin arnamarach rochomergedar uili, & dorignead leo tempoll suaichnich soineamail 'ma luaithred chuirp in meic sin id_est Arsemarus; & tairnic leo e co cend noi la & noi n-aidchi.
Rorindad & rohecrad im slesaib in tempaill sin id_est delb Ipsifile ac iarraid uisci do Grecaib intan robadar i nn-itaid remi sin, & delb Arsimaruis & na nathrach romarb é, & delb gae Capaneuis da romarb in nathair.
O tharnic tra in saethar sin do denam, tangadar senoraig croma chianaesta, & maccaim robega rebacha, & daescurslaig denmech deaith do chomorad aenaich in n-onoir in mic sin aroen re gasradaib Grec.
Et rob e inad inn aenaich id_est glend glasfherach comreid, & feda foithremla firglana 'na thimcheall iter da sliab chruindi chomarda, & rasuidetar buidne croda cathacha na n-Grec i mucha do lo & do laithi andsin.
Et roairim cach a sochraidi and, & o rohairmed, tucad chucu cet do buaib data deigremra & a comlin da tharbaib comaesta comdatha daibsi.
Et tucad chucu asa haithlIsin delba rindta roailli a n-athar & a senathar d'urgairdigud aicenta orru isinn oenach.
Et roleigit leosum andsin ar tus grega diana degretha srianailli socra sluagda sofhermaig dar moigib minreidi inn aenaig sin.
As i tra cetna ech tucad andsin id_est Arion ech aibind allmarda Adraist ind n-airdrig.
Ba suaichnich am egcosc inn eich sin id_est gabair gormglasa, gasta, gualandtiug, badba, bircluasach, socair, saemind, soermach, co moing caim corcarglain, co n-erboll comtroma comdatha, do bunad cenel eich Neptuín, dea in mara, uair is cuma conriadad si muir & tir.
Et ni ba miad le nech aili do lecud fuirri acht mad Adraist int ardri a oenur.
Et gid ed tuc-som da cliamain in la sin hi dochum inn oenaig id_est do Polinices & is ed roraid sin:
‘Na buail co menic t'ech, a gilla,’ ar se, ‘& comgres cach & is lor do gresacht fuirre-si sin, & reithfid in mag amal roreithset eich greini Faóaetan mic Apaill.’
Et roerig Ampiaraus andsin id_est sacart mor na Greci, dochum na comlingi cetna, & da ech ailli oengela fóe eo nn-étach a comdatha immi i comartha a sacerdoiti, & ba do shil eich Chastoir id_est Sillarais dona heachaib sin.
Et rocomerig 'na diaid sin Ademet, taisech na Tesailli, & lairthecha dana diana deigretha fae, & siad ailli aladbreca.
Et is iad ba comnesa do sin da mac Iasoin mic Esoin & Ipsifile id_est Toas & Eunihos; & ua cosmail tra delba na desIsin iter armaib & echaib & etaigib.
Tangadar 'na ndiaid sin and Coromis & Ipodomus.
Cromis, immorro, ba do shil hErcoil mic Ampitrionis do; & Ipodomus ba do sil Onamaus, rig Pissa, do; & ni greised nech dib sin a eocho sech aroili.
Et eich Diomit rig na n-Geittecda ua Cromis, & is e in Diemid isin doberead a aigedu da echaib co marbdais & co n-ithdis iad, cein no co riacht Ercoil ar aigidecht da thig, & co tard Ercail eisum fen daib & co rusmarbsad.
Ipodomus, immorro, eich a athar id_est Inomaus robadar foe seic.
Et is e int Enomaus rofocrad comrith n-echda ar gach fer ticed d'iarraid a ingine fair; & o teigtis a eich-sum dib, romarbdais aici in lucht sin fochetoir.
Et is amlaid robadar na heich sin & broen fola na fer romarbaid dib ara carput i comartha coscair.
tra acht rosuidiged leosum andsin crich & comartha cusa leicfitis an n-eocho & dair barrlom bunlethan robai i cind in muigi & carrac trenmor thunidi in n-aird aili and & ed cheithri n-urchur saigdi sithguirmi eatorru sin. Is i tra aimser i raibi Apaill mac Ioib ac sirsenm a chruiti & i mullach slebi Barnaps ac admolad na ndei.
Et atchondairc uad na Grecu forin moig mor reid ara rabadar; & robai ac tobairt aichni ar cach oen ba leith dib, & adchondairc andsin Admeit ri na Tesailli, & Ampiaraus uasalsacart, & bad caraid cumtha am dosum in dias sin.
Uair robui 'na haegairi thret do fhir dib id_est do Emit, intan rohathchuired asa deacht é & ua sacart uasal idbarta do Ampiaraus.
Et o rabui ag fegad amlaid sin, is ed roraid:
‘Cia iter,’ ar se, ‘in dea rogres na caraid-sea uil acum-sa dochum chathaigti na Tebi?
gid ed rafuil soni ngrada acum uar in dis sin, uair is tigerna & is cara bunaid Adiemit, ri na Tesailli.
Ampiaraus, immorro, rofitir fein gach ni asfas dochair ind.’
Et is cuma roraid sin & ro-muidsed frasa diana der dar gruaidib do, & tanic mar saegnen tened no mar saigid a sreing no co ranic i coillid Nem.
Isin uair sin robai Proteus ac cur crandchair a chathbarr 'm a n-inadaib comlenga, & rocoraigid iad-sum ban samla sin.
Robui tra ailgius & tindinis mor ac na feraib & ac na hechaib 'man comrith.
Ua hadbul, immorro, re heistecht sitrech & setfedach na n-ech sin & a lemenda re gloraib na srian aca n-imnastad.
Et asa haithlIsin roleicit i n-enfhecht & a n-enuair dochum a retha.
Ua dluith deinmech am docuas andsin, & nir-ba suaichnich soaichnid neach dib seach aroili re daithi & re denmidi dochuadar uaithib.
Et ua dicheltai uili na dirmanda sin dona haichthib comdorcha cumascda rochomerig dib re snuadallus na herma, re dendgail na roth, re hanalaib na n-each & na curad ic imchosnum thosaich isin chomling.
Et ua hilbrecca illathach na moigi minreidi risna cethaib comgela cubair consnigtis re hóilib na heachraidi ac fosenm na srianmirend isinn uair sin.
Et ba fogradach firmamint andsin re greasacht na curad comrumach uar na hechaib ailli allmarda.
Is andsin tra roarig Aroén id_est ech Adraist, marcach caem comuithech do bith fuirri id_est Polinices, & rogob dremni & dasacht & daebili, & robui ac fegad a tigerna fen & aca iarraid ar fud in muigi moradbail.
Et ge rabui, dochuaid sin urchur saigti sithguirmi andsin do gregaib glanailli Grec.
Ampiaraus immorro ba nesu d'Aroén & ba fada etorru & in marcach Tesalta id_est Ademet ina diaid sec.
Et is iad ua nesa do-siden dano da mac Iasoin id_est Enunios & Tous, & nir-greis nech dib-side a eochu sech araili do chomull a charadraid.
Crómos acgarb, immorro, & Ipodamus anachéil fo deoid, & a meit na miled sin da n-eachaib 'ga n-imarcur is ed uadera sin.
Ampiaraus rogob seic ar athgairid na conairi da tairechtain tosaich, & is ed ana cetna dorone Admeit, ri na Teasailli, & ba denmech in marcach isin, uair is cumma no-lenad do thaeib & do druim a eich.
Aroén, immorro, int ech robui fa Polinices, robui co siblach sechranda, uair nir-cumaing a certugud cein no cu ruc Ampiaraus tosach de.
Et ua he Admeid ua comnesu do-side, cein no cor-impa Aroén ech Adraist aris ar set na sliged.
Act cheana ni gresed Polinices & ni astadus, ucht robui ina tham & ina thaisi i nn-ichtur in carbaid inn uair sin.
Is andsin rofhacsad aris na heich diana deinmetha sin caethi a comretha, & dochuadar fordol conairi, co rogabsad a carpaid caema cumaidi i cend aroili & a cheli.
Acus gid ed, nir-ba lor lesna curadaib gresacht na n-ech o sporaib athgera iarnaide no co ndernsad o gothaib moraib & o a n-anmandaib dilsi uadein.
Rogres tra Admeit andsin Poloe & Siris a da each.
Rogreis dono Ampiaraus Asceton datha deigretha et Sicnus gleglan glegel gualandtiug.
Rogres, immorro, Cromis Strimon.
Robui Echion ua Uneos mac Iasoin.
Rogres dono Ipodomus Cidóna.
Rogres Tohas mac Iasoin Podarsen.
Nir-labair Polinices risin n-ech bui fai id_est re hAreon, uair nir-lam a guth do cloistecht di.
Et ba cuntabartach coscur co fada andsin iter na hechaib.
Is andsin tra roast Toas mac Iason Admeit, ri na Tesailli, intan roui ac dul secha, & ni thuc a brathair Eunios fortacht fair, uair rogresestar Ipodomus gasta gruadsolus a eochu etorru.
Tuc dono Cromis mac Ercail astod foreigni ar Ipodomus dar eis caich, comtis sinti a srianmirenda a ech, & co rabris a charpad.
Et o rabrisead amlaid sin carpad hIpodomuis, roimpaised a eich ris fochetoir da ithi, o robui 'na loigi, amal ba bes leo remIsin daine do ithi.
Et o 'dchondairc in trenfer calma Cromis sin, rotreic a buaid comretha, & roimpo d'indsaigid Ipodomuis, & roanaich e bar a echaib.
Tanic tra Apaill and sin d'fhortacht & d'fhoirithin do Ampiaraus do thobairt buada comlenga do.
Et is e ni doroni torathar firgrana feosach do deilb & do denam andsin ar lar inn aenaig, co ngebtais amaiti aduathmara ifirn grain & ecla reimi.
O 'tchondairc tra Areón anni sin, rogob aduath & urecla hi remi, cor-erig a mong co sesmach sirgarb osa gualaind, & co rothairring a carbad le & in n-ech ali bai fai, & co rothoit Polinices asin charpud co roibi bristi buaidirthi ar lar inn aenaich da n-eis.
Et robui-sium isin loigIsin cein co ndechaid carpat Impiarauis int sacairt, & carpad Ádmeit, ri na Teasailli, secha & lucht na comlenga ar chena.
Rothocaib-sium a chend co hanband eneirt asa haithli sin, & roerig do dechain na comlenga.
Is andsin roopair Ampiaraus imchosnum tosaich re Areón fuascrach firluath, ce ra-bi cen marcach fuirri, & rochomgres a eocho 'na diaid coma luaithigther re sidi nglasfuar ngaithi inn aimsir gairb gemrid a deini & a dedgairi.
Rocomlai 'na ndiaid co na roibi nech roime, & robo taisci andsin d'echaib Ampiaruis ina d'Arieón, mani gresed Nephtuin, dea in mara, in n-ech sin cor-ba le tosach na comlinga; & ger-ua taisci Arieón id_est ech Adraist andsin, ba coscrach Ampiaraus.
Tuc tra int ardri Adraist tairbert set & maine da Ampiaraus id_est dont sacart mor ar buaid na comlenga sin da breith id_est copan alaind orda asa n-ibead Earcail mac Ampitrionis fleada fina; & robatar andsin arna rindad delba na Ceandtuiri cosnomoch & na Lafitecda lanchalma & delb Marsisibiea rigan na Cichloiscthe o tuc Ercail na hairm ingantacha id_est cach ri dochid hi cind chatha, fuil rochuiread tara bel & dara sroin, tam & taisi, teiched & timi ticed dona sluagaib echtrand dos-cid ac cur chatha etorru fen: & delb na coscur comrumach dorigne Ercail archena sechnon in domuin.
Et tucad d'Admeit dono, da thaisech na Tesailli leand chaem corcorglan co nndelbaib imda arna n-ilecur d'orsnath inti.
Et o thuc Adraist na haisceda sin i comartha a choscuir don lucht sin, robui ac comdingnad a cleamna & tuc banchumail ndaeir do seic.
Et asa haithlIsin ronert Adraist drem dona sluagaib coisidib do chomling chomretha 'na fiadnaisi.
Rofrecrad esium iman ngnim sin.
Et roerig Idas re chach, & is amlaid robui & coroin coscuir comlenga ruc i sleb Olimp ima chend, & as iad ba sloig doson lucht Pisa & Eliis id_est na cathrach sin.
Roerig immorro 'na diaid sin Alchon croda coscurach a Sitsion.
Roerig 'na diaid sin Pedemus.
Ba coscrach comretha fa dó in fer sin i traig Ismis.
Roerich Dímás ar na cintis eich i comreathaib intan ba hoc, acht chena fa foraesta andsin he.
Roerig dono Parthanapeus no Parthanap, rig na hArcaidi, & ua subach sluaig in aenaig risin ngilla sin, & ua dual am deigrith don fir sin o mathair id_est o Athalannta; & ba do luth and fhir sin brith arna halltaib diana deigretha ar luas & ar lanrith; & int urchur focherded riam remi, conclised ara chind riasiu roshoithead talmain.
Et is andsin rothaithmig int siblaind n-alaind n-orda robui isin brut caem corrtharach, & rochuir de he, & roforruamnad corp daithgel deigdenmach in deglaich a hola; & roforruamnad dono Idas & Dimas ban samla cetna, & ba he Idas ba derrscaigthi delb isin chomling sin acht Partarnapeus a aenur, & ba sine Idas ina Parthanapeus.
Rouadar tra na fir sin ac fromad a luith resiu donetis a comling, & o racoraiged comartha in chomretha accu, roreithset ua chomaird chomluith no cor-scuch cach secha araili dib, & rochosain Parthanapeus tosach dib uili 'sinn uair sin, & ba luaithither re sidi ngaithi ngemreta in tethad & in tennad ruc o chach.
Et is e ua nesu do Idas athlom aduathmar, Pedimus & Dimas 'na ndiaid seic, & ua gairit etorru.
Ua hathlum, immorro, Alcon 'na ndiaid na fer sin.
Is amlaid tra robui Parthanapeus andsin & a fholt dualach dearrscaigthech scailti dara formna siar sechtair, & o raairig Idós cend na comlenga i comfhacus do, & Parthanapeus ac dul uad chuici, is e ni doronni, rosin in laim, & rogob ar bun inn fhoilt fhada findbuidIsin he, & rotrascair chuici dar ais.
O 'tchondcadar, immorro, na hArcaidi sin, roergedar d'indsaigi Idais da airlech, & raergedar sluaig Pisa & Elis dia frithaileam sideic, & is de sin fa mescbuaidirthi int aenach, & rotriallsad int aenach uili do buaidred co mor.
Et o 'tchualaig Adraist, int ardri, sin, roerig do thairmesc in tachair, & is ed roraid:
‘Traethar bar ferga, a firu,’ ar se, ‘& caiscid bar comruc, & dentar in comrith aris, & na lecar i comfhacus sib.
Na tuca nech uaib celc 'ma cheli.’
Dorondud tra leo-sium sin, & tuc Parthanapeus buaid na comlenga les in darna fecht, & ba samulta na taidled in talmain ara luas dorethad.
O rascuired sin, rotidnaiced seoid & maine doib log a mbuada id_est ech aibind do Parthanapeus, & sciath alaind aelgel do Idas saeigti, & saiged do chach ar cheana.
Et asa haithlIsin rocomtriallad leo cluichi disci do denum id_est cluichi méisi.
Et is amlaid donithea in cluichi sin, mias adbulmor iaraind no umaidi ar uaitnedaib iaraind 'na lamaib, & a himpod ima cuairt & a dibrucud i clethi aeoir & firmaminti; & mina frithailtea aris uar ind n-uaitni cetna, romarbad & romudaiged cach aen robid fuithi.
Is andsin rogab Adraist lama ar Perelass im ergi dochum in cluichi sin.
Roerich tra & rochuir in mes co fersecha firard uada, & robadar Greic sel fada 'ca fegad.
Et is iad so roerig da frithaileam ar sin id_est dias a hAichis, & triur a hEfir, & oenfher a Pisa, & ua he in sechtmad fer Acharnam.
Roerig, immorro, asa haithli sin, Ipomedon gruadsolus & mias adbulmor aile ina laim, & is ed roraid:
‘A ocu,’ ar se, ‘gebid in meis moir-sea in bar lamaib, uair is mo is feidmnert a tocbail & a tuirnem inna ni triallaid, & bid rethi togla ar tothocht don chathraig co saigthi id_est don Teib.’
Et rodibraig asa haithlIsin & nir-an ga hurnaidi aroen risna Grecaib acht mad Flegias & Menestius a hAchain, uair ba hecail leo tuindseom & truma na mesIsin ara met.
Et arae rofrithail Flegias calma comrumach 'na diaid sin in mes.
Raroith in meis & rochuir a n-aird i co nar-ba ler iter na nellaib frasacha firmora na firmaminti i ara hardi rochuir, co roseol anuas iar sin dochum thalman co domuin inti.
Et robadar Greic ac molad in gillIsin co mor isinn uair sin.
Et rotriall aris in fer sin a dibrucud, & ni riacht les; uair rothoit uad hi cen chummus gan cetugud do.
Roerig Menestius ar sin & rodibraic co hathlum & co hard hi.
Ipomodon immorro rogob ar sin hi; & ba hairdi roathchuir uad ina gach duni riam romi.
Et o thairnic in cluichi sin, tucad crocend taidlech tigri & cimas do dergor fair 'na thimchell do Impomedon, & tucad boga garbchuar Gnoisecda do Menestius: tucad dano claideb lethan langer ac Pilasceius ac senathair Adraist do Plieigias, luag a cluichi mesi.
Et ni ba setrech do chomorad cluichi chest na curaid isan uair sin, cein mata Capaneus, robui 'na stuaig bodba aduathmair urbada, aca iarraid bar na sluagaib nech dib d'ergi 'na agaid, & a lamanda tarbda tachair ima lamaib, co n-iallaib rofhada a cennaib a mer, co mellaib lantroma luaidi uara cendaib seic.
Et is ed roraid:
‘Ticed oenloech uaib, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘am agaid don cluichi cest, & robod maith lim co mad threnfer do Tiauandaib tisad and, uair rofaethsad limsa he isinn uair-sea.’
Ba socht mor re Grecaib sin, & rogob urecla adbul iad remi, & gid ead doerich loech lanoc do Lacondaib da indsaigid id_est Alacidamas.
Ba machtad tra re Grecaib ergi do, uair ba hoc arai n-aisi, ger-ua athlom n-engnoma; & ba he Pullux ua haeiti engnoma & cluichi cest don gilla sin.
O 'dchondairc Capaneus cuci he, roches air co mor, & robai ac faithfed & ac fochuidmed immi & ac iarraidh fhir aili maraen ris 'na agaid.
Ni ar timi na ar teichead dochuaid d'Alcidamas sin; acht rocomfergaid co fersech & co fircruaidh in n-agaid Capeneuis, co rothocbadar na lama lanchalma amal saeignena suaichinti solusda do chomamus cuirp araili.
Ba hecalma re Grecaib bas d'fhagbail don maccaem d'Alcidamas andsin, uair ua hadbul met & miri in miled robai ina agaid id_est Capaneus, uair nir commor coraid ar talmain risin trenfer sin.
Robai tra Alcidamas co feithmech firglicc aca fhrithalam.
Roopair-sium immorro co hacgarb & co hanacarach in maccoem, & rus-timchill amal timchillis feith fidu, no amal timchillis tond mara moradbail cairrgi cuain & calaid.
Rofhreastail & rofhrithoil Alcidamas sin, & ni teiged bem i ndilsi na i ndilmaine uad gan a buain do Chapaneus i cleithi i chind & dar tulport a gnuisi co ma forderg fuilidi a fholt & a aiged.
Is andsin rodasachtaiged im Capaneus amal leoman londletarthi, & rogob ac toirnim & ac trascrad Alciadamais o brathbuilleadaib mora mileta.
Ba dímain am dosom sin, uair roimdeagail Alcidiamas he co na ruacht lot no lanbrised fair; & rouadar amlaid sin re re ciana co rothuitset ara ngluinib caema comfillti re scis a n-imbuailti.
Et gid ed roerich cach dib aris dochum a cheli, & ag ergi doib, tuc Alcidamas bem ceisti do Chapaneus co torchair & cleithi a chendmullaich remi chum lair & lantalman, & ag eri do, roathbnail aris he co runuallsad na sluaig ac aicsin in gnima sin.
Roaitherig immorro Capaneus co hacarb aduathmar da digail sin ar Alcidamas.
Et o 'tothondairc Adraist anni sin, is ed roraid:
‘A fhiru,’ ar se, ‘ederdelaigter lib na milid rasu rafaeth nechtar dib re 'roili inn ecomlaind, & tabar lib seoit & maine da Capaneus do thairmesc a fergi.’
Roergedar andsin da ndegail Tid & Ipomedon.
Ua doilig am eterscarad na desIsin re med na fergi firmoiri roforbair intib, & roraidsed-sium re Capaneus:
‘Tairind t'fheirg,’ ar siad, ‘a ri, & tabair maithem n-anocail uaid don gilla oc-sa, uair is lindi luamaireacht in laich-sea.’
Nir-fhaem thra Capaneus, & is ed roraid:
‘A firu,’ ar se, ‘cindus leicfet uaim in gilla n-oc, roimir imned & edualand orum, gan a mordigail air?’
Et gid ed rucsad a muinter leo he, & rodeligsed iad amlaid sin, & rouadar munter Alcidamais ac genaib gaeire im Capaneus.
Et o thairnic in cluichi sin, roerig Tit mac Oeniusa & rofuacair caraigecht & comglic andsin uar na sluagaib.
Et is e roerig da indsaigid Agileus mac Ercail, & ba medithir re hArcail mac Amphitrionis ar met & ar mesnig in milid sin, uair ba da síl do.
Tid, immorro, is amlaid robui seic, fer isel tailc tarbda tren calma athlom ocla anacarach.
Ua tren & ua tarcaisnech ar gach n-oen tecmad ris.
Et rogobad ola chomshlemuin cumascda da churp isinn uair sin, & roerig dochum Agileus.
Is andsin roiad cach dib a lama & a rigthi dar araili, co ma samalta re seolchrand primluingi moiri no re ralaig roaird os mincrandaib firbeca fidbaidi Ageleius os cind Tit andsin aca thairnim & 'ga trascrad.
Et ger ua lugu Tit, ua tendi & ua talchairi e isinn uair sin, co rotimsaig & co rothimairg Ageleius, & co rotrascair dochum lair & lantalman.
Rocengail & rocuibrig 'na diaid sin i fiadnaisi na n-Grec uile he, & tucaid aisceada a comartha a choscair do arsin.
Robui ac braisi & ac bocasaich uasa cind, & tuc da muntir iad; & ar n-ergi do Agilleius co hoband mertnech asa chengal, tuc Adraist luirig n-imthruim n-iaraind do log a chluichi do chommorad.
Et asa haithlIsin roergedar dias dib do cluichi d'armaib aithgera urnochta id_est Agresius mac sic Epidaur, & Polinices mac Eidip.
Rothairmisc immorro int airdri Adraist iad, & is ed roraid:
‘Na denaid cathugud, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘cein no co ros-ti tachur na Tebi, uair dogebthai uar ndaithin cathaigthi & comlaind inti.’
Et rothairmisced iad amlaid sin.
Is andsin adubradar airig na n-Grec risin n-airdrig re hAdraist a chuid dona cluichib do denam comad moidi onoir ind n-adnocail.
‘Dogentar,’ ar se, & roerig.
Is e ni doronni, rodibraic saigid a fidbaic ibraide co setrech sirchalma co ndechaid uad re hed, & amal ba tresi di ac dul, roimpo co hathlum opund ar culu d'indsaigid in rig rus-telg.
Et ba fidgrad faistine acu-sum sin, uair is ed rothuiced asa sin Adraist a oenur do ternum a cathugud na Tebi & a rochtain ar culu co crichaib Grec.
Conid cainiud Airsemaris & a cluicheda cainteacha conigi sin.
O tarnic tra in cluichi caintecha sin, rodoirt Adraist fin aran adnocol, & robui ac molad in gilla amal dea uasal adartha, & is ed roraid:
‘A mic,’ ar se, ‘dogentar amal so idbarta ac Grecaib uili gacha bliadna duid-seo, & da taet lindi tigi na Tebi tret chumachta-su, bidid mo honoir idbarta aris acaindi.’
Et is ed sin ba hail do Grecaib uili da rad.
As i sin, immorro, aes & uair dobi imshnim mor ar menmain Ioib mic Satuirn, uair ua fada les-sum comnaidi na n-Grec i n-ingnais in chatha, & is andsin tucad a mac id_est Mearcuir dochum Ioib, & is ed roraid ris:
‘Erig,’ ar se, ‘d' indsaigid Mairt, dea in chatha, & abair risna Greic d'adandad dochum in catha.’
Et roerig Mercuir & dosiacht co tigib seselbacha Mairt, mic Ioib, dea na cath & na congal, & raid ris na Greic & na Tiabanda do chur a cend a chele.
Roerig tra Mairt lasin ngresacht sin, & tanic remi dar trachtaib traga Eipir co mullach slebi Acorintus iter in muir n-Iond iar n-airthiur & muir n-Eig ar n-iarthur.
Roscail uad andsin ecla & aduath, ferg & fuasnad ba sluagaib Grec, co rolingsedar menmanda risin fogur bres adchualadar i firmamint uasa cind & risin scel n-aduathmar n-urbadach sin.
Et rocraith a slega & a sceith, & rotrenbuail a eocho uas cind na sluag, cor-gab saínt & ailgius catha & comlaind na curaid isinn uair sin risin ngresacht & risin laidiud sin tuc Mairt mac Ioib forru.
O 'tchondairc, immorro, Baich mac Ioib, dei inn fhina, na Greic 'na mbuidnib degshluaig ac comlugud dochum na Tebei, tucad iachtad & osnaid mor os aird, & tainic remi d'indsaig a athar id_est Ioib, & roloig ina fhiadnaisi, & dabui ac iarraid fortachta dona Tiabandaib air, & is ed roraid:
‘Is olc a ndenaid,’ ar se, ‘a Ioib comorad catha i cend na Tiauanda & a tir do thogail forru, & doberi-siu do gach dei aili comairci in chiniuda is dual dó & ni thabraid damsa.
Uair is i Simile, ingen rig na Tebi, mo mathair, & dafhetar is i Iunaind ilcrothach dobeir ortsu in aimleas arin fath sin.’
O 'tchualaigh Ioib sin rotib a gin ngairi 'ma mac, & rothairbir poicc do, & adbert ris:
‘A mic,’ ar se, ‘ni fich na ferg dobeir orum comorad in chatha-sa.
Acht is ed ro-chindsead faidi & fisid o thus domuin co cuirfithea in cath croda-sa na Tebi.
Et na bid ecla ortsu, a Baich, togail na Tebi don chur-sa, & amae dlestis a n-olc do denam, uair is adbul a n-ecoiri.’
Ba forbailid Baich dona scelaib sin.
A ndala-sum coruigi sin.
Dala, immorro, na Tiauanda, ranic techtairi tairisi da muntir co hEcliocles, co rig na Tebi, & roindis do rigrad na n-Grec cona sluagaib & cona sochraitib i comfhocus do muigib tondglasa na Tebi.
Ba truag immorro & ba tindesnach risna Tiauandaib, in gach inad a robadar, na scela aidblIsin do chloisteacht.
Is andsin tra rothinoilit dochum Ethiocleis a sluaig & a sochraidi & a shuind chatha & a fhuird irgaili co faichthi fondglais a duin & a cathrach.
Tochestul & tinol na Tiabanda andso.
Et desid andsin cach drem degsluaig 'ma triath & 'ma thigerna do neoch thanic a hEonia & a hEobia & a Pótcis & a cathrachaib na Tiauanda ar cheana.
Roergetar immorro, mna & macaim & mindaine, & rolinsadar muir na cathrach & dumacha aili airechtais ac fegad int shluaig sin.
Is and dono robui inn og ilchrothach id_est Antigone, deirbfiur Etiocles & Polinices, i tur roard romor sel o mur na cathrach sin amach.
Uair is ed ba bes acusum gan sluaig & gan sochaidi da fhaiscin a n-ingen, no co faeitis re feraib.
Et ba ler disi andsin tochim na sluag uaithi uar in faichthi, & ni ba ler daibsium isi.
Et as e robi 'na farrad andsin Phorfas foirfi fireolach id_est fer grada a hathar & a sseanathar eseom, & a hoiti.
Et rogob-si 'ga fhiarfaigi de:
‘Cia in sluag romor-sa iter?’ arsi, ‘& atchimsea,’ ar si, ‘mergeda minglana Meinidceus corcargloin & airm croda Creoin coscraig.’
Rofhrecair, immorro, Porfas disi & is ed roraid:
‘In faicend tu and,’ ar se, ‘Drías a tulchaib taebuara Tanacra atuaid on uarda & mili saegdech 'na farrad?
Et in faicend tu ua do Nephtuin and & delb aeil ara armaib?
Atat and sud i sochraidi Ethiocleis curaid na cathrach Ochalia, & milid mera Medona, & gaiscedaig nuaglana Nísa, & trenfhir thalchara Thispé agruin.
Et is e is nesu doibsin Eurimedon croda coscorach mac Fanuuis, dea na caillted, & is e fhoires & airchises cach gabad coilled, & sluaig saidbri sonaidi Erithra maraen ris, & na sluaig tangadar a Colon ciuitas & a hEtanion agruin, & a hEleis ciuitas, & a Scíroin agruin, & gae gera guinecha & sceith cruindi cabracha leo sin.
Et ata and dono airechta Anchesta agruin do sil Nephtuin dei in mara & is e Neptuin garbas & fethnaiges in muir n-aduar n-ainfenach.
Et atait and na fir bit a Megalis i cocrich na Greci & na Tiauanda & ba sruth Melais & ba thobar n-Gargais id_est tobar mirbulta, & ba sruth Alietis.
Tamuin chruaidi chendtroma ba hairm daib sin, & craicind langarba leoman ba cathbairr 'ma cendaib, & cliatha cruaidi cranda ba sceith daib.
Et atat aireachta slebe Elicona o sruth o Parmessus id_est sruth ata ac sliab Ailip i tuaiscert na Tiauanda & o sruth Armeus.
Et ua cruitireda ceolbindi na curaid sin uili o na Moyisib id_est dei in bindisa.’
Et o raraid Porfas na briathra sin, & tuc na tuarascbala sin arna sluagaib, rolobair Antigone, & is ed roraid:
