‘Is mor am,’ arsi, ‘cosmailius na desIsin derbrathar ut adciam uaind iter na sluagaib; uair is at caema comarda iter arm & etach.
Et ropad maith lim,’ ar si, ‘da mad it e adam derbrathair fein dobeth in cumand ut.’
‘A ingen am,’ ar Porfas, ‘ni tusu cetduine roraid sin riu, uair is sochaide adubart riu connod brathair iad cen go bed.
Uair is e a athair in dara fir dib araili, & as amlaid doronad sin:
Nipe bean do Laiftecdaib rochomruic re maccaem n-og id_est Lapitus a ainm, & nir-comraic re mnai riam roimi, & do na tainic d'aes a denam.
Et ba hingnam comperta di, & darala Alatrius di don toirrches sin, & o ratuismed in mac sin ba gairit coma comor comdelba re athair he.
Et as iad in dias ud romothaigis-siu, in mac sin, & int athair id_est Lafitus & Altrius a mac & tri chet marcach sochraidi cach fhir dib isin tinol-sa a Clissanta & a Coriona.
Ata dono and Ipseius mac Assopas ri thuathtuaiscert na Tiabanda, & carpat caem ceith irriada fae, & sciath suairc sarcengailti do sechedaib glaeta gloleathair ara muin, & luireach trebraid trefhillti 'ma corp, & gae remur rofhata do na tabair urchur d'imroll ina laim.
Et ata sochraidi mor maraen ris sin do neoch thanic a hIton & a hAcamena a Midae fesand mor & a hAulis a Grea & a Plathea & a hAndtegon & mill lanmora luaidi rodibraicdis a tulaib trenamais na fir sin & nim tualaing-sea tra,’ ar se, ‘aireom ina tanic sund do slogaib athloma examla a hilchathrachaib na Tiauanda aróen re hIpitus n-arnaid n-aduathmar mac Naupulus id_est urri na cathrach medonda na Tiauanda.
Et imscith mo roisc, & rocomleath ceo crini thairsib ac tuream na slog, & nim tualaing a n-indsin ni as mo, a ingen,’ ar se.
Asa haithlIsin roerig Ethiocles, rig na Tebi, ar mur a chathrach d'acallaim a sluaig & a sochraidi, & is ed roraid riu:
‘A rigu maithi mormenmnacha,’ ar se, ‘ni misi tendas na tindesnaiges sib dochum in chathaigthi-sea, acht bar mbaid & bar mbeodacht fen, & bidam cubaid-sea dono lib ac cosnum uar cathrach & uar tiri.’
Et is amlaid robui 'ga rad sin, & tuc achmosana imda da brathair id_est do Polinices, mar nabeth ina fiadnaisi, & roordaich lucht a cometa ac din & ac diten na cathrach & ac gabail in muir.
Roordaich curadu croda re cathugud inn agaid gaiscedach Grec amuich an-echtair.
Dala na Tiauannda conigi sin.
Dala immorro na n-Grecs rochomergedar reompo can suan can sadaili i llo na a n-aidchi.
Et ger-ua imda derbairdeda doirrthi & figrad firuilc daib, ni rothoirmisc iad, & fa moidi fich fergi na firloech gach celmaine condtrachta dachuiread daib, no go rangadar co sruth siralaind sribuaine Assopus i tir na Tiauannda.
Roansad-sum gan dul tairis sin fo chetoir, uair ba hadbul a thuili & a thondgar int shrotha inn uair sin ar cur breachta druad do Baich fair id_est do dea inn fhina.
Is andsin tanic Ipamedon feochair fergach, & rogres a eochu isin n-ath resna sluagaib, & roraid riu:
‘Is metacht & is midlochus daib, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘gan dul dar in sruth, & ni bud maith do thogail na Tebi trenarmaigi a triall amlaid sin.’
Roergedarsum co dian denmnedach lasin ngresacht sin, & dachuadar dar in sruth, no co rangadar co tulaich taebalaind taitnemaich, & rochidis-sium uaithib asin tulaig sin tigi arda airegda & faicheda fondglasa firailli na Tebi togaidi.
Rogabad leosum andsin longphort lethan lanadbal, & robadar and re head na haidchi sin.
Ua doilig tra a fhis & a haisnes crith & comegla, sestan & sirsibul na Tianannda isinn aidchi sin, o 'tchondcadar pupuill aladbreca fhairsingi, & airm saiti sesmacha gaiscedach n-Grec re doirrsib a mbrecpupall ar ngabail a longphuirt doib.
Robui tra do met a n-ecla na ba' tairisi leo din na daingen da roibi accu isinn aidchi sin.
tra acht roscailid badba buaidirthi belderga, & demna aduathmara ifirn ua cheachtar in da sluag isinn aidchIsin do commorad uilc & anindi chaich dib re chele. O raergedar tra renna roglana roailli in lae arnamarach, roerig Iochasta, in rigan laimgel gruadsolus id_est mathair Ethiocleis, rig na Teibi, & Poliniceis, fhirthogla na cathrach, & a da hingin maraen ria id_est Ismine & Ántigone.
Ba foraesta forbthi am in rigan thanic andsin, & o rasiacht ar larmedon in longphuirt, tuc a faidi fergacha firguil os aird, & roraid:
‘A rigraid Grec,’ ar si, ‘cait a fuil mo mac-sa i trasta andso id_est Polinices?’
O 'tchualaich immorro in gilla a beith-si 'ga iarraid amlaid sin, tanic da hindsaigid, & robui 'ga cendsugud do briathraib suarca sithamla.
Rofhrecair-si dosum, & is ed roraid ris:
‘A mic,’ ar si, ‘is ead is maith lim sith suthain do bith etorrud-su & do brathair, & fiarchairi chairdisa re Tiauandaib; & tair limsa anund isin Teib, & dena sith ret brathair, & cuindig rigi da deoin air, & mina thuca dit i, is coraidi dit cathugud croda 'na agaid.’
Tanic tra cridi na n-Grec co mor andsin ar Iochasta, amal robui ac eterdeligud a mic on chathugud Tiauanda.
Rotriall tra Polinices dul le-si isin baili, & nir-thairmisc Adraist imi a dul, cein co tanic Tit mac Oeniusa & co n-ebairt:
‘Na dentar in sid,’ ar se, ‘no co tarar-sa arna Tiauandaib crechta mo chnis & mo chuirp,’ & rothocaib a chrechta & a ilgona dona sluagaib andsin.
Rothairmisc tra in scel sin fa Polinices dul isin cathraig & gan sid re brathair, & rolinsad na Greic uili o feargaib glemorgarba risna Tiauandaib, o 'dchondcadar crechta & ilgona Thid.
Is Isin aes & uair tangadar amach na tigri robitis ac imarchur charbaid Baich mic Ioib d'ol uisci co srothaib firuara firglana na Tebi; & in am dochuadar, dorala doib ara Ampiamrauis int sacairt moir Grecaig, & se ac lecun usci da echaib.
Rolingestar air na tigri diana dasachtacha fo chetoir id_est cenela anmidead erchoideacha marbas cethra & daine na tigri, & romarbsad fo chetoir int ara & na heochu, & romarbsad dono dias aili do Grecaib id_est Idas & Athamant a n-anmanda.
Et asa haithlIsin adchondairc Acondteus Arcadecda na tigri id_est taiseach morthuaithi do lucht na hArcaidi, & is 'na fherand ata in cloch bis ar lassad trebithu id_est Sifist a hainm, a haithli na n-echt sin do denam daib.
Et rodibraic da saigid a ndiaid aroili da n-indsaigi co rotregdastair a craideada & co rucsad na soigti leo isin mbaile & conid thall fuaridar bas.
Ba trom & ba torrsech re Tiauandaib in gnim sin, & roerig amach fer do muntir Baich da ndigail id_est Flegius a ainm, & rosiacht cen fhis, no co tuc bem claideb do Accondteus co torchair marb cen anmain.
Roergedar immorro na hArcaidi da digail sin, & ni riacht leo, uair ranic Flegius imslan isin cathraig ar ndigail enig Baich amuich.
A haithli in gnima sin, immorro, roas seastan & seselb adbulmor i llongphort lanlethan na n-Grec, & roraid Tit, mac Oenius, re hIochasta, & re hingenaib:
‘Denaid imthecht,’ ar se, ‘& ni berthai sid na osud lib don chur-sa.’
Roimthig Iochasta co dubach domenmach ar sin ar femed sida iter a macaib.
Roerig immorro Tid in milid croda coscoroch calma mac Oenius, & rogab a armu, & rocomgres a munter & slog na n-Grec ar-chena.
Dorindead tra andsin comergi croda curata & sitharchar tindisnach cur-ua cumascda combuaidirthi iter chairpthib & curadaib in longphuirt isinn uair sin.
Et robui da deni roergedar connar-leced tosach na toisigeacht da stocaib croda cathaigthi na da mergedaib suarca srollaigi acht a ndirmanda diana daescurshluaig & a ngeraiti gaiscid ac imchosnam gliad & ag iarraid irgaili dochum na Tiauanda.
Roergedar immorro da frestal & da frithaileam trenfhir tenda tairgsenacha talchara na Tebi, & rogob gach triath & gach tigerna dib ac gresacht & ar nertad a mormuntiri.
Is andsin tra rotrenindsaich cach aroile dib co ma samalta gredon & glorbresmaidm na mbuiden mbodba mbuaidirthIsin ac comrith ri aroili amal bad i ind fhidbad bresbraenach billeach barrglas rothuited i ladraib glac & i llamaib aroili re gaidsnim na gaithi garbfuairi gemreta, no mar bad he in la bratha brigurduirc brecdhuileach tisad do smurchaicilt in betha, & robris cach airech & gach airdri bernd rena buidin i cath aroili an uair sin.
Et mar dabadar isin comfheidm catha sin na sluaig ceachtarda, is and rofuataig a each rot romer trenfer do Tiauandaib le i cath na n-Grec id_est Terelas.
Et rofrithail Tid mac Oenius he, & tuc fuirmed fedma co setrech sirchalma do gae robui 'na laim air, cor-ua bir bodba trena chorp don churaid, & rouc a ech aris ar cula e, cor-ap and rothoit gan anmain iter na Tiauannda.
Rotrenindsaig tra na catha croda araili ar toitim an fhir sin co fergach firamnas, & rodluthaiged in chathirgal comrumach cor-ba dluithither re cleith lenad arna landluthud in lini sleg semnech sithfhata rosuidiged a sleasaib suarca saercland sochenelach andsin isin tres trenadbul sin rochuirsetar.
tra acht rodithaigit dronga de sin, & romaeltamnaigit meidi, & robanaid gnuisi, & roruamnaigit roisc, & roclaeit cetfada curad ac comthoitim. Et ar sin dorala in cath ina comracaib.
Rocomraic and Ipamedon ard allata do Grecaib & Siuaris siruallach do Thiauandaib; & i forcindiud in comraic sin, darochair Siuaris and do laim in Grecaig.
Rocomraicsedar asa haithlIsin da trenfer do Tiauandaib id_est Pilius & Perefans re hengaiscedaig do Grecaib id_est Menceius & dothoitsed na Tiauanda don tachur sin, & ruc Menceius a coscor & a comaidem.
Acus dorigne Partapeus ri na hArcaide ar sin echta ar na Tiauanda, & rothoit in triur-sa dib les id_est Ithis & Sibaris & Perefans.
Dothoit Cunesius gaisgedach do Grecaib re hEmon echtach mac Creoin do Tiauandaib; & ac toitim do, rogab Abas do Tiabandaib airm inn fhir sin, & rofocair comruc da eis; & tarlaic fer do Grecaib saigit do, co rus-facaib gan anmain.
Roerig ar sin sacart do muntir Baich id_est Euneius, & a edach delradach dathalaind imi asa ndenad idbarta do Baich; & tuc tainsem & tarcaisi mor arna Grecaib uili, & is ed roraid:
‘Na cuirid risna Tiabandaib, a Grecu,’ ar se, ‘uair is croda a curaid & is cumachta a ndei & is daingin muir a morcathrach.’
Et o 'dchualaig, immorro, in ri londmer gaisceadmer do Grecaib id_est Capaneus, rofhrithail he, & tanic ar cind conairi do inna stuaig agmair aduathmair, & roboccbertaich in sleig rindger rofada co crund caem comdiriuch do fid chuanda cuibrisc indti, & roraid:
‘Is baeth banda,’ ar se, ‘na briathra bocasaich raidi risna slogaib.
Et dursan nach e in dei da n-adraid ita id richt adrasta: uair da mad he, rofaethsad limsa.’
Et is cuma roraid-seom sin & tuc urchar n-indill diruch dochum Euneiuis, co roscailt a sciath.
co robris a druim, co riacht a marb dochum talman ua chetoir.
Is andsin rofhopair Ethiocles ri na Tiabanda ara & ilechta aidbli ar gasradaib Grec co ma dronga dianmarba les iad cach conair ina teged.
Polinices immorro tuc sec accarda & anucul dona Tiabandaib arin fialchairi mbunaid & ar grad na hatharrda dilisi duthaig.
Is andsin rofobair Ampiaraus int uasalsacart do Grecaib calma do denum, & rogres a eochu ana athloma co talchar tindisnach coma luaithred lanmin in roe croda comraic da eis cach conair concinget in cairpthech sin.
Et ba delradach dathalaind isinn uair sin amail renna rosollsi taitnem a cathbairr caim cumaidi & a sceith cuanda capradaig iter na cathaib ceachtarda, & imasae fa na sluagaib comma tregdaithi toitmithi trenfhir tenda Thiabanda fo armaib cach conair ina slaiged in sluag.
Et is andsin rocomraic dosum ar lar in chatha & Flegias feochair firgarg do Tiabandaib, & rochuirset comlond croda curata re hed & re hathaig, co rocreachtnaig cach aroili dib; & i forciund in comruic dorochair Flegias do laim ind arsid Ampiarauis.
Doriacht ar sin chuici fer dian diumsach aili do Thiabandaib id_est Pileius, & rochuirset na curaid cruaidirgal eturru, & rothoit in Tiabanda don gleo sin.
Asa haithlIsin robeansad ris in dana curaid croda comromacha don chiniud cetna id_est Cromis & Emetá; & rofuaibredar ar sin Ampiaraus co hainmin & co hacarb.
Acht ceana ba daibsium tiugbas tiugba in tachair sin, uair rothoitsed do gonaib amainse aicbeli Ampiarauis.
Atchondcadar sin triar talchar trenfher do Tiabandaib.
Roluathindsaigsed ar Ampiaraus do digail na sarecht sin air id_est Ipinorus & Ságis & Giian glondmer gaiscedach.
Et frecrais & frithailis int arnaid Ampiaraus iat o brathbuillib mera mileta comtis fadba fiarletairthe cuirp chaema chnesgela na curad comramach ua chrolindtib fola fichithi forruaidi da eis.
Et ar na toitim leis, rofobair Alchatous Tiabanda a n-irgail air, & rofhrithail-sium he, & tarraid cloich cruaid comamais, & tarlaic urchur do Alchatonus, cor-bean i cleithi i cendmullaig, co torcair can anmain.
Adchondairc ri sotal sarechtach do Tiauandaib int echt sin id_est Ipseus mac Assapos, & ba trom & ba trengalar les na hára acgarba aidbli dorad Ampiaraus ar na slogaib, & nir-ael fulang do gan a digail air, gen gor-thais da eneoch amal robui fen ac slaigi gasraidi Grec.
Et o rocomraicedar in da curaid croda sin, rogab cach dib ac tarcasni & ac tomaithium uar aroili.
O 'dchondairc tra Apaill dea na faistine sin, tuc urchar da ga don araid robui i carbat Ampiarauis id_est Alegmon, co rothoit gan anmain asa carbud amach, & tanic fen 'na inad, & rogob deilb inn arad fair, & ruc les na heocha & in carpad ar imgabail Ipseuis.
Et robui Apaill andsin ac setugud carpait Ampiarauis, & ac dirgud a urchur, & ac certugud a ech, cona tabrad in fer sin fasbuilli no urchur cen amus.
Rodidned dono he cona echaib ar urcharaib aicbeli a bidbad.
Is andsin roiadsat in cethrar curad-sa do Tiabandaib im Ampiaraus id_est in cosidi mer mordalach Meneleus, & in marcach ard allata Antipus, & int arsich engnuma Accíon, & in laech londmer Lapus.
Rocomgres Apaill eochu Ampiarauis i cend na curad sin co dian & co dasachtach, & roimir cles carpait furru, con torchradar ua chosaib na n-ech, co nderna comach & combrud da cnamaib fa chorraib in charbaid, & co fuaridar bas.
tra acht ba tairmesc erma & imtechta dona hechaib sin Ampiarauis, co na roictis a cosa comgabail in talman re himad na corp cnesgel curad letarthi & na sleg sesmach sirshaiti a sechnachaib na saerchland cor-ba comderg uili a eich & a charpat o braenaib fola falcmara forruaidi i taebaib trenmilead togaidi. Roben immorro Apaill andsin a deilb ndruidechta de, & dachuaid 'na richt fen, & rolobair re hAmpiaraus, & is ed roraid:
‘Is i seo,’ ar se, ‘crich & cindiud do shaegail, & ni edaim-sea t'imdegail ni as sia, & merdait do scela & do chlu co forcend saegail & co deread n-aimsiri, & erig i muigib aduathmara ifirn, amal rocinded dit; uair is ferr duid ina beth can adbaid n-adnocail i tir na Tebi togaidi.’
Rofhrecair Ampiaraus do-sum, & is ed roraid:
‘A uasail, a Apaill,’ ar se, ‘roairigis tu isin carpud im arrad, & is fir a n-abraid; uair adcluinim-sea fen srotha granna garbfuara ifirn ara trethan & ara tondgail acim iarraid, & adcluinim dono Cerber craessoslaici, cu Oirc, doirrseoir imnedach ifirn, acom amastraig & aeom gairm, & ber-siu let na coroni coserctha atat 'mam chend, uair ni dlegar a mbreth a n-ifirn.’
Roerich immorro Apaill uad-sum asa haithli sin, & rofhacaib e, & o dachuaid uad, tuc Ampiaraus a chnedchurad os aird re hecla ind etualaing.
Et is andsin tanic trethan & talamchumscugud mor isin talmain a rabadar, co roerig a luaithred & a langainem cor-ua ceo comdluith cumascda i timchell na sluag.
Et rocomerig torand tren mortolgach ar sin co rochuibrig & co rochengail na catha ceachtarda nar-ba tualaing duine dib ursclaigi na himbualad isinn uair sin, acht rouadar 'na sesam & cranda a sleg cosaiti re n-ochtaib.
Et o rabadar-som amlaid sin co tai tostach re hecla in bresmadmanda bratha buaidirthe, adchualadar rodianscailed in talman in tan sin, comma hall firdomuin fudomanta forba na faichthi fondglaisi ara rabadar, & rooslaic in talam & rosluic Ampiaraus trenadbal cona armaib & cona erred & cona echaib & cona charpad, no co ranic co hichtur ifirn n-aduair cen cheim ar cula.
O rasiacht immorro Ampiaraus i n-ifirn, rogob grain & ecla airechta aduathmara ifirn remi; uair nir-ba haithnid daib, connicIsin milid gan marbad na heich na carbaid do rochtain chucu.
Et tuc Oirc, ri ifirn, athais mor ar deib nuaglana nime 'man fer sin do lecud chuci, & dorigni spraic moir & tomaitheam adbul ar Ampiaraus badesin.
Rofhrecair Ampiaraus co hanband & co henirt dosum, & is ed roraid:
‘Toirind t'fheirg,’ ar se, ‘uair ni d'indred na d'argain ifirn tanac-sa, & ni tre m'olc fen tucad chucaib-si me, acht mo bancheli fen dam brath ar in muntorc oir do thobairt do Argia di id_est do mnai Poliniceis.
Et roailgius-sa me fen ar teiched thoigeachta do thogail Tebi; uair rofhedur co fuigbind m'aeided aici.
Et na bid a olc acid-su mo thoideacht-sa ille; uair dogentar cluicheada caintecha & adnocail onoracha dam ac Grecaib, & cuir-seo me a ngrianbrogaib ailli ifirn.’
Rocendsaiged tra aicned Oirc o 'tchualaich sin, & rofhaem gach ni roraid Ampiaraus.
Da rig dec do Tiabandaib romarb Ampiaraus in sacart id_est in fer tuaichill tuicsenach da thodochaide.
Imtusa na n-Grec, immorro, robadar ac iarraid Ampiarauis sechnon in chatha; uair nir-bo demin leo a aided inn fhir sin, & ba heclach iad resin tulmaidm talman adchondcatar ar lar in maigi i rabadar.
Et in am robadar amlaid sin, tanic Palemon taisech do Grecaib dochum Adraist, & roindis do aided Ampiarauis id_est a thoitim isin tulmaidm thalman, & gan a faicsin 'na diaid, & adbert:
‘A airdri,’ ar se, ‘facbum in tir n-aneoil n-urbudach-sa i tangamar, uair itat tulcha na Tebi ac slucad na slog, & atat a curaid 'gar commaideam, & a ndei 'gar mbrath & 'gar trecun.’
Roshocht Adraist ara n-ecein sin, & rochreid a chetoir sin, cein no co tangadar dias aile do muntir chuci id_est Mopsus & Actor, & cor-indiseadar ana cetna do cona thuilled & cona tormuch.
Et is don scel sin roimpotar catha croda na n-Grec dochum a longphort co teichech & co tindisnach gan chrich comlaind & gan rebchatha do corugud.
Ua scitha a n-eich & a n-araid, & bat mertnecha a milid, & ba toirsech a trenfhir a haithli na hirgailIsin ar-tuit Ampiaraus.
Dala na Tiabanda, immorro, ba subach sonairt rochingset, & tanic ind adaid fae sin.
Cetcath na Tebi sin.
Ba dubach domeanmnach tra rochaithseadar Greic in n-aidchIsin ina longphort, & ni head molad a n-ech na a n-engnuma fein dorindsed, acht comroma Ampiarauis & a gnimrada gaiscedacha d'indisin.
Et rochindsead sollamna saineamla & idbarta onoracha do denam do.
Et robadar snima & sirimshnima in chathaigthi co mor ara menmain daib na n-Grec, cein no co rortoit a suan & a sirchodlud orru.
Nir-ba hamlaid sin tra rochaithset na Tiabanda ind aidchi sin, acht robadar ac ol & ac aibnius & ac admolad a n-engnuma a n-aithrech & a senaithrech & ic idbartaib da ndeib uaisli adartha.
Et is Isin cetadaig indister Eidip mac Laiuis athair Ethiocleis & Poliniceis do tobairt a haithli a dalta d'ol & d'
aibnius dochum na Tiabanda, & indister connar-foilcead a fholt & conar-hindlad a aiged o radallad he co haes na fuairi-sea ar met na duba.
Et ni d'ol na d'aibnis dono tainic cucu isinn aidchi sin, acht do commorad in chatha iter na Tiabandaib & na Grecaib, & ba halaind in cleithi donid-som sin, & is amlaid sin robadar in lucht sin in aidchi sin.
Adraist, immorro, ardri Grec, ge rachadladar a shloig re hathscis na hirgaili, ni rachadail fen ac eistecht re gairib suba & somenman na Tiabanda isan aidci sin, & ba hadbul a imshnim leis-seom sin.
O thanic, immorro, la co lansoillsi arnabarach, dorigned condi & comairli ac Grecaib da ordugud cia norigfaidis i n-inad Ampiarauis, & dogenad faistine & fireolus d'aisneis dara eiss daib.
Is he tra rohordaiged leo 'na inad id_est in fisid fireolach id_est Tiodomos mac Melamfuis, & is e athair ind fhir sin Melamfus dorindi faistine aroen re hAmpiaraus do Grecaib re teacht ar in sluaiged sin.
Et o rahorned tra co honorach andsin Tiodomus i nn-inad Ampiarauis, roeirig co subach in sacart sin, & dorigned idbarta & admolta les a n-onoir na bande Terra id_est in talam ar bithin na dianscailed & na dluiged fo Grecaib amal dorigne ba Ampiaraus; & darondad dono leo idbarta & adnucul onorach & cluichi caintecha d'
Ampiaraus.
Et o thairnig sin, roerigetar badba belderga bruthmara & irdemna aduathmara ichtair ifirn co cathraig na Tiabanda da aslach & da furail forru comergi d'indsaigid na n-Grec.
Et is bec na rosrainit ass a sludraigib tigi na Tebi re trethan & re tindscedul na Tiabanda andsin ac comergi i nn-oenfecht dar secht ndoirrsib delithi arda uraibni na cathrach comdaingni re gresacht na mbadb mbuaidirthIsin oru.
Et is amlaid seo dochuadar amach id_est rogres Creon croda curata a buidin dar in dorus n-ard n-allata solusglan danad ainm Oegis; & tanic Ethiocles ardri na Tiabanda dar in dorus niamda n-alaind id_est Neistae.
Niam orda robai fair.
Tanic Emon airsid conna furrigaib dar dorus Emolois.
Chind leoman a comartha seic.
Roerig immorro Ipseius mac Asopas dar dorus primda Prodida.
Delba dregon dorindad and-seig.
Tanic Drias dasachtach id_est ri Tanagura on uarda oigretaig cona dirmaib deagsluaig dar dorus alaind Eleachtra.
Nathracha rofursannait andside.
Tanic Eurimedon cona muntir mormenmnaig dar dorus n-ilbrec danad ainm Ipsitas.
Delba loiscend batar andside.
Tanic dono in milid mormenmnach Menidcheus dar dorus ndaingen Dírse.
Delba buthfad badar andside.
Nir-ba suaill am inni ris ba samalta comergi int shluaig sin ac facbail na cathrach id_est re fuaim & re fothrand na fairrgi fondglaisi co crithnaig & co comgluais in cruindi comfhairsing re treathan na tond ac triall tar trachtaib in talman.
Dala na n-Grec, immorro, roergedar co malla mertnech dochum in chatha in la sin, & roiadsat andsin munter Ampiarauis im Tiodomas mac Melampas, co robe in sechtmad ri do Grecaib in la sin isin cath.
Is andsin roordaich gach ri dib sin a trein & a thaisich inna fiadnaisi fri comruc & cathugud dar a ceand.
Mairg am do Grecaib & do Tiabandaib da tanic in la sin, uair rofacbaid airechta gan urrigu dib, & tuatha cen taisechu, & baileda gen brugudu, & cathbairr chaemu cen curadu, & airm gen fiadnu, & carbaid cen comarbada, da comergi don gleo garbtren in lae sin.
Is andsin robui co seasmach sirshiublach in crodachumachtach Mairt id_est dea in chatha, & sleagh aithger amnas ina laim consnigtis & conreithdis ria srotha falcmara fola o fograinne co hurlaind oc thairrngairi bais & aideada na curad ceachtarda, co rocomtheann & cor-comgres co hacgarb anindeach na hairsidi athloma sin dochum a chele & in chathaigthi, co na tard nech dib sin a crich na a cathraig dariacht.
Ros-lin fuailfed fergi fithigi iad, coma hurloma lama na loechraidi do chlaidbib cruaidi cathaigthi & do slegaib seta sodibraicthi re hailgius na hirgaili.
tra acht na bad mera milid in chatha, uair ba hadbul re aisneis trethan & tindenas na n-echrad n-allmarda ac comchrathad na carpat ac foshenm na srianmireand, comdais suarca sneachtaidi na faicheada fondglasa risna caeboib coemchubair consnigtis co siradbol dar oilib na hechraidi cach conairi concingtis na cairpthig. Et is andsin rocomaicsich cach d'aroile dib, & ba he dlus rohimnaiscid na hairsidi sin, co comraictis a troigthi ar n-ichtur & a n-aigthi ar n-uachtur, & a sceith chuanna chabradacha re 'roili, & a cloidbi cruadgera cathaigthi, & a cathbairr choema chummaidi re cheli, coma snasta data datha & dellradacha dona cumdaigib.
Badar ac na curadaib cathbairr thaidlecha aroili cein no co roforruamait a frasad na fala a corpthaib na curad ac imcombualad iartoin.
Et o raerig confad comtnuthach cosnumach iter na curadaib sin & romearaid menmanda na miled, rochrithnaich in talam trenadbul re trethnaich na trenfher re tendta in tachair, comma breasmaidm buaidirtha crislach cocuasta na firmaméindti, amal comcumaisctis na gaetha garbgluairi gadsnimacha in ceathar duil comairsing co nn-aiceantaib examla, amal nobetis isin caip cumascda as ar-tebit ar tus co taibseanach id_est asin mais.
Et ba hindtamuil aidchi dona hairsidib sin re hirgail neoil dorcha dermairi na n-arm n-examla aca ndi-brugun co dluith os in degshluag comma cumang int aer anbthenach uastu re himud na n-urchar aca n-athchur eturru.
Uair rochomdibraicid andsin bera aithgera iarnaidi, & rofrasaid slega suainmecha sodibraici.
Et rolaeit cairgi comchruindi a taiblib tulamais, contaidlitis amal saignena solusta os na sluagaib, & rotelgid saitheada sarechta saeget eturru, & ni talam contaidlidis ac toitim na hairm sin, acht anad i cendaib curad & i taebaib trenfher & i sleasaib saerchland.
tra acht rothimchill cach a chele dib andsin, amal timchellas tond mara moir ochra cuan & calad, & darala 'na comracaib iad. Is andsin darala Ipseus mac Asopas do Tiabandaib aigid ind agaid & Menalca do Grecaib id_est taisech na n-Eoballda.
Roscail & ros-crothastar Ipseus Tiabanda munter Menalca, cur-fhacsad a tigerna a oenur i n-eigin irgaili da n-eis.
Is andsin rochuir-seom curadchomlond re hIpseus re re cian, & o tharraid baegal gona ar in n-Grecda sin i lleith da druim, co rop don leith araill dotharraing Menalcos as in sleig; & ac toitim do, datharlaic urchor do Ipseus di, co rus-gon, & adbath fen fo chetoir.
Acus asa haithli tarlaic airsid ammaindsech do Thiabandaib id_est Amindtus urchar do saigit do Iasid mac Pedimuis do Grecaib co torchair de.
Is andsin rocomraic coraid do Cailidondaib id_est Agreius re trenfher do Tiabandaib id_est Pegeius, & robui cach dibh ac comairlech aroli, co tuc Agreius builli do Peig, co roben a laim ndes on gualaind de, & co rothoit lam in laich sin.
Robui ac siubal & ac lemnig ar lar & a claideb conmert inti.
Et o 'tchondairc Acetes do Grecaib sin, tanic & rotrenbuail in laim ar lar, co rus-crechtnaig co mor.
Rocomraic andsin Ipis do Thiabandaib re hAccamas n-anacarach do Grecaib, & rothoit in Tiauanda do gonaib in Grecda sin.
Rocomraic dono arís do Ipseus mac Asopuis & do Arcus engnumach do Grecaib.
Rogargaigsead a ngliaid, & rocruadaigsed a comlond, & rothoit Argus Grecda, ger-u airsid, don irgail sin.
Et arna thoitim sin les, darala in trenfher Tiphis do Grecaib chuici, & se bar eoch, & rochuirset comlond, & tanic andsin a ara i fiadnaisi Thiphis id_est Abas, & rogon co hamnas Ipceus.
Ipceus, immorro, trascrais, & trenmarbais na firu sin, co torchradar les.
Is andsin tarla comrac cethrair ar lar in chatha id_est dias brathar do Tiabandaib id_est Ión & Dapnis, & dias brathar do Grecaib id_est Fares & Abás, & roba chomlund bagach braithremail sin do leith dar leth, cein cor-thuitsead in dias Tiabanda sin risin dis do Grecaib.
Et o rotuitsead leo, tucsad aichni cor brathir iad ar comdichracht a comraic & ar cosmaileacht a ndelba, & tanic a n-aicned co mor forro, & ba truag leo a toitim dia lamaib.
tra acht ba suaichinti sarecha saercland isin chath cheachtarda sin, & is andsin ratrascair, & rotimchill Emon echtach anrata do shíl calma Chathim gasrada Grec, comtis buidni buaidertha, & comtis taircsenaich techig re trethan in Tiabanda sin aca tuargain. Roindsaig, immorro, Tid talchar togaidi mac rig na Calidoine sluagu tenda na Tiabanda 'na aigid sin, comdis dirmada dianscailti, & comtis crithnaigthi comlaind, & comtis ailsedaig engnuma da eis.
Ba he tra samail na desi sin, amal norethidis da buindi diana dileand a slebtib arda amreidi, co tochlait, & co timairgid leo turscara in talman, co linait na fangleanna fo ethib dib.
Is andsin roerig Idas mac Conceist do Tiabandaib, & is amlaid roerig & aithleanda loisctheacha lasamna 'na laim, & rodibriced ba na sluagaib iat, co mba buaidirthi gasraidi Grec leis, & mar dabui ban samla sin, tarla Tid mac rig na Calidone da indsaigid, & tuc sadud setrech sleigi bar in fer, co torchair & tend a droma re lar & a aithindeada urderga air anuas, & is ed roraid Tid ris:
‘Ni loiscfea tra loechraid Lerna ni as mo id_est na Greic, acht chena coingebthar tu coma luaithred lanmin do chorp arna loscad ona hathindib taebderga raimarchrais fein.’
Et o darigni-sium sin, imasae fa sluag na Tiabanda, amal tigir croda confadaig 'ma cethraib comimda, & torchair in cuicer rigmilead-sa les don ruathar sin id_est Caon curita, & Polus primechtach, & Cromis coscorach, & Elicon anglondach, & Taigis trenchalma.
Emon, immorro, nir-ba lugu a echta in airseda isin ar na sluagaib Grec, & ni tharaid dil a fhergi dib re lanailgius a luathmarbtha, ger-ba dluithi na sluaig aca slaidi, & ger-ua calma curaid chroda Chalidóne, munter talchar Tid.
Rotholl & rothanaig in trenfer Tiabanda sin iad id_est Emon crechtach mac Crioin, cein no co tarla chuici in macaem beoda borrfadach id_est Butis.
Robui seic immorro ac tairmesc na trenfher gan teiched do denam re n-Emon.
Et mar dabui-sium amlaid sin ac trengresacht caich dochum in chomluind, tanic Emon chuici gan airigud, co tuc builli do thuaig truim Tiabanda do, co rodluig & co rodianscail a chend ar do air.
Et rochuir Ipaiss sacart Apaill comrac 'na diaid sin ris, & i forcind in chomruic dorochair-sium re hEmon.
Et arna thuitim leis, rofobair Polites sacart do Baich id_est dea inn fhina debaid agmar aicbel ris, & dorochair dono in fer sin do laim Emon croda cetna, & ger-ba sacart sin, nir-ba sruitheada a n-aideada re hEmon.
Et rofoibredar dias aili do Ghrecaib 'na diaid sin id_est Hiperíon & Damasus daigechtach, & torchradar les-sium iad.
tra acht robo dith ar Grecaib don gleo sin, mene beth Menerua, bandei in gaiscid, ac imguin leo. Et robui Ercoil ac gabail re Tiabandaib, uair robo dei in tan sin he.
Rochomraic iter in deIsin ar lar in chatha id_est iter Ercoil & Menerba.
Is ed roraid Ercoil:
‘A siur inmain,’ ar se, ‘a Menerba, ca hecendal roimluaid ind aroen i cend aroili isin chath-sa na n-Grec & na Tiabanda?
Uair rap usa limsa tachur re m'athair uasal re hIoib, ina ritsu, a Menerua; uair ba mor do coscur chathbuadach rucas-sa tred chumachta-su.
Et cetaigim dit, a ingen, masa thindenus let, in Teib do thogail.’
Rochetaig-sium immorro andsin, & rocendsaich Menerba o briathraib ailgenaib Ercail, & rofhacaib in cath iarsin, & roimgaib dono Ercail Emon gan beth ac fortacht do, & roleicsead coimdilsi iter na curadaib.
Ba hanmainditi tra Emon ac airlech na n-Grec Ercoil da fhacbail amlaid sin, & roairig Emon Tiabanda gan airsideacht 'na urchuraib & gan bailci 'na buillib.
Roimpo co hathlom do dechad asin chath.
Adchondairc, immorro, mac rig na Calidone Emon ac teched.
Tuc urchur n-inelldiuriuch chuici cor-ben int sleg iter bili in sceith & a cathbarr ina munel; & ger-ba beo 'na diaid, robo cromcend caichi, & ni rosamail silliud dara eis ar gnuis in gaiscedaig rogon he, uair nir-ba tualaing tachair ris, acht roela & rofacaib in cath arsin.
Asa haithlIsin dorala taisech tuaithi do Tiabandaib id_est Protiuis a ainm, d'indsaigid in Chaladonda cetna.
Seoilaid-seam co setreach in sleig da indsaigid co romarb Tid in milid cosin midach bui fae don urchur sin.
Et arsin roopair Corebus croda do Thiabandaib gleo garb arna Grecaib, & ba sacart sruitheata dona Muisib id_est do bandeib in bindiusa in fer sin.
Et ger-ba sacart tra, nir-ba saeglach; uair fuair a airlech do laim mic rig na Calidone.
Roerich 'na diaid sin Aitis oc engnomach do Thiabandaib; & ar gairi in cleamnasa, roobair in gilla sin calma do denum.
Uair is amlaid robui ar naidm Ismen do id_est derfiur do Ethiocles do rig na Tebhi.
Et is amlaid robui in gilla sin & lene coem corcorglan immi.
Et ba cumdaigthi carbat & cathbarr inn fhir sin d'or alaind ilecairthi & saigdi ailli orda 'na laim.
Et imasae-sium fa na sluagaib ban samla sin amal leoman londmer ua thretaib teicheacha in talman.
Et as e ni doroigne Aitis.
Robui co baeth mear borrfadach ac gairm mic rig na Calidone chuici do chomruc & da chomlond ris.
O 'tchualaig Tid sin, sillis fair, & faiphtis gen gaire 'na agaid, & raidis ris:
‘Is comdingna cuicil, a gilla,’ ar se, ‘uair is mor am maisi dit milid mar misi dod marbad.’
Et is amlaid roraid-sium sin, roleic a armu uili ar lar cenmotha birán bunsaigi baisi bui 'na laim, uair nir miad leis airm croda churada do imirt ar in gilla oc naidenta sin, & tuc urchar dIsin do co roben in eslind a chuirp, & co torchair fo chetoir.
Et ger-ba dathchain derscaigthech airm & etgud inn fhir sin, nir miad & nir maisi re mac rig na Calidone a fodbugud impu sin.
Et ar na thoitim sin leis, 'masoe ba sluagaib na Tiabanda.
Rosoiged na trenu & na taiseachu, & ni beanad re drongaib ndaesscursluaig na re drochlaechaib coma dithfine ar saerclandaib togaidi na Tiabanda don tres sin no cor-erig Menidceius do Thiabandaib, & cor-gres na sluagu, & is ed roraid:
‘A truagu, a Tiabanda,’ ar se, ‘nach nar daib cen athais engnumach do digail ar na Grecaib?’
Tuc tra in gresacht sin brig & baraind n-adbail i trenferaib na Tiabanda co rochomdluthaigsed in chathirgal i cend aroili.
Et in tan robadar-sum amlaid sin, is and darala da ingin Eidip co hanband imshnimach ac comrad re 'roili thall i cathraig na Tebi, & ba hadbul a n-imsnim im dail a mbraithrech, uair na fedadar cia dib bud coscrach don chur sin, & is andsin roraid Ismine:
‘Is truag limsa,’ ar si, ‘a shiur inmain, comorad in chatha-sa iter mo braithrib, & adchondarc aslingi,’ ar si, ‘fes dam fein re hAithis calma curata, & ni fuil derbairdi na figrad firuilc nach facca-sa andsin.’
Et immar dabadhar-som ac in comrad sin, adchondcadar buidin moir cucu isin cathraig.
Et is amlaid rabadar & corp lethmarb leadairthi accu i crislach a sceith, & is e bui andsin Athais, & adchondairc Iochasta he, & rogairm a hingena chuci, & doriachtadar uili uasa cind, & robadar ac saithin a medar & a ngloir ar in ngilla, & nir-ba tualaing-sium tra a n-acallaim acht robui 'ca fechud, cein no cor-elath uad in beccan bethad robui fa bruindib.
Cen tra robadar na mna thall isin chathraig ar na himraitib sin, rothennsad curaid croda in catha cechtarda amuich i cend aroili, amal na comraictis riam remi sin.
Ba he tresi & tenni roimir cach bar a cheli dib isinn uair sin, co roerig eturru in bé néit badba buaidirthi id_est Enio, siur Mairt id_est dei in chatha.
tra acht ba glondmer gaiscedaig Grec isinn irgail sin, uair ba sarechtach saigdi in rig id_est Parthanapeus, & ba hathluma allata echrada Ipamedon ac toirnium na Tiabanda, & bad sodanaich sargala & sargona slega Capaneuis. Ger-ua linmara gaiscedaig Grec andsin tra & ger-ba ili a n-echta, rodearscaich dib uile in trenfer tairpthech tairisi talchar id_est Tid mac rig na Cailidone.
Et rogob robur roecla a bidbadu reimi co na faeltais fosugud ar a chind, acht mad techead tindneasnach ar gach leath reimi.
Et 'otchondairc-sium iad ban samla sin, is ed roraid riu:
‘Na teiched itir, a Tiabanda, acht as cora daib a digail orumsa in coica curad romarbus feacht aili uaib & na hilmilid rothoitsead aniu dom laim.’
Et in am robui-sium 'ga rad sin, adchondairc uad taidlech suaichnid solusglan chathbarr Ethiocleis, ri na Tiabanda, isin cath.
Is andsin immorro roboccbertaich-sium in sleig searbsroin sarechtaich, & tuc ro n-urchair uada di ar amus Ethiocleis.
Et robad scith lim scur don chathugud sin, mani thairmiscdis na dei in n-urchur co rob ed robean in n-araid Ethiocleis id_est Iflegias co rus-facaib gan anmain.
Et o 'tchonnaic-sium sin, roimir coma chlaidib ar na cathaib ac rochtain Ethiocleis, cein no go tucsad trentaisich tenda na Tiabanda fidba aithger urnocht da n-armaib i timchell in airdrig, & co rucsad leo ar culu asin cath amach he ar imgabail Tid.
Et gid ead nir-thairmisc a trengal-sium sin ac dithugud na sluag, no co torchradar na taisich-sea da laim id_est Toas tomaithmech, & Deilochus dasachtach, & Clonius coscorach, & Ipatas ainindeach.
Et is e ni donid Tid andsin mar damarbad in curaid, rodibraiced a chend & a chathbarr uad i n-oenfeacht uan cath.
Et as andsin rogabad cumung conaire ar lar in catha ac slaigi na sluag ar Tit, co na fedad imluad n-imtheachta risna cladaib comarda do chorpaib curad ar na cruadleadrad & re fadbaib fuilidi na trenfer ac toitim 'na timchell da gach leth.
Et rochomiadsad andsin imi do gach leith & do cach thaib trenfir tenna talchara na Tiabanda, & rothelcset airm ecsamla imda as cach aird da indsaigid, cor-ba coill comdluith do slegaib cruaidi comclanda a sciath mor mileata in tan rocrathad uad.
Nir-ba tarba dono cathbarr do chind in curad sin risna cairrgib cruaidi comamis rothelgtis na Tiabanda do as cach aird, cor-ba comderg do chru a chind.
Nir-bo din dono luirech don lech sin re himad na saeigid srengluath ac dul trempi, comdis riathair ruamannda ucht & taeib in trenmiled sin ar na tollad.
Et in silliud rosill secha ar na sluagaib, atchondairc Menerba, bandei in gaiscid, ac dingbail neich dona harmaib sin de.
Ba fortacht & ba forithin mor leis-sium sin.
Acht ceana nir-ba din ar scis do, uair roseol chuici tresin cath sleg crandremarcrofhairsing sech bili in sceith cor-ben i n-ucht in airseda sin id_est mic rig na Calidone, co roscailt & co roscail a cridi 'na chliab, & ni fes dono cia thuc in n-urchar sin re himad na n-arm & re dlus int sluaig, cein no cor-sill uad int anglond & int airsid Tith cae da danic chuici int sleg, & co tard aichni i tiug int shluaig ar inte rus-teilc id_est Menilipus mac Astacis.
Et o thuc aichni air uada, rogab in sleig a llaim in fhir ba nessa do id_est Opleius do Grecaib, & tuc urchar fertsech feramail uad, ger-b anband robui, co tarla do Menelepus trena cliab & tre chraidi.
Is andsin roindsaigset Greic inn oenfecht dochum Thid, & rucsad leo he do lethtaib in chatha, & rossaidsed da sciath comdaingen corcarda imi andsin id_est sciath do gach leith do.
Et is ed so roraidsed ris, co ternobad don guin sin.
Et cuma roraidsed sin & robadar ac toirrsi truim & ac domenmain moir.
Tid, immorro, mac rig cuanda Calidone, roairig fen airdena bais ac tiachtain chuici, & is ed roraid:
‘Airchisid dim, a Grecu,’ arse, ‘& ni m'idnocol có m'atharda na m'adnocol sirim oraib, uair is miscais lim anoissi in corp aprisc irchradach-sa i fuilim.
Acht sirim oraib cend Menelipuis do thobairt cucum, uair adar lim rotoirned a nert don urchur tucus do.
Et, a rigrad Grec,’ arse, ‘tabraid dam in n-aiscid sin uaib.
Et caidi,’ ar se, ‘Ipomedon anrata, & caidi Partanopeus primechtach?
Tabraid in Grecda glormer Capaneus.
Tabraid uaib dam, a ocu, cend in churad rom-chrechtnaig.’
Et o 'tchualaich-sium sin, roerig Capaneus i remthus re cach co hairm i rraibi Menelipus; & o ranic, rothocaib leis he os a gualaind cli chomnert, no cor-chuir urchar uad de i fiadnaisi Thid.
O 'tchonnaic immorro Tid andsin Menelipus re fuineachtaib bais & i nn-airdeanaib eca, is ed roraid:
‘Tabraid a chend in churad i comfochraib dam,’ ar se.
Et o thucad, robui seal 'ga fhegad co hainindech, & is comairli darigni, rotairind air, & rogob 'ga chacnam & 'ca cruadtescad andsin cind Menelipuis.
Et antan robui-sium amlaid sin, is and tainic Menerba id_est bandei in gaiscid, o Ioib, mac Saduirn, & is ime dochuaid da indsaigid d'iarraid fortachta ar Thid isin cath; & o nach tucad di, rochundig ar Ioib dei do denam do Thid.
rig dec do Thiabandaib, is ed romarb Tid isin lo sin ar galaib oenfhir. Et tucad disi sin, & tanic dochum Thid, & 'ca aiscin di, rogob aduath & ecla mor hi remi.
Adchondairc he ac ithi chind Menelipuis, & o raerigedar nathracha garba gaisedacha na Gorgoni 'ma cend na bandei id_est Menerba, roimpa, & roteich o Thid, & rofhacaib ban samla sin da eis he.
Et robui-sium amlaid sin ac ithi chind Menelipuis, cein co roetla uad in becan bethad robui and, & co fuair bas fo chetuair.
Conaid confad Thid conigi sin.
Ba hadbal tra toirrsi & domenma na n-Grec don gnim sin.
O rochualadar immorro na Tiabanda Tid croda confadach do chacnum & do ithi chind Menelibuis, rogob fichfergi & anindi adbul iad.
Na Greic, immorro, ba lughaide a nguba & a ngeran a los Tid.
Uair ba holc acu dul dar in recht n-indligthech ndeona id_est duni d'ithi.
Et is ed innister and dono co rofhacaib Mairt, dea in chatha, in chath i lla sin re haduath in gnima sin dorindi Tid.
Is andsin roericheadar na Tiabanda co tindisnach do digail Menelipuis, amal bad fialchairdi diles dearbrathar do iad uili; & rogres Ethiocles rig na Tebi co tren andsin na sluagu, & is ed roraid:
‘Adar lind, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘nidad daini in sluag cusa soichi id_est na Greic, acht mad nathracha nemi & leomain lanmera ac ithi daine amal dorigni Tid, & ni tabraid da n-airi na dei uasta risna hairdib aduathmara doniad.’
Et o roraid-seom sin, rotrenindsaig na Grecu, & ba haicnead oenduine uili andsin ac na Tiabandaib do chosnum chuirp Thid risna Grecaib co ndiglaidis air cend Menelipuis d'ithi, & na huilc ar cheana dorindi Is andsin tra roerig Fama, ingen Terra, co firluath foluaimneach, & roscail in scel sin ba hilltuathaib na n-Grec id_est Tid da marbad.
Et ged chualaig Polinices mac Eidip sin a fer comtha & comaind da marbad, nir-chreid a chetuair.
Uair rabui d'aichni a eangnuma aici-sium nar-ba doig les curaid da commaidem, na milid da marbad, na hairsidi d'arrach inn fhir sin can fis.
Et gid ed o cualaig-sium a deimin, rosocht fair coma cruaidhither ri crandlaem gach n-alt & gach n-aigi de o chind co bond, & robanad imi mar scoith-sheamair no mar lenid ar na lantuar, & roerich ceo comdorcha cumad dara rosc coma dorcha doimtheachta do gach conair.
Romescad a menma coma balba buaidirthi na briathra rolabrad isan uair sin.
Is andsin rogab a armu, & tanic reimi co toirrseach toitmendach & a sleag ina diaid gan tiachtain de a tocuala re truma na toirrsi.
Et in chonair thanic, doruladar do munter Tid os cind chuirp a tigerna.
Rotaisbenad leo dosum he, & o 'tchondoirc-sium he, roleic ina loigi fo chetoir ar corp a charad, & robai ac nuall moir, & is ed roraid:
‘A fhir cumtha,’ arse, ‘ni hiad so aisceada dingbala rodligis dimsa id_est do thoitim i tír na Tebi ic cosnum rigi damsa & misi slan dar th' eis.
Et bid fada bam loingseach-sa dod lo, uair ni buigbead brathair na carait cumtha mar thusu dot eis.
Et, a Grecu,’ ar se, ‘facbaid-si misi m'aenur sund na marbthar sib ni as mo.
Acht leicid etrum-sa & mo brathair, uair is fo lim ita gan rigi & gan flaitheamnas dar eis Tid.
Et truag dono, a Thid, nach rothoitius-sa leatsu inn adaig racomraicsemar aroen ar tus i cathraig alaind Adraist.
Et ba caeom do chlu in la dochuadais d'iarraid rigi damsa cusin Teib, & adar lim ni lemdais laich gaili do ledrad iter, na curaid comruc rit.
Et cia na dirmanda diairmithi na degsluaig rotrascradar?
Uair ni mo na Ioib badein no Mairt dea in chatha confaeltis fuirmed farain fort.’
Et asa haithlIsin tuc a lam dar agaid fordorcha fulidi in gilla, & roglan na frasa fala di.
‘Ba miscais am let,’ ar se, ‘mo namait-sea cosaniu, & ni biu-sa beo tar th' eis iter.’
Et is cuma adbert sin & ronocht a claideam & rothriall a lecun co heslind, no gor-iadsad a munter lama tairis, & gor-tairmisc a cliamain uasal Adraist é, & robui 'ca comdignad, cor-chuir a claideb 'na tindtech.
Et robui Polinices co hanband enirt andsin re crad na cumad & re truma na toirrsi.
Cained Tid connigi sin, & lamchomairt Poliniceis moir mic Eidip andsein.
Acus o rabui-sium amlaid sin, rochromsad trenfhir thogaidi na Tiabanda 'man airdrig id_est Ethiocles dochum in chatha.
Is e rofhrecair iad isinn uair sin in rigmilid ard allata Ipomedon do Grecaib, & as amlaid robui, inna buidin bodba ar lar in chatha in fer sin, & sciath comnart cruindleathan fair, & sleag remur rofhata 'na laim, & claideb lethan langer isin laim araill.
Et nir-ba suaill ni ris ba samalta eisium andsin id_est carrac thend thunidi i crichib cuain & calaith, & na tonda taebuaine in mara crithainbtheanaig cumascda 'ga trenbualad, & sisi gan scailiud gan scuchud reompu.
Is andsin dono rogob Eithiocles for acallaim na n-Grec, & is ed roraid riu:
‘Cid on,’ ar se, ‘nach mebal daib beith ac ditin cuirp croda colaich Thid?
saethar dimain a denam.
Uair gid a oenur rofhacbad sib he, ni loigfitis ethaidi imluaimnecha aoeir air na cuanarta croesach con, & ni loiscfed tend coemchoiserca he, a haithli in chuil doronni id_est duni d'ithi.’
Et is cuma adbertsom sin & tuc urchur do Ipomedon Grecda gruadsolus dont shleig rigda robui ina laim, co tarla 'na sesum asa sciath suaichnid sechtfhillti.
Et tucsat dono dias aili do Tiabandaib da urchar inn oenfhecht do Ipomedon id_est Pheres fuabartach & Liccus lanchalma.
Saeigis secha urchar Phires, & tescais cir chathbairr in churad urchur Liccuis.
Ipomedon, tra, ger-uat imda urchair do, ni cem ar cul ruc as a n-inud i roibi, acht robui co hathlum anrata ac luathimirt a sceith i nn-agaid na laechraidi.
Is andsin adchond-cadar da gaiscedach glondmera do Grecaib in n-eicin sin i roibi Ipamedon id_est Alcon anrata mac Sitsión, & Idas athlom anglondach a Pisa.
Tangadar sin, & a mbuidni diana danarda maroen riu, do fhortacht & d'fhoirithin Ipamedon.
Et tucsad gluin re gliaid aroen ris, & ba foirithin dosum sin ona ceathaib cumascda cruadarm robadar as cach aird air.
Et o rathocaib a cheand & rodibraic in sleig ngairbremur n-Grecda robai 'na laim, coma luaithithir re saeigid a sreng ar na seolad tresna sluagaib, co tarla inni Polistas, comdis airdni athchumtha da heis, & tresin fer sin co rotholl in milid Mopsus, & co rotrenmarb in triar Tiabanda ba nesa do id_est Pothcis & Cidon & Tanager, & tresna feraib sin cen anad, cor-ben i cind inn airseda Eiritsis, cor-ba silta semanna na sleigi da fhiaclaib & da inchind, coma seiser sarlaech romarb Ipamedon don oenurchar.
Et asa haithlIsin roeirich Leondtem ar scath int shluaig, & tuc urchar fas falaig dochum Ipamedoin, & tanic 'na diaid sin co dichelta, & rotharraing Tid chuici.
Ger-b adbul in ecen engnoma i roibi Ipamedon, atchondairc in Tiabanda ac tarraing Thid, & tuc bemclaideb do cor-ben a laim 'ga gualaind de, & is ed roraid:
‘Tid,’ ar se, ‘dobean do laim dit.’ tra acht ba tri rucsad Tiabanda chucu corp Tid, & rucsad na Greic uaithib ba tri he a fornirt cathaigthi & engnuma & imgona.
Acht ata ni cheana, nir-etsad trenmilid na Tiabanda uili cumscugud Ipamedoin o churp Thid, & ge ratelcthea do reitheda togla tulamais da scailter cnuic & cathracha, ni claefidis é uada, no co tanic in fhiuir aduathmar ifirnaidi id_est Tesifoné.
Et rogob aduath na catha ceachtarda re hurgrain na hamaidi sin, cen co facadar hi.
Is andsin rogabsi delb fhir do Grecaib fuirri id_est Alis, & tanic co foill fethamail dochum Ipamedon, & rolabair ris.
Ba hingnad re hIpamedon in ecla & in uromuin rogob e re guth na baidbi, & si a richt Alis gaiscedaig.
Uair is ed roraid-si, & si ac toirrsi:
‘Is dimaín a ndénai,’ ar si, ‘apaigi gasrad n-Grec do ditin, & ba doilgi dit Adraist int ardrig do brith do Tiabandaib asin chath ina cheli, & ata acat cetgairm-su seach cach da fhortacht & da forithin.
Et is truag limsa mar adchondarc a trillsi taitneamacha i llamaib na loechraide 'ga lantarraing.
Et ni fata uait itir e id_est i fail i faichi in ndluim lanmoir luaithrid, & in ceo comthiug os cendaib int shluaig.’
Ni fhitir thra Ipomedon cid dogenad de sin, & roathgres in badb sin he, & adbert ris:
‘Is coru dit Adraist d'fhorithin inna anad acinn apach treththoll-sa Thid.’
Is andsin rochuir-sium ar faesum a muintire in cathirgal dara eis id_est corp Tit, & tanic i nndiaid na baidbi, & si i richt Alis, cein no co ndeachaid uad ina richt fein hi.
Et o dachuaid-si uad, adchondairc na Grecu, & Adraist eturru ina charbad, gan ecla gan imsnim air.
Et is imi doroni Tesifone in ceilc sin co mbertais na Tiabanda corp Tit leo dar eis Ipomone.
Dala immorro na Tiabanda rucsad leo corp Tid fo chetoir dar eis Ipomedoin.
Rocurid gairi coscair & commaideam acu uasa chind, & o 'dchualaig Ipomedon sin, tuc aichni ar in gnim:
‘Is fir,’ ar se, ‘os cind chuirp Thid doberar in gair-sea.’
Acht chena ba hannam re trenfheraib tomaítheam air cein ba beo, uair ba menci leis roena romadmand & dith ar tuathaib na Tiabanda remi.
Et o rasiacht cucu amlaid sin corp Tith, roiadsad immi ass cach aird, & darindset guingaland de amal nobeith beo, & ba buaid ngaiscid ris trenfher dib rofordergad a armu asa apach.
Nir-fhuiling tra do Ipomedon sin do cloistecht gan dul da indsaigid, ge rafitir gur-b anburus dó cathugud dar cend chuirp gen anmain and.
Et tanic remi, & a claideb urnocht ina laim, & ni thuc aichni ar carait na ar cumthach andsin re tendta in tindesnais & re fiuchud na fergi.
Acht cheana ba tairmeasc dosum na sligthi sleamna risna srothaib falcmara fala, conferdais a taebuib na trenfher ar na tuargain dosum, & re himad arm na n-airsed ar na n-airleach, & carbad cruadbristi na curad ar na comach, & re loechaib leathmarba ac urtriall aitheirgi.
Et robo thairmesc luith & lanimtheachta do in guin tucastar Ethiocles ri na Tiabanda air.
Et nir-airig-sium sin, no ma rofhitir, nir miad leis a legin ris, no co ndiglad ar inti dos-tuc air.
Is andsin adchondairc-sium ara tairisi Tid & ech a thigerna 'na laim ac foshenm a srein co siblach, & rotriall-som fuirri, & o rotriall, robui int ech ac doibli & ac debili ris, & is ed roraid-sium ria:
‘Cid nam-leig-sea ort, a eich?’ arse, ‘uair ni fhuil do shuil re crichaib na Calidone, na risin rig rad-riadaig, & bageba ferbruigib firglana i ngartaib Grec, & tair limsa do digailt Thid ar na Tiabanda.’
Ba samalta, tra, co tuiced int ech a n-ebairt-sium ria, & roan ris & dochuaid-sium fuirri, & o dachuaid, roling int ech co luthmar lanathlum assa bail robui, co rocrithnaigsedar faichtega firglana & tulcha tondglasa na Teibi re trethan.
Rodlumait, immorro, & rodaingnigid dirmanna danarda na Tiabanda, o 'tchondcadar Ipomedon cucu ban samla sin.
Rothuairc & rothesc andsin Ipomedon iadsum, comtis tamain thulmera ac tuitim chuirp na curad da eis.
Roimpotar na Tiabanda remi-sium, & rotheichset dona moigib reidi ara rapadar, no co rangadar co himlib amreidi srotha Ismen, & roopredar caeiti falaig forru andsin, & robui tuili falcmar firdomain isin sruth intan rosiachtadar-sum da indsaigid he.
Ba gairit dono a n-osad-sum andsin intan rosiacht Ipomedon da n-indsaigid, & roobair iad gan toirnem & gan toirlem da eoch, acht robui 'ca timchellad & 'ga timsugud.
Is andsin rolingestar na Tiabanda i nn-athaib & i nn-indberaib na haband, & roleicsead a n-armu uaithib risin sruth re tindenus in techid, & ba he dichracht in teichid commitis i teand re grian & re gainem int shrotha aca falach ar ecla Ipomedoin, uair ba ferr leo a ndianbadud ina bith ac fulang imnid inn fhir sin.
Gach oen dib ba treoraig usci, rotrialldais snam darin sruth, no co mbertis na cathchresa ceangailti & na luireacha lanchumga i nn-ichtur iad.
Imasae-sium fuithib amal bleidmil moradbul muiridi ba bradanaib becca ballbreca, co scailit & co scanrit remi co hochraib cuan & calath.
Is andsin rocomraic fer do muntir Ipomedoin id_est Ión, & Cromis do Tiabandaib ar lar na haband, & rothoit andsin Ión risin Tiabanda.
Nir-bo echt cen aithi sin, tra, uair thuc Antipus do Grecaib coscur Cromis fo chetoir.
Ni head sin dono nach taras ar Anntopus, uair rothoit re hIpseus mac Asopas do Tiabandaib, & ba cend saegail sin do Astiages & do Linus do Grecaib, uair rothoitsed andsin comthoitim re hIpseus Tiabanda.
Is andsin rotrascair, & rothoirind Ipomedon sluagu toirrseacha na Tebi.
Robuaidir immorro 'na haigid Ipseus na buidni Grecda badar maraen re Ipomedon, coma forruad fuilidi sruth alaind Ismen isinn uair sin, ger-ba tonda tibreacha taebglana intan tangadar na catha sin.
Deithbir on ba drochad comnart comimtheachta d'armaib imda arbristi uachtur na haband on bruach co 'raill, & ba hacaireda comdaingni conairi laich leadharthacha lanbaiti re grian & re gainem ichtair na haband.
Intan robadar amlaid sin, rosin Agriphus do Tiabandaib a laim dochum chraibi robui uasa chind i mbruach na haband, & tug Menetceus do Grecaib beim claidib do, cor-leig in laim risin craib, & co rothoit isin n-abaind fo chetoir.
Tuc immorro Ipseus do Tiabandaib sadud sleigi ar Saigis do Grecaib, coma crechtach comoslaichti a chnes a n-ichtur na haband.
Et rotriall Agenor a brathair a thocbail leis, & o nar-et a imarchur, roleig a badud fen maroen ris.
Et rothoit dono Caletus do Tiabandaib andsin isin saebchoiri ba chomair, co robaided and.
Ger-ba bas tra crich cach curad dib sin, ba hecsamla a n-aideda, uair is and dorala sleg Megalis do Tiabandaib 'na seol risin sruth dochum Aigerteis do Grecaibh co rus-facaibh can anmain.
Is andsin rogonadh tra ech taebhsolus Tit ro fa Ipomedon co roiue co debeil dasachtach aca chur-som di.
Et fo hingnath leis-sium sin, uair ni fitir cidh ima roiue, no co facaidh ant slegh 'na sesam eisti.
Et o doconnairc-sium sin, dotairling di, & roben ant sleg aisti, & rofopair da cois sluighi na sluagh, co rotoitsit in coicer miledh so do maithibh na Tiauanda les don ruathar sin id_est Nomius neimhnech, & Mimas mileta, & Lucus luathechtach, & Leceis lanchalma, & Teius mac Teisfis.
Et tuc maithem n-anacuil do mac ele Teisfis id_est Fanenus, & is ed roraid ris:
‘Eiridh, a ghille,’ ar se, ‘do Teib, & innis innti mar dodigail misi Tit ar na Tiabanda, & is maith lium-sa cuirp na Tiabanda do bheth fo torthraib muiridibh can ithi can aite n-adnacail acu amal corp taebhgel Tit can onoir adnacail d'fhaghbail.’
Et ar sin rogab Ipimedon co dur desachtach comach claidim ar na Tiabandaib, co rrotoitsit na trenfhir-si da laim id_est Theron trenmileta, & Gian garbarmach, & Eriginus airdechtach, & Eris ergalach, & Cretis cosnamach.
Snamaighi sarcalma in fer sin, & tuc urchur do tsleig dochum Arsolais fircalmai antan bai ac snam darin sruth dochum a muintire, cor-facaibh can anmain.
Cia tra dochuimnighfed eachta Ipimedoin ar na Tiabandaib isin lo sin acht mad ar imadh fisidh fireolach no comachtach cianaesta senchasa?
As andsin dono rogab dalb aisi beodachta aenmacaem do Tiabandaib na facaidh cath riam roime id_est Crenes mac Fuinn & Nimpa id_est Ismen dei in mora no an srotha sin a mathair, & tainic dochum an catha.
Ba suaithnich solusta iter na sluaghaibh an gille sin, uair is amlaidh rouai & slegh coimremar uasta & claidem slipta saineamail 'na laim, & sciath oirderc ilbreachtach co ndelbaibh imdhaibh hecsamlaib innti for a muin.
Et tainic fon samla sin dochum Ipimedoin, & rouai aga gressacht & aga grennugud o ghuth mor, & atbert:
‘Ni fethamail conferthor risna feraib-si,’ ar se, ‘& ni suairc soola an sruth coemcoiserctha dar th'eis.’
Nir-lauair immorro Ipimedon ris-sium acht roinn-saigh é, & roeiridh an abhond ré aigid, coma gabail ar lamhaibh in laich sin re lanbualadh na buinnedha diana diluatha consnaighdis dar a formnaibh re hesaibh na hobond.
Et cidh edh robuail-sium, & roathbuail Croneis, co torchair é leis.
Adclos immorro don mathir in mic an gnim sin, & tainic co denmnedach dasachtach, & a folt scailti fo cend & isi ac dluighi a hetaig & ac bualadh a hochta & ac sirgairm & ag cathgairm a mic, & ge douai, ni fuair.
Acht chena rohincoiscedh di-se a mac do beth an bail a teit sruth Ismen isin muir a mach, & tainic co himluaimnech opond roimpi no co riacht conici an bail a mboi.
Et o rainic, rochuir a cenn fon sruth, & rouai aca iarraidh iter na corpaibh diclethi dichennta rouatar isin abhonn, no co fuair é, & ó dofuair, rotocaibh le co buidh banamail, no co ranic an bruach, & roleic uaithi arin fer fothremail, & roglan a corp & a chrechta, & rouai ac toirsi uas a cinn, & is ed roraidh:
‘Olc,’ ar si, ‘dot shenathir-se, na dei uasail do marbad do lecudh, a mic, & bat fochlachan for a lama o cianaibh antan dochuaidis uaim, & madh anois, immorro, is garbgne do ghnuisi & is tretholl do thaebh.’
Et rouai ag gresacht a athar Ismen dochum Ipomedoin do digail an gnima sin fair, & roraidh:
‘Is tairpthech adrasta Ipomedon,’ arsi, ‘& is tiugha taebdorchai tonna srotha Ismen re fuil & re fadhbha na Tiabanda do righruathar an righ sin.
Et tar-sa, a Ismen,’ ar si, ‘co ndernam adhnacul uasal andso dot ua id_est do mmo mac so.’
Et o docuala Ismen sin, rosiacht co toirsech teindesnach da inndsaighid é, & is ed roraid:
‘Ni huasal an onoir dam o cenn na dei id_est o Ioip, ára aidhble do chur fon sruth coemcoisrectha, & is mór do dheibh coema cumachta rohoiledh foa bruach, ge rolinadh do chorpaibh.
Et, a Ipomedoin,’ ar se, ‘masa dei misi, ni ba fhecht can aighfi duit an macaem so do mar--badh duit, & robo cumachtach & robad comaidhem let rochtain co muighibh Megene ar marbad m'ua-sa & can a digail fort.’
Et is cuma doraidh-sium sin & rotinóil & rotimsaigh srotha & esa & aibhne na Tiabanda co sruth n-Ismén, & roeirigh leosum tuile srotha Ismen dar bruachaibh & dar bordaibh, cuma locha linnti landoimne na hinada firma tartmora nach raibhi usci riam roime ann nach ua comnesa do Ipomedon, & rob ingnath leis usci na habann ag eirghi uime do cach taibh & do cach leth.
Et roeiridh ainmfine adbual mór andsin a sruth Ismen, co rrobris a buird & a bruacha co rrocumscaigi a cairci cendgarbha as a n-aitibh & as a n-inadaibh.
Imsnim a mac samla sin ní fuair Ipomedon riam roime, uair is ed tainic a n-aige & a n-ardde ant srotha co rochuired uadha na cairci commora da uillibh & da gluinibh, & is ed asbert:
‘A Ismen,’ ar sé, ‘can as tainic ditsa iter cumachta mar so do beth agut id_est mo thraethad-sa agut?’
Et o roraidh-sium sin, roleic Ismen railci romóra re trethan na tonn da innsaigidh co rrotuaircsit & co rotrenbuailsit co minic a ucht & a urbruinne.
Et ó nar-fael-sam trumma & tuinnsim na ralec romór sin & treisi ant srotha aca tuarcain, tuc a druimm riu, & roleic risin sruth é.
Et is cuma co mbuailtis buinnetha ruadha robarta int srotha trenadhbail Ipomedon, & na cetha do cairgibh comuscdha & do chruaidharmaibh dotelcdis Tiabanda do thir dó.
Ní fitir-sium tra cidh do dhenum, & ní fhuair dona sluagaibh nech rolamad buain ris, cer-ua ferrdi leis bás d'fagbail.
As andsin, immorro, doui bile dossach da thalmain os bruachaib ant srotha, & rosin-sium an laim ndeis cuige, & rogab lan a glaici do barr an bile, & rotoit an bile as an bunad & as a fremaibh re truma an miled aca tarraing, coma saobhcoire sírdomain a inudh da eis, & rosluiced Ipomedon isin saobhcoire sin.
Et antan consilldís na srotha an sarlaech sin, is ed roraidh:
‘As truagh duit, a Mairt, a dei in catha, bás mar so do imirt ormsa, mar dodhenta ar midlaech.
Et nír cusindiu rim a mac a samla.’
Conadh i oighidh Ipomedoin gruadsolais na Mecine isin glan Greic sin.
O 'dchuala immorro Iunand ilchrothach sin, tainic dochom Ioib, & adbert fris:
‘Is lór leici na Gregaigh do lot,’ ar si, ‘uair romarbad Tit tre sárugud Menerua, & fuair Aimpiaraus a oighidh triana indeoil Apaill, & saorthar dom-sa Ipomedon, uair is do gasraidh Grec a bunadhcenel, & iss dam-sa roidhbradh a mbreth les do chrud a crichi co a tir isin cathrig a Mbecine.
Et caidhi in gellad dorignis, co leicfedha na Gregaigh d'adhlucud iartain, & corp Ipomedoin a n-abaind a n-usci?’
O 'dcuala Iob sin, rouai ac fegadh na Teue uadhai, & rotraigh & rotoirinn tuile srotha Ismén, coma follus Ipomedon isin ait a raibhi ann.
O doconncatar na Tiabanda é fon samla sin, tucsat frais do shleghaibh & do saighdibh cuigi, coma coill comdluith a corp dibh, & cer-ua lanmarb letartai in laech sin, nir-lam laech do Tiabandaib a fodhuadh fo cloidem na fo cathbarr, cein no co rainic Ipseus, mac Asopais, da innsaigidh, cor-ben a arm uadh, & rouai ac buadhnas & ac bocasaich sechnon ant sluaigh, & cloidem ruithnech in rig aili ina laim & a cathbarr uo cenn.
‘Ata sunn,’ ar se, ‘coscarach Ipomedon, & rouai ac digail Tit ar na Tiabandaib.
Rodithaigit & rodianscailit a sruth Ismen iad,’ co madh X XI II righ romarbh Ipomedon enechsolus don ruathar sin ac digail Thit ar na Tiabandaib; & ni cuimnighit scribhinne ar chena na sluaghu romarbh ann.
Ba galar tromm tra risin righ mormenmnach ria Capaneus mac Tairsis do Grecaib an commaidhem sin do cloisdeacht; & robocbertaigh int sleg 'na laimh, & is ed roraidh:
‘Ba coir duit, a lam,’ ar sé, ‘cungnam cathaigthi lemsa, uair is iniud ata mo tairisi & ni ha caruit cumachtaig ele.’
Rothelc an gaiscedach sin an gius ngarbhsnoighthe rouai 'na laim, & roseol do innsaigid Ipseuis, cor-dianbris a druim ar scoltad a sceith & ar letradh a luirighi, coma samalta ri tor coimnert cloichi arna cruaidhbrisedh traethad in trenfir no in miledh sin ac toitim, & is ed roraidh Capaneus:
‘Fegh let,’ ar se, ‘misi rot-marbh, & is adhuar onorach dot hainm misi do d'marbad.’
Cuma atbert-sium sin & doben a claidem & cathbarr Ipomedoin de, & roben a claidhem fein leis dé, & rochuir air Ipomedon iat am bail a mboi 'na luighi, & is ed roraid ris:
‘Ac so, a ri, a Ipomedoin, th' airm fen duit, & airm do namat foraon friu, & loiscfidhtir lind leth ar leth iat antan idhbertar tu dona deibh.’
Cidh tra acht rouoi crich coscorach an catha sin co cunntabartach iter na Tiabanda & na Greic.
Uair ua hadhbul garbh nuallgubha na n-Grec ac cainedh Ipomedoin, & nir lugha toirsi na Tiabanda ac cainedh Ipseuis.
Cein tra rouatar-sam amlaidh sin, as ann dochuaidh Athalanta mathair Partanapeuis V II righa dochuadar do thogail Teue co sruth Latain do dhenum idhbarta do Dean id_est banndei na selcairechta i seic, & ua selcaire amra a mac-si dono Partanapeus, & is ed uadera disi na hidhbarta sin do dhenum id_est taidhbhsedha adhfhuathmara adcidh 'san oidhchi id_est fadhbh & arm a mic & a muntire d'fhaiscin 'na fiadnaisi, & can a beth etarru, & adconnairc fós a n-aislingi dair dosach dighuinn docoisercadh do Dean, a racuired a harmu antan uo scith i a haithle a sealca, a barr & a gega do toitim ri tenntaibh taluan, & rofiarfaid-si cidh rotesc an crann.
Rofhrecair Menadhnas hi id_est bansacart do muintir Baich, dei fortochta Tiabanda in Baich sin.
Rogabh hecla & adhfhuath Athalanta don gnim sin, & roeirigh co moch arnamaireach d'fhaicsin an chroinn sin, & atconnairc a barr fair.
Tainic co tric tindesnach co tempul Dean ar na fothracud fo tri a sruth Lathain, & rouai ag edarguidhi Dean, & is ed roraidh:
‘A bainndei,’ ar si, ‘a Dean, is am banselcairi-si bunaidh duit, & is duit roidhbrais mo mhac id_est Partanapeus, & guidim-si tusa fon mac sin do tabairt co coscrach, & cipindus bes trá a torrachtain hecin cugum, co facar e.
Et innis dam in at firu na fisi atconnarc?
madh firu, tabhair bas sochraid do mo mhac, & cuma taisci fis mo bais-si cuigi-sium.’
Atconnairc-si altoir Dean, comdis fliuch iad do deraib, & rouai aga nglanadh.
O 'dconnairc, immorro, in baindei Dean sin, tainic rompi dochum na Téue dar sleib Menail & dar mullach tsleibi Parnars, no co tarla Apaill dei na faistine di, & co ndebairt ria:
‘Rofetar-sa do toisc, a ingen,’ ar sé, ‘id_est do saerud Partanapeuis a cath na Teue ar na radha da mathair rit.
Acht chena is dimain duit-si sin, uair tainic crich tsaogail an gille sin, & ni fetann tiachtain ri toicthi.
Et in faicci misi co toirsech d'eis in ríghsagairt Aimpiaruis, & nir-ua tualaing me a adnacul?’
Rofrecair Dean, & is ed roraidh:
‘Uair is cinnti,’ ar sí, ‘is cóir damsa fortachta arin fer sin & a aife ar inti ros-muirfe.’
Et tuc cach dith poic da ceiliu, & tainic Dean rompi co Teibh, & conici an inadh ar-maibh-si cloinn Neobe fecht riam roime.
Imthusa na n-Grec & na Tiabanda, immorro, nir-gabh confadh catha a mac samla sin riam roime iat, uair ua hadhbul tairpthige & tindenus na Tiabanda do digail Ipseuis ar na Grecaigh.
Ba mó immorro fich & ferc na ngasraíd n-Grec do dhigail Ipomedoin arna Tiabandaib, coma tren cridheda can teiched caich o cheliu dibh.
Is andsin rogres Partanapeus, ri óc na hArcaide, a ech dian dimsach dasachtach iter na sluagaibh.
Et is amlaidh douai int ech & croicenn tiugh tigri uimpi a comardha coscair.
Ba hé eirred in righ sin ui fuirre id_est lene coem cor-cairglan ar na deghdathad a tenta ba lia, & inar orsnaith ilbrec re cnis doroine a mathair dó re techt don turus sin, & cris socair seimidhe tairis a muigh a n-echtair ar na ilecar do lecaib loghmora, & sciath capradhach cromm air, & cloidim trom trenbuillech 'na laim.
Cimus alaind ordha ac comdrud a edaig uime na gabad luth láma dó, soighedbolc suaichnich sarechtach, & cathbarr slemon slabradhach fo cenn, & rochuir-sium de é, & roleic a trilis taidhlig tromcais ri tincur na greine, coma sochain ri sillad do cach duine a taithnemh na trillsIsin ua cenn.
Et ua ferrde delbh an gille sin in fiuchadh ferci dus-fainic dó isin uair sin.
Et ge rrouai-sium amlaidh sin, tucsat na Tiabanda faill frithailme air.
Roleicsit inudh lathrech do ar a óici & ar a anarsaidheacht leo.
Rouai-sium immorro co dur dasachtach aca dianscailiudh an dara fecht & rouai co tenntomaith-mech ac a timsugud an fecht araill.
Rouatar tra mná na Tiabanda a hinadaib arda oirechtais ac molad & ac measnugud gnimraid in gille oig sin.
O 'dconnairc immorro Dean eisium fon samla sin, is ed roraidh:
‘Is truagh & is doilig lium, a gille,’ ar si, ‘an buaidred baisi for-atai, uair ní fetar ca furtacht dober fort, & rob usa duit a beth ac seilc araon rit mathair a fidhnemedaib Neim ina beth a n-irgail catha fon samlai sin.
Et is tren gresis do mathair misi atrasda 'mat fortacht.’
Et o roui-si ac an comradh sin, tainic neill diamair dluith tairis co lormedon an catha dochum an gille, & dobean a soighedbholc amach, & tuc soighdi cumdachta do do na tabartha urchur n-imruille itir, & rochraith sug amro isi for a ech co na gebdais airm hí.
Is andsin innsaigidh Partanapeus uan samlaIsin uana s--luaghaib, amal cuilen letarthach leoman ua tretaibh teithmeacha, acht ní fetar a airem a dorchratar do Tiabandaib da laim genmótha a tamoin & a toisigh, & at e andso a n-anmanna daine dibh id_est Corebus mac Tanagra & Eirictonius anriata, & Argus ard érérgna, & Lamis lanalaind, & Lidus lanchomachtach, uair ua sacart, & Aalan uasal arsata a Eboia.
Cidh tra acht ni hurchar n-imroill tuc, & rosoighedh re sail a cheile uaidh, & cuidh an duine rochreitfedh coma a haonuolc no a henuogha doteilcthea na saitheda soighed dotheilcedh an trenfer sin?
Uair is cuma congontis & conferdis uadh na frasa sin da culaib & da aigid & do cach taibh de.
As andsin tra roinnsaighsit na Tiabanda Partanapeus, uair nir miadh leó can a digail fair na huilc doroine Et is é dotreninnsaigh dibh ar tús é id_est Ampion do bunadhceneil Ioib mic talchair Satuirnn, & is ed roraid ris:
‘A Partanapeuis,’ ar sé, ‘is mór in diumus & in dasachtacht rogab ac cur áir na Tiabanda, uair nir miadh ri milid no ri trenfer dith comlond rit ar th' oici & ar th' anarsaidhecht.
Facaibh in cath, & imigh co hArcait & dena cluiche re do comais; no mad móo a clú let, dofaeithis linne isin cath so.’
O 'dcuala immorro Partanapeus sin, doraidh:
‘Ní don cinedh techmech Tiabanda am mathair mná damsa itir,’ ar sé, ‘acht is don cinedh Athlanta feramail Aircedach.’
Ni fuilgid tra Ampion sin do cloisdecht, & dorat rothrénurchur do sleig dighuinn dermair rouai 'na laim dochum Partanapeuis.
O 'dconnairc Partanapeus dellrad na sleigi dia innsaigid, roimgaibh co hathlum i, & roleic ant sleg sechai.
Ua moidi ferc Ampion urchur n-imroill do tabairt dó.
Et o rouatar amhlaidh sin, tainic Dean ar lár in catha d'foiridhin Partanapeuis, & roghabh delbh Doreis do Grecaib fuirre, uair ua he-sseic ua hoidi teglaig do Partanapeus, & is dé roathain a mathair é ri techt don turus sin, & o rogab-si a dhelbh-sam fuirri, is and atbert ri Partanapeus:
‘Is lór ar-lenais do Tiabandaibh, a gille,’ ar sé, ‘& eirigh imlan dochum na mara ó tancais d'enech na ndei.’
Nír-gabh-sam amh cuigi sin, & is ed roraidh:
‘A fhir cumtha, a Doirsis,’ ar se, ‘leic dam co romarbar anti rom-gonaid id_est Ampion, & ní lenam na Tiabanda ni bhus mhó; & o rofaeth lium é, dober a ech & a édach do Dean, & dober a soigheduolc do mo mathair.’
Et ó roraidh-sium sin, dofoillsiged dó Uenir banndei Deana do beth ac cungnam ri Greca, & rogreis a lennan id_est Mairt mac Ioib, dei in catha, co ndechsad d'furtacht na Tiabanda.
Uair doui Ermione, ingen Mairt & Uenir, senmathair na Tiabanda, & is de sin roleig in crodha cathcumachtach id_est Mairt dochum Deana, & ó rosiacht, rouai acc aithisiugud na hingine co mór, & is ed doraidh ria.
‘Ní commórad catha na irgaile no gaiscid is let-sa do denum, a Dheán,’ ar sé, ‘acht soighde cathalaind sealca do dhiubrucud.’
Et tainig co tai d'anacul id_est Partanapeuis.
Et tainic 'na ndiaidh sin Mairt do gresacht na Tiabanda a cenn na n-Grec.
Et is é dogres dibh ar tús id_est Drias mac Arion, & roimir in gille sin a gnim gaiscedach ar na hArcaidechaibh & ar hoirechtaibh ar chena rouatar araon ri Partanapeus ac cur in catha sin.
Et ní tuc Drias taisi na tess andsin ac sluighi na sluagh, uair ua demin leis, ce madh athscith n-engnuma é, rotaesadh Partanapeus da laim.
Partanapeus, immorro, ruc a engnum uadh na derbhairedha urbadacha ó rodeilig Deana ris id_est a nert do tercugud, & a soighiduolc d'folmagud d'urchuraib dimaine, & dellrad sceith Driais iter na sluagaibh aca sluighi.
Rogab adhfhuath mór Partanapeus dona gnimaib sin, & rochuir a sreang an slait sodiubraici 'na laim, cer-ua dimain dó; uair intan roui ac cur na soighdi ar in sreing, as ann tuc Drias dasachtach do Tiabandaibh urchur do shleig uillig aghmair rouai 'na laim, cur-ua taobhtholl treghdai an toebh co 'raill andsin Partanapeus, mac Meliager, ri cathbuadach na Calidoine; & is é in Meliager sin ua comalta comgaiscid do Theis, mac Eigh, mic Neptain.
Roiterdeligther re each & re armaib é, & nir-toirind Drias an laim, co tuc urchur don ech, co rrothesc & co rrotrenletair a sirigh, & is cumai tuc Drias na hurcharu sin & torchair fen co dianmarb fo cétoir.
Fo hingnad immorro leosum sin, uair ní fetatar cia ros-marbh.
Acht chena is í Dean ros-marbh a ndigail Partanapeuis, amal rogell thúas da mathair, co ndigheolad a mac ar inti ros-marbfedh.
O torchair tra Partanapeus, rotocatar a munter leo é a n-inad diamair doimtheachta do taibh in muighi; & ger-u anfonn rouai-sium andsin, ní hiat a cnedha fen roacain, acht rouai Caledonda lan cumtha ac cainedh a eich do marthadh.
Acht chena tancotar airdhedha bais de innsaighidh fen; uair tainic duibhi & dodhealbh da ghnuis and, ger-ua glangruadh corcra conuigIsin é.
Et roshilestar frassa forgranna fola dar a chorp sithghel snechtamail isin uair sin, & tainic failte & menfudh & medharglór dó, & is i timna contacair uó dheoigh:
‘A Doirsis,’ ar sé, ‘uair dotuitius-sa andso, imthigh-si dochum dingna mo mathar truaighi-si toirsighi, & na hadaim di a cétoir m'oidhedh d'faghuail damsa, & intan toicceua m'arm & m'edach dí, & abair ria rodligius-sa m'oidhedh da fhaghuail, uair is dar sarugud-si & dar ainneoil na ndei tanac dochum in catha-sa, & na denaid duba na domenmha don scel, & beir let mo trilis dí a n-inad commordha m'oidhedha, & abair ria can m'airm & can mo coin do leicedh do nech ele, acht a mbeth aici fen, & ibair fen na hairm-si fuilet im laim uait do Dean.’
Et a haithle na timnaIsin roscailed a anum re a corp dó a cétoir.
As andsin tra rotindesnaigh Ioib mac Satuirnn maithi móra d'innsaigidh na sluag sin do toirmesc a tachair.
Acht chena ní hair mhaithi re Grecu no ri Tiabanda dorinni-sium sin acht d'foiridhtin na cined coem comidech rodilcennaig and maroen Ua hadhfhuathmar tra re aitrebh magh na Teue isin oidhchi sin, uair rofacbad and mileda cona muntir arna marbad, & urrigha cona oirechtaib arna n-oirlig, & taisigh cona trenferaib arna tuitim, & airm arna daighbrisedh, & eich deghredhtha arna ndianmarbad ar-conighdis fo cairpthib curata tús in lai roime.
As andsin rodeiligset na sluaigh sin id_est na Tiabanda co tighibh, & Grecaigh, in laechraid letarthach, co longphortaib.
Et ger-ua cumgai na doirsi dona deghsluagaibh sin ac dul dochum an catha, ba lethna lanfairsinga ac techt uadha re himut a n-esfadha.
Rouai dono gredhan & gubai adhual ac cechtarnai dibh sin.
Ua hadhual subha re Tiabanda in cetar ríg do Grecaibh do marbad et a sloigh ar sechran da n-eisi id_est Ampiaraus & Tit & Ipomedon & Partanapeus.
Rosiachtatar na Tiabanda na cathracha, & is i comairle rocinnsit, forairedha & forcoimet do chur uathaib ar loncphortaith na n-Grec isin oidhchi sin, ar bithin nach helodis uatha.
Et is iad dochuaidh don coimed sin id_est Meighis mileta & Licus laechdha cona munteraibh.
Et rucsat fleda fína & tinnti leó.
Et rouai Etiocles, rí na Teue, aca nertadh, & is ed roraid riu:
‘Denaid calmacht, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘& métaigidh bar menmanna, & comedaid co maith anocht na Grecaigh, & is leibh a coscur & a comaidhem, uair dothoitsit a rígha id_est Ampiaraus uasalsagart & Tithius trenmilid & Ipimedon airedha.’
Et nir-airimh-sium Partanapeus, uair ua nair leis-sium a oige & a tuitim le Tiabanda.
‘Ocus ní fhuil dibh anoisi itir,’ ar sé, ‘acht mad in senoir anuonn Adrast, & in gille óg can engnam Polinices, & in duine dasachtach Capaneus mac Tairsis, & cid iat sec,’ ar sé, ‘romairbfidhe uile, mina tisadh an aiged fai.’
Et o roraidh Eitiocles an aithesc sin re lucht na foraire, roeircetar co hathlam ettrócar can oirisim ce rouatar a mná & a muntera aca fastodh, no co rancatar a comfhoccus don longphort sin na n-Grec, & rouatar co fuirechair ac fledhugud andsin an dá la conici sin.
Dala uantrachta & uanndala na n-Grec tar eis a fer, is andsin dorindsead idbarta onoracha a templaib uaisli Iunainde do rochtain a fer co cosgrach slan somenmnach da n-indsaigid, & rabadar 'ca cuimnechad do Iunaind cach doronsad na Tiabanda Et ni fidir-si cid dodenad uime sin, acht is i comairli doroine, cumsanadh & codlad d'furalam arna Tiabanda isinn aidchIsin do rochtain a marabtha dona Grecaib.
Et is andsin rochuir bancumachtaig da muintir uaithi id_est Iris, dochum dea an chodalta id_est Somnus.
Et o rasiacht Iris co tigib suanamla Somnais, is ed roraid ris:
‘Adubairt Iunaind rit,’ ar si, ‘a Shomnais, suan & sirchodlad d'furail ar na Tiabandaib eter amuich & tall.’
Raerig immorro Somnus do denam an gnima sin, & rothuit a codlad co trom trenmeirtnech ar na Tiabanda in cach inad a mbadar, con rabadar uili co mertnech midlaechda 'na suanchodalta.
Na Gregaig, immorro, rabadar seig co fuireachair fergach ar tí na Tiabanda robai 'na timcheall, & antan robadar amlaid sin, raeirig Tiodomas mac Menilampuis in shagairt celmanaig do Gregaib, & is eiseig rohordaigeadh a n-inad Ampiarauis aca-sam, & ragab ar faisdine dona Gregaib, co tangadar uili a n-eninad 'mon airdrig 'ma Adraist do denam a comairli, & ba toirrseach cumthach iad-sam ac fegadh inad falam na rig romarbad da muintir.
Is andsin trá roeirig in celmanaigtheoir cumachtach, id_est Tiodomus, do gresacht na sluag, & is ed roraidh:
‘Rodilsigsed na déi daib trá na Tiabanda isinn aidchi-si nocht, & rothogaib Ampiaraus uasal cend damsa, & is ed roraidh ribsi bar muinter do digailt anocht ar na Tiabanda, uair is cindti daib a coscur do chur, & cen co dech nech aili and, rachadsa.’
Lasin ngresacht sin tra roeirgedar co hathlam ainnindeach trein & taisig na n-Greg.
Acht chena is andsin rothog Tiodomas an trichait trenmiled ba ferr leis do Gregaib.
Et ba hé a nduthracht uili na Greg isin uair sin trenfhobairt na Tiabanda, & adubradar cert crandchair do chur aturra, uair ba hé a roga cach aein fo leith dib comadh hé risad ar tus na Tiabanda.
Is andsin roeirig Adraist airdri, & asbert:
‘Anaid, a firu,’ ar se, ‘& is lor uathad do thabairt a n-air, & rachmaid uili re soillsi an lai da fobairt.’
Asa haithlIsin trá roeirig an fisid fireolach Tiodomas & Agilleus mac Earcail maraen ris.
Ba hindamail da athair an gilla sin, & Echtor uasal, uair ni roibi Gregda ba glicca inas, & deichnibar maraén ré cach fer dib sin.
Is andsin rochuir Tiodomas a eirrid suaichnidh de a n-ucht in airdrig Adraist.
Et ragab a chathbarr & luirig Polinixes moir mic Eidip ime.
Ragab dono Acthor anrata claidium Chapaneuis ina laim.
Rug immorro Agillus mac Earcail airm Nomis nemnig leis, uair nir-ba cuibdi cathaigthi leis isin aíti saigdi Ercail rabadar aigi fein.
Et a haithlIsin rolingsed an lucht sin co hathlam tar mullach muir an longphuirt amach, uair nir-b ail leo fuaim na ndorus n-umaidi aga n-oslugad do cloisteacht.
Et gairid dochuadar antan fuaradar na firu meascda medar-chodaltaecha, ‘A Gregda,’ ar se Tiodomas, ‘nach iad so lucht rabai ac forbais foraib?
is urusa daib anosa a dhigail orra.’
Et rabean a chlaidim asa thinntig, & tainig tresna sluagaib, & rabai 'ga slaigi & 'ca marbad co na fetar airim a n-airimi na cuimniugud comand a curad adorchair andsin re Tiodomas.
Uair dofhagaib-sium and laich ar na lanmarbad 'na cosrachaib, & curaid ar na comach a crislach a sciath, & treinfhir ar na tuargain a leapthaib feoir & fidnemid.
Rabadar dono na dei adartha andsin, ag cungnam re Gregaib, & ag tescad ar na Tiabandaib.
Agilleus, immorro, mac Earcail, nir-ba luga na hara dochuir ar na Tiabandaib, & rabai 'ca ndithubadh & 'ca ndilgend, no co tarla Palameinus ceolbind cruitiri na Tiabanda dó a haithli oirfidthe dona sluagaib; & nir-fhogain a binnius do-sin, ar adorchair a chetoir do laim mic Earcail.
Gid Echtair, dono, nir-bo tlaith a thres ac trenmarbad na Tiabanda co torchair Tamiris trenchalma do Tiabandaib do laim.
Rothuit dono Eitiocles do Tiabandaib re Tagus do Gregaib.
Rabai Palpitus do Tiabandaib 'na tromchodlad eter chuingib an charpaid no co riacht Tiodomas do Gregaib chuigi, & ba he duscad tug air beim claidim do thabairt dó cor-bá taman mael da eiss.
Rabadar amlaid sin ag trénmarbad na Tiabanda, no co tainig irdered na haidchi chucu, & adchondairc Eachtor amaindsech do Gregaib sin.
Ragairead Tiodomas chuici, & is ed doraid ris:
‘Is lor,’ ar se, ‘an coscur rugsamar, uair torchratar lind an ba hinmarbtha andso do Thiabandaib, & denam imtecht risin coscur cathbuadach-sa rugsamar.’
Rafhaem Tiodomas sin, & rabai ag admolad bandei na haidchi id_est Pebi, ar an coscur tug doib isinn aidchi sin.
Et cach coscur oidchi beris cach is tre impidi na bandei sin, Pebe, iar sithsenchasa gentligi.
Et rogeall di co n-idberad do cethraib di coimlín ar-marb do sluagaib andsin, & roimpadar co subach sirforfhailid leisna gnimaib sin dochum a longphuirt.
Et dobadar da milid mornemnacha aco-som andsin id_est Opiliius do muinntir Thid, mic rig na Cailidoni, & Dimas do muinntir Partanopeuis rig na hArcaidegda, & nir ferr di leisin dis sin beith beo tar eis a tigernadh, & doraidh Opliius re Dimas:
‘A fir chumtha,’ ar se, ‘in olc lat ind do thigerna id_est Partanopeus, a corp do beith fa conaib & ethaidib na Teibi?
Acht chena is tren romthraid-sea & chraides mo cridi mo thigerna fein do beith amlaid id_est Tid, mac rig na Cailidoine; & na rach-sa beo co Cailidoin can a chorp-sum do beith lium.’
‘Truag dono sin,’ ar Dimas, ‘is am toirrsigi-si tar eis mo tigerna ina cach duine, & rachad-sa andsin gé dechair-si cen co dechair.’
Is andsin dochuadar rompo d'iarraid in armaigi do thabairt chorp a tigernad leó, & robadar 'ca n-iarraid no cor-eirgedar ruithned greine glanshoillse arnamarach, & cor-ba leir daib cach lanradarcc umpo.
Et is and fuair cach fer dib corp a thigerna, & rothogbadar leo iad ana n-oireadaib firmora furmid, & dochuadar rompo co tái toirrseach tindesnach dochum a longphuirt.
Ba doilig leo immorro lanshoillsiugud an laí da tarrachtain ag na gnimaib sin.
An tan tra rosiachtadar a gcomfhogus a longphuirt, adcualadar fogur bres & fothrand mór ina ndiaidh.
Et is é robaí andsin Ampion do Thiapandaib cona dirim ndegsluaig maraen ris, ar nach curdis na fairaireda, & dothaiscelad ar longphort na n-Greg isin maidin mochrach, & adcondairc Ampion andsin do Gregaib & curpu na curad forra, & rotrengreis a each no co ruc forra, & is ed doraid riu:
‘Fuirgid, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘co findam cia sib.
Acht chena is follus duind foraib cur-a bidbaid do Thiabandaib sib.’
Is andsin dobai cach dibsium ag tindenus seoch aroili ré heagla Aimpioin.
Acht chena ni daib fein dob eagail leo ní, acht na cuirp crodcrechtnaigthi rabadar for a muin d'fagbail.
Rabaí dono Ampion Tiabanda ag tomaithem mor forro, & tuc urchar don fhir robaí ar tus dib id_est do Dimas, cor-thuit an sleg can aigbeile ina fhiadnaisi.
Is andsin tainig an milid mormenmnach Ifitus do Thiabandaib, & tuc fuirmed seidrech sarchalma sleigi ar Opleiius ara roibi corp Tid, cor-bris a druim and, & co rotregd corp Tit robai ara muin co rotorchair don goin sin.
Rathsill immorro Dimas dara ais, & adcon-daircc imarcraid na Tiabanda ag tromlaigi air, & ni fhidir an maithem n-anacail roshirfed, no an comland dochuirfed Acht chena isi comairli dorigne.
Rochuir de an corp rabai fair id_est corp Partanopeuis, & rochuir a craicend tren tigrigi robai uime ina laim chlí, & a claidim lainderta lasamain ina laim deis, & doimpo fan samla sin risna sluagaib amal leoman lanfhergach risna gabaid gaisgedaig arna chrad 'ma chuilenaib, conid cuma leis bas & betha d'fagbail.
