Imacomraig do andsin & Ampion airsid Tiabanda re hag & re hirgail, & tug Ampion andsin beim claidim do Dimas, cor-ben a lam clí comnairt 'ga gualaind de, & rothairrngedar na Tiabanda corp Partanopeuis uadh.
O 'dchondairc-sium immorro sin, robai co truag toirrseach ag iarraid chuirp ag iarraid a tigerna orra, & asbert ríu:
‘Ar na deib rib, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘denaid faelleas risin corp tairrngtai, & tabraid mo chorp-sa d'enaib & do eathaidib, uair is cora ina an corp fuil agaib.’
Is andsin doraid Ampion ris-sium:
‘Leigfigther corp do thigerna duid, & leigfigther tú fein as mar tai, da mbraite & da treigtea na Gregaig damsa.’
Rafhregair Dimas dosum, & is ed doraid:
‘Ní dingnind-si, trá sin, gidead roanced mo thigerna 'na bethaid, & mé fein can olc do buain rium.’
Et is cuma adbert-sam sain & roleig a ucht & a urbruindi 'ma claidim n-urnocht, co fuair bas and fo chetoir.
tra acht rothuitsed amlaid sin id_est Opleiius & Dimus, tre cuibdi a comaid amal rothuitset tall Nisus & Euriallus do Throigiandaib a marloinges Aeniass antan romarbsad munter Tuirn an dara fer dib, amal indister ar loinges Aenias. Et asa haithlIsin dochuir Ampion fesa uad co Teib d'indisin na scel sin innti, & dochuaid fein roime d'forbaisi ar longfort na n-Greg & do thogbail na cenn sin doib.
Is andsin dochonncadar na Greig chucu Tiodomas ramarb na foraireada, & sé subach sirforbfaeilid ag comaidem na ngnim doroine, & tugad leosam ilacha aithise & gairi comaidme is maraen ris, & antan robadar amlaid sin ag comaidim a coscair, is and romothaigsed Opliius & Dimus do beith 'na n-ingnais.
Rafhas guba & geran aco, o na facadar na firu sin.
Imtusa Aimpion Tiabanda, immorro, tainig roime no co riacht a comfhogus don longphort, & o 'dchonnairc na hara aidbli dona Tiabandaib, rosocht air co mor, co nar-b athlam ré himtheacht, & co nar-ba cubaid comraith ré méd na cumad dos-fanig iga faigsin, & roimpo a chetoir andsin, & tainig ar culu dochum na Tebi.
Imtusa na n-Greg, immorro, roeirgedar co hathlam agarbh dar doirrsib a longfuirt do dul dochum na Tiabanda, & is and dochuatar tré lár in armuig tucadar a munter isinn aidchi reime sin.
Ba subach tra íad-sam 'ca faicsin amal dotoglaidis tigi & treaba na Tiabanda uile.
Is andsin ronert Capaneius gasrada Greg um dul do thren-fobairt na Teibi, & as ed adbert ríu:
‘Eirgid, a oga,’ ar se, ‘maraen riumsa, uair as fada atú can mo bladh & can mo mornert do thogbail ag togail na Teibi.
Uair is í mo deslam daithgel daingean is dee damsa, & is é mo chlaidem cruaid curata as cumachtach dam.’
Et o raraid-sium sin, rochoimeirig Adraist ant airdrig co croda curata, & Poilinicseis mor mac Eidip id_est loingsech na togla, & Tiodomas mac Meinelampuis, & da mac Iasoin mic Easoin id_est Toas & Aeunios, & Agelleus mac Earcail.
Et tangadar co tren mórtindesnach co muraib na Teibi, & antan rangadar an cathraig, is and dobai Ampion echtach aga indisin dona Tiabandaib a faraireadha do marbad dona Gregaib.
Et doriachtais andsin gasrada Greg can rathubad co mbeidis ar lar na Teibi, minbad an milid menmnach Megareius d'iachtad & d'eigim forra do muraib na cathrach, & is ed doraidh:
‘Duntar & daingnigter lib, a firu,’ arse, ‘doirrsi bar cathrach, & ataid bar namaid da bar n-indsaigi id_est sloig menmnacha na n-Greg.’
Is andsin doeirgedar na Tiabanda, & roiadsat doirrsi a cathrach a chédoir, acht aendorus nama id_est Ogis; & dosiacht Etion do Tiabandaib a aenur da iadad a n-agaid na n-Greg, & antan robai 'ca dunadh, rathriallsad ogbaid arnaid Spartana dul tairis ar eigin.
Is andsin rofhobair Eichion co feramail iád, co rathuitsed treínfhir ar tairrseach an dorais do thres an Tiabanda sin daib id_est Eicion.
Is iad so fa ferr dothuit andsin do Gregaib do laim Eichion id_est Panapes a telchaib tondglasa Taigeit, & an snamaigi soinemail o sruth Oureota id_est Ebalus, & ant airsid engnamach Alcidamas.
Et fa tren a tres an lochta sin ar tairsig na Teibe, gein no co riachtadar an dias so do Tiabandaib d'foirithin Echioin id_est Acron & Almentes, cor-iadsad ar eigin an dorus.
Et bá hadbal easbaid ceachtar an dá sluag sin, uair rofagbaid drem do Thiabandaib ré dorus amuich ré teindesnaigi rohiadad an baili.
Rabadar dono drem thall do Gregaib can rochtain amach dochum a munntiri, uair dothuitsed thall isin baili gaiscedaig do Gregaib id_est Ormenus & Amantur, & rodichendad leosan an gilla sin, uair is amlaid robai & muintorc alaind orda 'ma braigid.
Imtusa, immorro, na n-Greg, rothogladar & rodianscaileadar mur n-imeallach na Teibi risin ré sin, & rodruidsed andsin curaid & coisigida na n-Greg a comfhogus do muraib na cathrach.
Uair ní roichdis a n-echrada tar na clascaib coimlethna robadar 'na thimcheall.
Rabadar dono na Tiabanda ag daingniubad a cathrach, coma hadbal fuaimnech na sabad ag suidiugud tresna slabradaib ag drud & ag dluthubadh na comlad n-adbal n-umaidi ré doirrsib clochta comdaingne na cathrach.
Rabadar dono drem do Gregaib andsin ag dibragad soigead teintigi a mullaigib tor & tiged na Teibi da loscad.
Rabadar dono drem ele dib 'ca togail & 'ca tollad asa hichtar & sceallbord do sciathaib 'na timcheall.
Ralinsad immorro na Tiabanda taibleda na Teibi do didin na tor & na tigead.
Raba doilig fulang fuithib isin uair sin, ar imad arm n-examla ag dibragad uaithib dochum na n-Greg.
Ratheilgsed slega suainmecha sodibraigthi, & soigde imluatha eitecha, & clocha cruaidi comamais, & mill lanmora luaidi; & ba he an dlus na fras sin rotheilgsed na Tiabanda ag didin a cathrach, cor-bó comdluith ré cethaib cruaidi clothneachta a n-airm & a n-ilfhaebair ag buain dar aigthib sciath & dar cathbarraib cruaidi na n-Greg.
Ní har time na ar teichead dochuaid sin dona Gregaib.
Acht tugsad a n-aigthi co dluith & co dichra re cnis na cathrach, & robadar 'ca trentogail.
Is andsin dorala Anteius croda curata do Gregaib timcheall na cathrach, co tarla sleg trom Tiabanda 'na uchtbruindi da indsaigid, co rasráin asa charbad amach é, co rabadar a chosa a llenmain a rothaib & a refedaib an charbaid, & cor-timchill an cathraig fon samla sin, & co fuair bas arsin.
O 'dchondcadar immorro na Greig sin, tugsad gair badba buaidirthi os aird, & roseindid a sduicc croda cathaigthi leó, & roroindsead a sluaga ider doirrsib na Teibe, & robadar 'ca dianscaileadh.
Ba hadfhuathmar tra re heisteacht isinn uair sestan & seisseilbi na Tiabanda sechnon na sencathrach ar med na heagla ros-gab risin trenfhobairt tucsad na Greig 'na timcell, & rolinsad tigi & teampaill na cathrach sin, & robadar ag duba & ag domenmain & ig imraitib ilearda atarra.
Et dobadar drem dib andsin 'ca rada an rigi do thabairt do Poilinicseis ré head na bliadna sin & Eitiocleis do cur ara char & ar indarba uaithib.
Adubairt drem eili dib nar-bo choir an comairli sin, & gid hí donidis, na gebad Polinicseis uaithib, no co tairsed forra cach egoir doronsad ris.
Acht is fair desid leo a fisid fhireolach da thabairt da n-indsaigi id_est Tiresias, & firinde faistine do denam doib.
Is andsin doerig Tiresias, & doraid ré a ingin id_est re Manta:
‘Dena altoir idbarta duind, a ingen, & fhado teinti.’
Et dorigne in ingen sin, no co tairnig lé.
Is andsin adces taidbsi nathrach ar barr uachtarach na lasrach roeirig dona teintib, & is tresin ngnim sin rothuig Teresias fuagrad na faistine, & rahadnad é andsin o fhis & o fhaistine.
Et is ed doraidh risna Tiabanda:
‘Da nderntai cach ní ader-sa rib, bud lib coscar don chur-sa id_est in duine as só do síl Chaithim, mic Aigenoir, d'idbairt dona deib, & dobad mó cin don duine sin fortacht & foirithin d'fadbail dona Tiabandaib trena bithin.’
Adchualaid sin Creon curata do shil calma Caithim, & ragab eagla mór hé ar bithin, uair doshail comad hé a mac fein nohidbortha andsin id_est Menetius.
Uair fa hé sin fa só aco-sam don shil rigda do claind Chaithim mic Aiginoir.
Et adbert Créon andsin risin fisid:
‘Ceil an gnim sin,’ ar se, ‘& na labair ní as mó é.’
Rabai immorro an fisidh 'na thasd ar sin.
Et o rabái, ragabsad Tiabanda uili a n-aenfhecht lama air um thuilleadh fhís do denam doib.
Raeirig andsin Teresias & a ingen Manta, & ragabsad fial falaid tairsib, no co riachtadar co hairm a roibi Meneitius mac Creoin, & is and robái an gilla i dorus do doirsib na cathrach & dirmata diairmigthi do Gregaib ar na toitim leis & Emon echtach a brathair ag cathugud araen ris andsin a comais ar chena.
Ni roibi dib nech bad aili na bad erergna inas an gilla sin id_est Minceius, & asbert andsin ris Manto ingen Tiresiais:
‘A gilla,’ ar si, ‘ataid na dei 'cot iarraid dod t'idbairt daib tar cend na Tiabanda uili, & fagaib an corp tromda talmanda atai, uair is ferr duit beith i nn-ingnaib roglanaib richid ar t'edparid dar cend t'atharda.’
Rafaem-sam trá sin on ingin, uair ba maisi leiss a oiged fein ar socar d'fadbail da athardaib, & tainig roime co tindesnach co larmedon an baili d'agallaim a mathar & a athar.
Et o rainig, robái a athair 'ga agallaim, & is ed roraid ris:
‘A mic,’ ar se, ‘na herig in turus teigi, uair is breg uili cach ní raidis Teresias rit.’
Nir-faem immorro Menetius anad, ge rabai a athair aga fhastod, & tug ceilg ima a athair, & is ed doraid ris:
‘Ní risin toisc sin triallaim dul itir,’ ar se, ‘& ní hed rom-greisfed Tiresias da rad rim.
Acht is ed roimluaid mo brathair do guin do Gregaib id_est Emon, & a nirt eisimail tugsad uaithib he, & erigid-siu 'na agaid, uair is comfogus bas dó, & ag so misi d'iarraid an primlega id_est Eicion da indsaigid.’
Radeiligsead amlaid sin, & tainig Creon roime co cumthach cuntabartach d 'iarraidh a mic eli.
Meníceius immorro o radealaig a athair ris amlaid sin, tainig roime co tricc tindesnach no co ndechaid ar mur na cathrach, & o rasiacht, ralabair o soine gotha moir, & is ed asbert:
‘A dei da tabraim-si me fein,’ ar se, ‘tabraid eigin coscar an chatha & an tachair-si uaib do Thiabandaib.
Toirrnid & trascraidh gasrada gruadhglana Grec ar co taethsad leo-sum iád.’
O daraid-sium sin, roleig eislind a chuirp 'ma chruad-rind a chlaidim coma forderg fuilidi mur na cathrach da fuil & da indib.
Rugsad na Tiabanda a chorp chucu anund isin cathraig, & rafhagsad hé a tig a athar ar ndenam a admolta, a cheapoigi caintige, & dochuadar rompo dochum an chatha ar sin.
Raeíg, immorro, & roiacht a mathair os cind an gilla, & is ed roraid:
‘Ba dimain damsa trá a mhic,’ ar si, ‘m' aileamain co honorach ort, & nir chosmail mo chlann & clann colach Iochasta, ge ramarbad mo mac-sa & a mic-si co slan id_est Eidiocleis & Polinicseis.’
Et robaí-si ar na himraitib sin no co tangadar a munnter da hindsaigi & go rugsad leo ana tech leptha hí, & rabadar 'ca coimdingnad and.
O rabadar na Tiabanda risna gnimaib sin, rogreis an trenmilid Capaneius gasraid na n-Greg dochum dorais na Teibi, & imasai fein fo na sluaghaib, & rothimchill & rothrascair marcacha na Tiabanda.
Rathanaid & rotrenmarb na curaid concingdis da cois im doirrsib na cathrach.
tra acht fa trascairthi tuir & tigi dona cairrgib comora rodibraigead an trenfer sin isin cathraig, & ba brathbristi buidne da bemindaib claidim an curad sin, & ba suaichinti slesa saerchland arna sarguin ona slegaib roteilgead. Et is ed ba samalta ré Tiabanda andsin coma hiad na secht rigmilid do Gregaib dothuit leó na beidis a n-aenfhecht aga dimchillad & aga trenmarbad donn aenfhuabairt sin tug Capaneius oirtho.
Uair is cuma romarbad iad ider og & shen, mnaib & mindainib, co na handais curaid na cathmilid ara chind do comrag ris, & coma hadfhuath ré cach nduine seal ar-sithsillead ré méd a graine an Gregda sin.
tra acht ní ba tualaing fisid na fireolach admolad echta in fhir sin, mana beidis na dei co duthrachtach 'ca degcuimneachadh daib. Et is é méd na menman rus-gab cun chathugud conar-ba miad na maisi leis tachar ré trebaib an talman acht re deib nuaglana nime.
Et rabái andsin Capaneius ag fegadh arin n-aer n-ard n-anfenach osa chind, & adchondairc da ralaig mbeaca aimreidi comard ré cloich na cathrach a comfhogus dó, & is ed doraid-sium andsin:
‘Ni leigeand am mo mormenma dam,’ ar se, ‘can dreim riu so, co findar ona deib an ba tarba do Thiabandaib an duine ramarbsad 'na n-anoir, & co findar an fuilid na dei fein do niadh no do nirt.’
Et rodring co subach forfailid asa haithlIsin co mullach mur na cathrach.
Sochtais immorro ar Thiabanda 'ca fhaigsin 'na sduaig agmair urbadaig amal nothisadh an la buaidirthi bratha do murad a cathrach 'na cendaib, & gid ead tugsad a n-aigthi air, & rodibraigsed he a tigib & a taibledaib na Tebe do railgib romora & do chlochaib comamais.
Faelait-sium trá na frasa firmora sin confertais na fir fair, & cothaigis and amal charraig coimnert iter buindedaib ruadha rabarta na saebsruth aga sitladh, & o rascuirsed na Tiabanda na frasa sin de, ragab-sam ag tainsium & ag tarcaisi moir forro.
Doraid riu:
‘Cuich ar bad tor,’ ar se, ‘na muir thana Tiabanda-sa do thrasgrad & do thoirnem dochum lair?’
Et cuma adbert sin & rathrascair na crandoga comdaigne claraid & na taidbli deaftha badar bar mur na cathrach a cendaib na Tiabanda, & rabai tra fan samla sin ag trasgrad na Teibi da mur & da mullach.
Is andsin dono robadar caraid chumachtacha na Tiabanda & caraid chumachtacha na n-Greg ag agallaim Ioif, mic Saduirn, & cach dib ag iarraid fhoirithne da charaid.
Is iad trá robai andsin ac congnam ré Tiabanda id_est Apaill uasal, mac Ioif, & Beinir banchumachtach, & Baich brigach borrfadach, & Ercail anrata, mac Ioif.
Is iád immorro rabái ac gabail re Gregaib id_est Iunaind ilchrothach & Menarba morchumachtach, & Pers primeolach mac Ioif, & Dane ingen rig Greg a mathair.
Rabái trá Ioif co firen iter an lucht sin can chungnam ré neach seach aroili dibh gein no co riacht Capaneius he, & is ed doraid Capaneius, uair ní fhuair tachar o Thiabandaib ait a mbaí ar mur a cathrach:
‘Cait a fhuilid itir,’ ar se, ‘dee meta mertnecha na Tiabanda id_est Apaill & Baich & hErcail?
ní da ngresacht,’ ar se, ‘uair ní miadh lium, acht, a Ioif chena,’ arse, ‘as rit-su as dingmala lium tachar, & tarr dom indsaighi, masad cumachtaig ar saignenaib.’
O 'dchualaid Ioif sin, tibis gen gairi, & raidis ar sin:
‘Is granda an gresacht daberi foraind, & is coir t'olc do denam.’
Et asa haithlIsin tug Ioif neoill chiuine comdorcha & tuairseacha tromfleachaidh ar dreich thalman, conar-ba leir tulcha no tigi na Tiabanda isin tan sin.
Et tainig trid sin torand bres bresbratha uas cind na Teibi id_est feib co ngluaised firmaimint asa slatrach & asa suidiugud.
Rabaí immorro Capaneius can gluasacht arin mur risin, gein co rasoillsigsead saignena teintighi ag tuitim ar dreich & ar tuagebair an talman.
Is ed doraid-sium 'ca faigsin:
‘Is coir immorro,’ ar se, ‘tenta mar so d'fhacbail do Thiabandaib, & dogeb-sa aithin-neada adanta & dairgi dossacha ar derglasad anoss da ndibragad doib.’
Et antan rabái Capaneius ag an bogasach briathar sin, darala chuigi soignen crithrech corcorderg, cor-chuir a chathbarr da chend, & co rascailt a sciath o bili co bord, & co rachomlas a chorp fein uile o chind co bond.
Atchondcadar na catha cechtarrda sin, & roscuchsad da cach leith o muraib na cathrach ar imgabail chuirp an churad do thoitim forra.
Et dorochair andsin Capaneius tar mur na Teibi amach, co roib sligi a chuirp ar na loscadh an conair rothuitt do mur na cathrach, & co fhuair bass amlaid sin o saignen Ioif ar in morbrethir doraid ina agaid.
Et rochomlas an mag firalaind ferach ara roibi do lasraig a chuirp.
tra acht fa coir dona cineadaib cuimniugud gnimrad an gilla sin & dona deib a admolad da eis, uair ní toit fer la nert cet curadh min bad dei do dinguail. O darochair tra Capaneius, rochuir Ioif mac Saduirn dorcata do dreich an talman.
Rathimsaigsead na Tiabanda uili co haeninad, & tangadar a mna & a macaim a tigib & a templaib, uair nir-lamsad eirgi coruigIsin re gairbthreas Capaneuis doib.
Rameabaid immorro do Gregaib andsin on chathraig, & cena ni har teithead na Tiabanda sin, acht ar eagla Ioif mic Shaduirn da loscad mar doloisc Capaneius.
O 'dcondcadar milid menmnacha chlaindi Caithim mic Aigenoir sin, ralensad co longphort & co lepthaib iad, & is iad so rolen ar tus iad do Thiabandaib na Gregu id_est Eourimedon óg anrata mac Pain, & Lapidus lanchalma, & a mac maraen ris id_est Alatriius; & rochuirsed na treinfhir sin ara aidbli ar na Gregaib, no co rangadar a longphort.
Et rabadar ag forbais forro iarsin.
Ba hingnad isinn uair sin udmailli na tuicten, & na fir robadar isinn uair roime ag forbais ar na Tiabanda beith daib-sinn ag forbais forro-sam a chedoir o rathuit Capaneius.
Et is iad dothuit ré Tiabandaib 'ma doirrsib an longphuirt sin an ogbaid thangadar a cathraig Ercail a sochraidi na n-Greg no cor-erig ant airsid engnama id_est Enipeius, & co raseind sdocc comairci dona feraib do dul isin longphort anunn ar teithed na Tiabanda, & mar dobái Enipeius ag seinm a sduicc, tarla saigead croda corranach da indsaigid, co rus-fagaib can anmain, & co roibi a sdocc fas ag fogrugud da eis.
Comrag rig na Teibi & rig na togla andso id_est da mac Eidip id_est Poilinicseis mor & Eitiocleis óg anrata.
Is andsin roerig an badb granna geranach thindesnach thuasanach id_est Tisipone, a hichtar ifirn, do thendad & do thinninus na da derbrathar sin a cend aroili id_est Eitiocleis & Polinicseis.
Et o nar-sail-si a rochtain lé a haenar fuailfed feirgi na deisIsin do thabairt os aird, raleig gairm ard adfhuathmar ara síair mengaig míchuirtig id_est Megera, & o 'dchualaid Megera sin, doerig co hathlam a haitib islib an aibne Oirc, & o dariacht dochum a sethar, asbert fria Tisipoine:
‘Misi dochomor na catha cos aníu,’ ar si, ‘iter an lucht sin, & ber-si do roga anois cia dib gresfi dochum an chatha.
Acht chena is cora Eitiocles do legad dam-sa, uair is aigi ata a mathair & a shiur ac astad, & imtig-siu romad dochum longphuirt na n-Grec an loingsig Poliniceis da trengresacht.’
Rascar thrá cach dib re 'roili andsin co firluath foluaimneach, & táinig Megera roimpi dochum Poliniceis, & ragab deilb a bancheili fuirri id_est Argia ingine Adraist.
Et is and dorala Polinices dí go dubach dobronach a ndoras an longphuirt, & snim & sirimradud an chatha co mor ara menmain, & cuma a charat chomaind air id_est Titt mic Aeniasa.
O 'dchondairc-sium andsin Megera, & sí a richt a bancheli, ba hingnad leis, & asbert fría:
‘Cred teigi, a ingen,’ ar se, ‘& ca toirrsi ara-tai?’
Ni thug sí fregra air-sium, & o na tug fregra air, dothuig cur-ba taibsi sin.
Uair nir-shail a bancheili fein do thorachtain o gortaib Greg conuigIsin da indsaigid.
Et gid ead robuaidir an badb sin Polinices coma ferr leis cath & congal d'fagbail isinn uair sin ina rigi & flaithius ar an Teib tondglas cona tuathaib togaidi.
Et rainig roime co tindesnach d'agallaim a clemna id_est Adraisd, & is ed daraid ris:
‘As fada dam-sa,’ ar se, ‘cor-chinnius comairli tar eis mo charad, & dursan nach and doronus comairli & mo brathair an cetla tangadar Greig dochum na Tebi, ré síu dofaetsad a dorchair adraind.
Et dogen-sa anoissi,’ ar se, ‘comrac & Eitiocles, & na toirmisc-siu umma a denam.
Et slainti duitsi, a airdrig, tar m'eis & do maithib na n-Greg ar chena.’
Ba comthoirrseach tra na curaid don cheleabrad sin Poliniceis, & dobai Adraisd 'ca choimdignad & 'ca fhastod, & nir-an-sam aigi, uair dobai an bodb aga buadread id_est Megera, & is ed aderid ris:
‘Na fuirig, a gilla,’ ar si, ‘& ata do brathair Eitiocles agad tograim & ag tindinus do comrag & do comlann rit.’
Is andsin immorro doerig Polinices co tricc tindesnach, & rogreis a each dar muigib minreidhi, no co rainig cathraig na Teibi.
Dala Poliniceis conuigi sin.
Imthusa Eitiocleis rig na Teibi is amlaid dobai ag denam idbarta anorach do Ioib mac Saduirn tar chend choscair do Thiabandaib, & robai ag slondad charadraid Ioif & na Tiabanda.
Et antan rabai amlaid sin Eitiocles ag denam na n-idbart, rosceind crithel chirdub do teinid na hidbarta, co raloisc a chathbarr & ghruad an righ.
Et o robái-sium amlaid sin, tainig techtairi co tren & co tindesnach da indsaigid id_est Efithus, & is ed doraid ré hEtiocles:
‘Toirmisg co luath na hidbarta,’ ar se, ‘& doriacht do brathair co dorus na Teibi dod t'indsaigi, & ata 'cod gairm & 'cod grennachad a aenur do chomrag & do chomland rit.’
Adchualaid immorro Eitiocles sin, & roerig co fergach feramail, & nir-ba miad les an scel doriacht da indsaigid.
Et tangadar andsin chuigi a curaid comlaind & a gnathamais comaidechta, & is ed doraidsed friss:
‘An, a airdrig,’ ar siad, ‘ad rigshuidhi, & bí co fosaidh forbailid, & dingebamaid-ne do bidbaid dit, & rofaeth ante fogres comland fort.’
Acus doriacht andsin Creon cumachtach da indsaigid, & ní do thoirmisc an tachair rothriall, acht rogab for athisib bhriathar do thabairt ar Eitiocles aga tennadh & aga threnghresacht dochum an comlainn.
Acus is ed doraid ris:
‘Ní bí sid na suba isinn atharda-sa,’ ar se, ‘gein bei-si a rigi forra, & is lor lat ar mic-ne & ar mbraithri do thuitim a cathaib & a n-irgalaib dar do chend, & tú fein co timteicheach ar imgabail do brathar, & seisium agad grennubadh-sa a ndorus na cathrach.’
Rafhregair Eitiocles co fichda fergach do Creón, & is ed doraid fris:
‘Ní hí tra cuma do munntiri dobeir ort-su sin da rada, acht dob ail let fein beith isin rigi-si, da faethaind-si isin comrag.
Et, a fhiru,’ ar se, ‘trelmaigi m'armu dam uaib co fheraind comlann & an curad croda ata 'com-gresacht id_est Polinices, & damad coscrach mé on chomlann dotairisinn ar Creon a fhuigell ainindeach egoir.’
Agus in am rabai Eitiocles ar na himraitib sin, is and doriacht a mhathair id_est Iochasta, co hanband acaintech da indsaigid, & a lama langela ar lethad, & a bruinde taitnemach tarrnocht, & intan rosiacht chuigi amlaid sin, is and dobái in gilla ac gabail a arm & a chatherriud comraig & comlaind uime, & a each siblach soérmach ar sibal ina srian a laim a arad ina fhiadnaisi.
Is ed immorro doraid a mhathair ris:
‘Uch, a mhic,’ ar si, ‘ca dasacht rod-gresand do chomrag red bhrathair?
cá leth rachus antí bus coscrach uaib isin comland arm ar marbad aroili?
Et is ma chin da bar n-athair aniu beith a n-ingnais a shúl ré síu beith ag fegad bar comraig & bar comlaind a mhacu.
Et bennacht ort,’ ar si, ‘urderg do laim eisium-sa ar tus & imir bas oram ré siu adcear taeb do bhrathar ruisti rotholl uaid, ina do taeb-so uadha-sum arna tregdad dosan dosam.’
Ba comrath re carraig amh disi sin, & ba robad do breith do troich; uair ge raeist a mac ria, ní rus-faem ní dar-labair ris.
Is andsin tainig in óg fhial ilchrothach id_est Aintigoine, siur na mac sin, can fhis can airiubad do neoch isin cathraig, no co riacht ar mullach an muir, & a haiti cianaesta comairleach maraen ria id_est Forfass.
Et imar thainig sí andsin, adchondairc uaithi a brathair id_est Polinices mor, mac Eidip, ag dibragad tiged na Teibi, & ag crathad na sleg ac sirgrendachadh a brathar.
Et o adcondairc-si sin, iachtais & eigis co hard, & raidis ris:
‘Ar na dee rit, a gilla,’ ar si, ‘toirind t'fheirg, & orchis dod bunadchinel fein.
Et ni bá maith th' fhir chatha idir,’ ar si, ‘tar in ngrendugud doberi ar do brathair, & is eisium robai gus aníu ar anfir, uair dofheimid comraind crichi na feraind duidsi, & dothoirmisc do bhrathair,’ ar si, ‘ar aslach a mathar fair can gliaid & can debaid do denam rit-so.
Et bennacht fortsa, dena-sa oram-sa ar in cairdes fuil adraind ar chena.’
Et o raraid in ingen na briathra banda banamla sin re brathair, tanig taidhlech ar menmain an miled andsin, & toirrnis a arma, & fillis aradna na hechraidi ar culu, & tastais seal ag fegad na ingine.
Et cuma rabadar-sum amlaid sin, ragreis an badb demnach dasachtach Eitiocles a coinde & a comdail a brathar dar dorus na Teibi, co racumscaigid comlada da corranaib, & co rathairrngid urrsanda na cathrach asa coimegur re trodgail na trenmiled ag tindenus araen ré a tigerna dochum Poliniceis.
O rasiacht Eitiocles ar lar na faidchi fondglaissi na Teibe, raraid:
‘A atharda na rig,’ ar se, ‘id_est a Theib thondglas togaidi, is ag antí beres coscar as so aníu as cubaid do beith-siu.’
O 'dchualaid immorro Polinices sin, ní ar time na ar teithed dochuaid dó, acht ar trenindsaigid a bhrathar, & ar tomaithem n-adbal do denam 'na agaid, & is ed doraid:
‘A Eitiocleis,’ ar se, ‘an cumain let can comall caradraid & can chomraind crichi da damthain damsa?
Et ní fír catha agad am agaid-sea idir, & bá cora comland do chur rimsa ní bad thaisci ina torchair do rigaib & do rodainib adraind cosaníu.’
Ba hadbul tra misgais & formad in fhir isin id_est Eitiocleis ag Polinices aga fhaigsin ar a rigdacht concuingeadh dochum an chomraig, uair is amlaid rabái & buidhne diairmigthi degsluaig maraen ris, & cathbarr rigda ruithnigthech 'ma chend, & dillaitt dathchain deigdenmach co n-edaigib caema corcarglana ara eochaib aibind allmurdaib fa chruindsciath taidlech taitnemach fair.
Et ger-ba hadbal re Polinices sin, ba rigda a arm fein & a errid.
Uair is amlaid robai & edach rigda roalaind uime ar na cuma do mnaib minglana Meiginne do ré taidecht don turus sin, & airm suaichinta soineamla leiss ar na shlibadh co slemangér do gaibnib Greg, & each luthmar lanalaind fai.
Et o raindsaigset na hair-sida sin ar aroili, roeirgedar amaidi duaibsechdemnacha fora n-armaib & fora n-echaib id_est Tisipoine ag tindenus Eitiocleis & Megera ag trengresacht Poiliniceis.
Rachrith an bé Neíd a heiteda crithrecha comlasta aca comgresacht, comdais lasracha lanmora taidleach na n-arm aga n-urnochtad agna curadaib dochum araili isinn uair sin, & rochrithnaig an talam trenadbal amal rothuitid asa hait & asa hinad ré taicim na trenfer sin dochum araili.
Raeirgedar andsin da fegad lucht na cathrach ar inadaib aibne oirechtais, & ar muraib ardmoraib an baili.
Rabadar andsin 'na fiadnaisi daescursluagh dubach digair na Tiabanda, & a seanoraig snimacha ag sirthoirrsi, & maithreacha taebnochta ag trenguba, & naidin go tai ag geran do gleó na deisi sin.
Agus tangadar andsin a hifirn anmann in neoch domarbad do Thiabandaib & do Ghregaib ar cath na Teibi, co ralinsad an mag morreid a rabadar na milid sin, & co rabadar ag faidib & ag fedgairi & ag foluamain co hadfhuathmar da cach leith umpu.
Adchualaid immorro ant airdrig Adraist can toirmeasg o Tiabandaib ar tachur na deisi sin, & ragreis a each aterro co hathlam da n-edarscarad.
Et raidis and:
‘A Ghregu & a Thiabanda,’ ar se, ‘toirmisgid na fira-sa da fingail, & a Eitiocleis,’ ar se, ‘cid ad eascara, an agamsa;, a Pholiniceis, masa roshaint rigi fuil agad, ag siud rigi na n-Greg duit & toirmisc do chomrag.’
Ní mó trá dochualadar-san sin na ralabairthea risin muir duasanaig turcarthaig can anad da glór & da gredan timcheall an betha.
Agus o rafheimid Adraist dedail na deisi sin, & adchondairc a n-eocha tenda ag trenshibal, & a slega suainmeacha 'ca seoladh as a meraib seta sithgeala, roimpó uaithib dochum a longpuirt, & doleig coimdisli iter na curadaib da eís.
Rabái tra an toici aga toirmesc thoitmi isinn uair bicc sin, uair dogresedar a n-eocha bá dó dochum aroili.
Ní thug nech dib goin na aladh for a cheili re hathlaime a n-inggabala & re febhus in imditin tucsat na trenmilid for aroile, & roleigsed an tresfeacht a srein co lag asa lamaib, & rogreiseadar co hainmín na heocha i sboraib aithgera iarnaidi.
Adchondcadar treinfhir thenda na Tiabanda & gaisgedaig gloindmera na n-Greg.
Racoimergedar do chosnum a triath & a tigerna isinn eigin irgaili a rabadar.
tra acht robái a tuicthi don dis sin tuitim re 'roili id_est Eitiocles & Polinices. Tainig bandei int shida id_est Pax, do dingnaib roglana riched dochum na cath cechtarda sin, cor-ba subach sidamailatorra fein, co raleigsead comrag do Eitiocles & do Polinices can chungnam ré nechtar dib.
Is de sin rahadandait ferga ficthecha firmora isna feraib sin, & roduraigestar na crideda croda cosnamacha dochum araili.
Ba huchbad aín da n-oirechtaib beith ag fegad na fingaili sin.
Uair ba cosmaili gnuisi na ngaisgedach fa cathbarraib ailli ordaigi.
Ba hiardaigi aenmathar & ba haithni aenathar curaid croda cosnamach in comlaind sin, ger-ba ainindeach ré 'roili isin uair sin.
Is andsin tra seolais an rí ogal anrata id_est Eitiocles, an sleig taidlig dulfaebraig dochum Poliniceis.
Fuirmis Polinices an sciath 'na hagaid cur-sceind di amal carraicc.
No-bertaigis Polinices an sleig suainmig sithfada rabai 'na laim, & raidis:
‘A dei nime,’ ar se, ‘seolaid in urchur-sa & idberad-sa me fein daib as mo rigi ar mbreith choscair an churad so.’
Agus o raraid-sium sin, athchuiris uad an sleig, coma hairgi astoid on tsliasaid co 'raill do eoch Eitiocleis in birbodba sin.
O ragonad int each, roling co hathlam, & robris a srian, & rogab ar luaimnig & ar lanmeraigecht, coma forderg forruad da fuil cach conair concingead.
Failtigis Polinices don gnim sin, & greisis co hathlam a each da indsaig, & cu racomraigidar srein na heachraidi & lama na laechraidi & airm na n-airsed a n-aeninad.
Et o racomraigsed, torbiris cach dib laim a timcheall araile, co rathuitsed da n-echaib, feib tiastais ré haill no re hanborus.
Raeirgedar fo chetoir a n-aenfecht co hainmin agarb dochum araili, & rochomraig doib a n-ingnais a n-each.
Et bá hé dlus a comraig cona facus fairgsi na fordelugud iter na feraib isinn uair sin, coma comcheangailti a cathbairr & a claidmi, & coma comascda lama na laechraidi ag trenoirrleach aroili, amar da leoman loindmera, no mar da thiger trena thnuthacha, no mar da nathraig níata nemneacha.
tra acht rotholl & rothrengon cach aroili dib andsin, coma criathir chomtholl cnes chechtair de; & ger-b imda na halaid andsin arna hairsidaib, ní riachtadar gona aigbeili eislindi o cach dib ara cheili risin ré sin. Nir-bá cain tra cairdess na deisi derbrathar sin, uair fa santaigi re cechtar dib togail & tinnsadain fola a corp a cheili ina imdegail & didin a taeib bodeisin.
Agus is andsin tra furmis & fordingis Polinices mór mac Eidip in claidim claislethan curata rabai 'na laim a cnes a brathar co rug urraind n-eslinn trena chliab & trena cridhi.
O raairig immorro Eitiocles a arrach desin, fuirmis a sciath ara scath, & triallais teitheadh asin tres, & a brathair d'imgabail.
Leanais immorro Polinices é, & trenbuailis a sgiath air.
Et raidis:
‘Ca leth trialltar an teithed idir?’ arse.
‘Et is nair duit, a gilla, rigi & flaithius gus aníu agat, & loingsech lansiblach mar misi dod marbad.’
O 'dchualaid Eitiocleis sin, roimpo co cealgach cruadcrideach, & roleig tend a droma re tenntaib talman, & roindill a arm air anuas.
O 'dchondairc immorro na Tiabanda sin, tucsad gairi duba & domenman os aird, co roibi a macalla a fedaib & a foithrib na crich comfhogus.
Rothindisnaig Polinices dochum a brathar fai sin, & is ed doraid ris:
‘Maith tra lium t'aiscin mar tai adrasta,’ ar se, ‘id_est do rosc ruibnech roglas ag dorchachad ad chind, & do gnuis glan gruadalaind ac garbad & ac glasad fort, & airrdena ega ag taidecht dod t'insaigid.
Et a firu,’ ar se, ‘tabraid fleisc na rigi dam, co faicea Eitiocles am laim hí re siu bhagaba bass.’
Et is cuma doraid-sium sin & rothoirind ar Eitiocles do buain a airm & a edaig de da n-idbairt dona deib amal rogeall roime.
Et imarro dobai-sium ana sduaig moir mileata os cind Eitiocleis ag triall a fuidb do buain de, saithis Eitiocles an claidim aniss a n-uchtbruinde Poliniceis, conisfagaib 'na chliab ar scaltad a chridi.
Et fuair fein bass fo chetoir a ndiaid an gnima sin.
Is ed roraid immorro Polinices ar tabairt na gona digla sin air:
‘A mibraithir,’ ar se, ‘as fata rochuimnigis do chealga & t'aininde, & tu re bruinne bais, no co torchar-sa let.’
Et o raraid-sium sin, torchair 'na cosair cró a cend a brathar, & fuaradar araen bass & oiged fochetoir isin choimlepaid sin.
O 'dchualaid immorro an seanoir dall id_est Eidip, athair na deisi sin, bas d'fhagbail do chach dib ré cheili, ba mór a uchbad & a eigen lais an scel sin do cloistecht.
Et roerig co hoband & a ingen fá laim id_est Antigoine.
raraid ria:
‘Maith, a ingen,’ ar se, ‘tabair eolas dam co hairm a fuilet mo mic ar na marbad.’
Is andsin tainig in ingen roime tresin n-ar cosan inad a rabadar an dias sin id_est Eitiocles & Polinices.
Et o rangadar na curpu, rofobradar nuallguba n-adbail do denam, & is ed doraid Eidip andsin:
‘Is cumthach mo chridi-si adrasta os bar cinn, a macu,’ ar se, ‘ger-sa miscais cos aníu sib, as inmmain atrasda; & scail, a ingen, corpu na fer,’ arse, ‘co loiger atorro ar medon.’
Et is amlaid doraid-sium sin & rosin an laim ag iarraid airm na miled da marbad bodein.
O 'dchondairc immorro a ingen sin, roedla uaid na harma, & rofholaig air iad, & o nach fuair-sium na harmu, rogab denmne & dasacht hé, & rabai ag guba truim toirrsig os cind na fher.
Imtusa Iochasta immorro id_est mathair na mac, tainig seig amach fa na faidib firtruagha sin & sedfine na fer sin 'na laim id_est claidim lethan Laiiuis, athar Eidip, & tainig leiss ar mur na Teibi, & roleig co comthrom 'man claidim sin hí, co fhuair bas 'sa chetoir andsin do chumaid a mac.
Táinig immorro a hingen id_est Antigoine, & rabai a guba & a geran co mor ‘os do chind.’
Ba truag trá an timtochell toicten doronad andsin id_est in lucht rochathaig & rochuiblengaig 'man rigi sin, nach iad dochaith a maithius na a somaine acht a n-escaraid; uair rorigsad na tuatha Tiabanda sin Créón curata do shil cosnamach Caithim mic Aigenoir andsin ar marbad Eitiocleis.
Et ar bithin a mac do thoirbert fein tar cend choscair do Thiabandaib, tucsad-sam rigi don fhir sin, & is é cetsmacht rigi do ordaigh-sium andsin id_est can duine do Gregaib do loscad na d'adlucadh i tir na Teibi acht a leigin fá eathaidib áeoir & fa chuanartaib con allaid.
Et raerig andsin Creón a n-agaid Eidip mic Laiiuis, & is ed doraid ris:
‘Na tairr isin Teib, & na benad do chol na do chorbad rind, acht dentar aitt & adba duit a fedaib & a fhasach na Teibi, uair dothuitsed do mic tred mignimaib féin.’
Sochtais bar Eidiph o 'dchualaid sin, & rolinad o feirg & o londus adbal é, & is ed roraidh co loindeach lanfergach:
‘Is truag am linde,’ ar se, ‘an toicthi Thiabanda dorochtain ag duiligthi mar thussa do chur a rigi & a flaithus tar eis na rig rodileas robái remad indti.’
Et robai-sium amlaid sin ag tainsium & ag tarcaisne ar Créon co moradbal.
Ralabair immorro Antigoine ré Creón, & is ed asbert ris:
‘Tigead do chraide oraind, a Chreón,’ ar si, ‘& na tabair dod t'airi briathra an duine doilig dicheillid-si, & dober-sa air,’ ar si, ‘fognam & fomamugud deit, & ni leigfigther a teamplaib caema coisergtha na a n-inadaib aibne oireachtais ad t'fhiadnaisi-siu hé.’ tra acht tainig aignedh Creoin andsin ar briathraib na hingine, & raidis ria:
‘Leigfer, a ingen, deit-si sin,’ ar se, ‘& dentar aidi & adba dó i sleib Citharon a comfhogus don Teib, & bid andsin é can cheim isin cathraig-si d'ar n-indsaigi-ne.’
Et o raraid Creon na briathra sin, deisid ina rigda isin chathraig & maithi na Tiabanda maraen ris.
Imthusa na n-Greg immorro, o thainig in adaig da n-indsaigid, roimtigsed a n-élod a n-urtosach na haidchi sin, & rofhagsad a longphort lanfolam & treba na Teibi da n-eiss.
Nir-togad tra mergeda ré milid Greg agonn imthecht sin, na taisig ré na trenfheraib, na uirrig ré n-airechtaib, acht dochuaid cach dib ar athgairid eolais reime dochum a chrichi & a chineoil, & ba ferr daib na tiastais an tangadar.
'Ma Tiabanda, immorro, ba fada leo in adaig sin can cuirp a carad & a cumthach d'adlucud & d'anorugud, & ní thugsad da n-uid na da n-airi dala na n-Greg in aidchi sin.
Et o tainig an la cona lanshoillsi arnamarach, raeirgedar co moch na Tiabanda, & dochuadar isin n-armach, & dobadar co cend tri lá & tri n-aidchi ag loiscib & ag adlucad a caem & a carad in neoch dothuit dib re Gregaib.
Nir miad immorro ré Créon a mhac do loscad ider na corpaib sin na Tiabanda id_est Menicius; & dotinoilead ré Creón sceith & slega na n-Greg in neoch rafhagbaid isin n-armuig, & dorindead leis aentine dib, & roloisced leis corp a mhic isin teinid adbail idbarta sin.
Et o tairnig ré Tiabandaib na teintIsin do denam & na cuirp do loscad & d'adlucud, dochuadar 'na cathraig arsin, & dobadar co fledach fosaid inti.
Adchualadar tra banntracht na n-Grec na scela sin, & adchualaid Argía, ingen alaind Adraist, ben Poliniceis a ceili do marbad and.
Et o 'dchualaid, dothuit.
Rothuitsed taissi & taimnella fuirri don sgel sin, & doerig eistib ar n-uair, & is ed doraid:
‘Rachad-sa trá,’ ar si, ‘co roisir an Teib con fhaiciur corp cnisgeal mo cetmunnteri can a legad d'ethaidib imluaimnecha aeoir na do chuanartaib craesacha con.’
Is andsin rochoimeirig-sí roimpi risin toisc sin, & nir luga snim a saethar id_est Defili, ingen rig Greg, ben Tid, mic rig Calidoine, ac cainead a fir fan samla cetna.
Ba buaidirthi immorro bean Ipimedon dona scelaib sin id_est Neiccea a hainm, ingen rig na n-Aithininnsta, & nir luga easbaid Athlainti id_est mathar Partanapeuis, and, & ba chumthach dono bancheili Chapaneiuis id_est Euadne, id_est ingen in rig na n-Eberda.
Et tangadar sin rompo co toirseach cumthach, & Airgia rompo, dochum na Tebi, & tugsadar Iunaind ilchrothach sligeda seachmaill seach na Greic dona mnaib sin id_est do sleib Ismos & do chathraig Eiusis.
Is andsin dorala aenfher do Grecaib ar cáe meraigthi dona mnaib sin isin sligid id_est Ornitus a ainm, & o 'dchualaid sestan & medair na mban, sochtais fair, & aithniss iád, & caidhis leo, ar ba mor a truaighe & raidis riú:
‘A bandtracht gruadglan Greg,’ ar se, ‘ca leth teigthi?
Et an sailti amlaid anor d'fadbail agaib & ag Creon claencholach?
Et is í mo chomairli-si daib can techt an turuis sin, uair ní leigfigter daib na cuirp da teigthi d'iarraid.
Is ed si cora daib, dul co hairm a fhuil Teiss, mac Eig, mic Neptuin, ag sruth thondglan Tearamón, ar mbuaidchoscair catha andsin do bandtrachtaib borrfadacha na Sceithia, & abraid ris ar in mbaid mbunaid dul lib do digail bar cend ar Créon croda eolach.
Et cuimnighedh dó bes co rotoit Partanapeus mac Meliager re Tiabandaib, uair comalta comgaiscedach dosum Meliager & ni maithfea do Tiabandaib mac a chomalta & a chompanaig do chomach.’
O 'dchualaid na mná sin, robadar drem dib aga nertadh dul co Teib a chedoir.
Rabadar dono drem eili dib aga rad bá cora dul co Teiss.
Acht cena rochind Argia dul co Teib can fuireach idir ar gradh chuirp a chaemcheili, & asbert risna mnaib ar chena:
‘Eirgid-si dochum Theiss, & sirid fortacht fair, & rachad-sa co Teib & m'oidi Menetess maraen rium, uair ataid seathracha & carait mo cheili innti.’
Et dodealaigsed amlaid sin, & dochuaid Argia & a hoidi isin sligid a tainig Ornitus tré fedaib foithremla fasaig & tresna cailltib dluithi doimtheachta & dar cnocaib cendgarba cairrgecha co riachtadar sliabh Penith a comfhogus don Teib.
Et raidis andsin ria:
‘Adar lium-sa, a ingen,’ ar se, ‘as fagus an Teib duind, uair ad-cluinim-si anoisi brentada buaidirthi mora & foscad & fuaimneach na n-ethaidega ag eirgi dona habaigib isinn armach.’
Adchualaid in ingen sin & sochtais fuirri, & tug treall a thoirrse & ar comrath cumthach uaithi risin cathraig, uair tall ceill do rignacht na cathrach, & tainig asa haithli co tech aegairi ba coimnesa di isint sleib.
Adhnais & fhadaigis di tiruairsin teinid bigi bai as dig, co racomlasadar na haithindeada, & o ralasadar, dobean-si aithindi dib, & roeirig sí, & dogab athinni crithrech comlasamain dib ré heolus na haidchi d'iarraid chuirp a ceili.
Rathoirmisc Menetess uimpi-sIsin conna faictis na Tiabanda taidlech in athindi isinn aidchi sin.
Indsaigid in armaig arsin, & sirit co rafegaid co fuireachair leo cind curad arna comach & taib tholla trenfher & cnis gonta gaisgedaig na n-Grec ag iarraid Poliniceis moir mic Eidip & na miled Grecach ar chena.
Is and doerig Iunaind ilchrothach a himdaid Ioif mic Saduirn d'iarraid fortachta & fhoirithni do Gregaib ar Menerba ar bande an gaisgid airm a roibi caithir Theiss, mic Eig, mic Neptuin.
Et ag dul do Iunaind risin toisc sin, adchondairc Airgia, ingin Adraist, ag siredh in aír do churp a caemcheili a ndorcadaid na haidchi.
Ragreis Iunaind andsin bandei na haidchi id_est Luna um soillsiugud do Airgia no ga fadba corp a Is andsin rosoillsig luna maigi & tulcha & an talam & o rashoillsig, aithnis Airgia uaithi corp & cumthach a caemcheili Poliniceis, mic Eidip.
Et saigis da indsaigid & adchondairc an mígne marbda bai fora ceili.
Tainig anbaindi 'na hanmain & tam ar a tengaid & ceo cumad tar a rosc, & leigis 'na loigi fair hí, & pogais an gilla, & asa haithlIsin raidis ris:
‘Is truag atathar andsin adrasta, a gilla,’ ar si, ‘& is at fudammanta firdoimne na halaid fiarledarthe confer do brathair fort, & fá tren damsa ag toirmesc umat in turais-sa & dursan nacha-ranais agam & biaid do mac becc 'com choimdingnadh tar h'eis id_est Tesanndrus mac Poliniceis, & ní ricfa ceili eili mo chneas-sa na mo choimleabaid tar th' eis ar th' inmoine.
Et dursan ar coimriachtain intan conrangus icon cathraig alaind Adraist, & is fada bam comthach-sa dod bas ar t'eis.’
Acus antan robai-si 'con nuallguba sin, is and tainig amach asin Teib Ainntigoine, siur Poliniceis & Eotiocleis & aithindi lasamain 'na laim ag dul d'adlucad a braithrech.
Et is a ngoid dochuaid sí an toisc sin, uair nir-lamh ré Créón dul cosaird do loscad chorp a braithrech.
Et o 'dchondairc Airgia a farrad na fer, labrais ría:
‘Gabadh cia sud?’ arsi.
Ní rafhregair Airgia di ar met a huaman.
Labrais Antigoine an dara fecht, & is ed asbert:
‘A duine,’ ar sí, ‘nach gabad egla & misi Antigoine, siur na fer os atai a cind? arna deib rit, cid bé cia thú, tabair congnam dam a comlosgud a corp.’
O 'dchulaid Airgia sin, ba failid a haigned de, & dorigne a sloindead di,:
‘Masa thusa sin,’ ar si, ‘is im-si Airgia, ingen Adraist, bean Poliniceis.’
Comaiscsit andsin a n-aenmaigin os cind na corp & comlaigid forro & badar and ac comrath & ac comtoirrsi id_est Airgia ag indisin scel & tesmolta a fir Poliniceis, Antigoine ag adhmolad & ag fhaisneis scel Eitiocleiss.
Ba fada ré Menetes, ré hoiti Airgia, robai ina farrad, a comrath 'na inngnais & raidis riú:
‘Caisgid bar comrath,’ ar se, ‘& denaid iní ras-tangabair, & is deread don aidchi, & ata an lá ac coimthriall chugaib.’
Et is andsin doeirgedar a triur, & rotogbadar 'ma seach leo cuirp na fer sin Eotiocleis & Poliniceis co himlib srotha Ismen, rabai a comfhogus don Teib.
Et o raglansad andsin curpu na curad o thondaib srotha alaind Ismen, fuaradar teinid a crand a comfhogus doib arna marthain tre chumachtaib na ndee and, & rofhadodar-sam tor teinead romoire do chrinach & do chomlasamain na cailleadh, & dochuirsed na curpu fuirri ba chetoir, & rabadar na cuirp ac comlasadh, & rodianscailsed, & rodelaig an teine & an buinde lasamain lasrach baí uastu a comartha eassaentaga & ainindi na deisi asa cuirp rabái Et intan robadar fan samla sin, tainig torand bres adbalmor and, co rachrithnaigsed tuir & tigi na Tebi, cor-erigsedar fairiri & forcoimedaid an baili, & tangadar milid na cathrach amach ar an mag mor reidh.
O 'dchondairc Meinitess, ragab eagla mor hé, & rabadar na mna agan teinid can eagla Chreoin na a muntire forro, uair ba ferrdi leó bass d'fadbail o rasiacht leó aní rus-tangadar.
Et robadar aga indisi a n-ardchomrath atorra, co cluindis munter an rig mar thugsad leo na curpu co hairm a rabadar, & o 'dclos íad fan samla sin, docuas da n-indsaigid.
Roceanglaid & rochuibrigid íad & rugaid a forcho-mal dochum Chreón cholaigh.
Dala Airgia mná Poliniceis conuigi sin.
Toichestal na mban n-Grecach so sís.
Imthusa immorro na mban dochuaid d'iarraid fhoirithne ar Theis, mac Eigh, mic Neptain, rangadar co hathlum co cathraig Theis, & ni roiue Teis annsa chathraig in tan sin, & rofhiarfacht doib isin baili can a cinel, & cid ní risi ndechadar.
Rofregradar-sam a n-aenfhecht, & roindisedar tachar na Tiabanda & na n-Greg & claenbhreth Creoin can chuirp na n-Greg do legan do loscad ná do lesubad 'na tir na 'na talmain.
Et o raindisedar na scela sin, is and dobaí altoir alaind idbarta ar lár an baili, arna coisegrad do dee na trocairi id_est Misericordia, & fidnemad fhoithreamail 'ma thimcheall.
Et ní ba dilmain do duine dul chum na haltora sin acht do dainib uaisli robid i n-egindail & i ndochumal, & dochuadar na mna da hindsaigidh d'iarraid furtachta fuirri, & antan robadar ag iarraid a n-itchi um fhoirithin agon altoir, is andsin adchualadar an suba & in somenmain & na gairi comaidmi amuich ar an fhaithchi.
Agus is é dobai andsin, Teis, mac Eig, mic Neftuin & coscur & comaidim na Sceithia tuaiscertaigi aigi o shleib Boir.
Et tangadar amach andsin lucht an baili iter mnaib & feraib do fhegad Theiss um fhoirithin.
Et uma robai-sium amlaid & sceith na Sceitheagda 'na thimcheall, carpaid & cloidmi na Cichloiscthi; & Ipoliti rigan na Cichloiscthi, a carbad chaemcheithirriada ar eachaib ailli allmarda aengela 'na farrad.
Is andsin tangadar mna buaidirthi badbchaeintecha tamacha toirrseacha na n-Grec dochum an gilla sin.
Aithnigis-sium iad, & fiarfaigis scela dib.
Rafhregair Euogeini, ben Capaneiuis, dó, & is ed isbert fris:
‘A thren-milid, a Theiss,’ ar si, ‘an cualadais ar na n-Grec do chur do Thiabandaib ad ingnais & a righe do marbad?
Et a hArgus tangamar-ni id_est a cathraig oireachais na n-Grec, & ba hiad ar fhir-ni na riga domarbad andsin.
Et rachind Créon ri na Teibi can a cuirp do lecin do loscad na d'adlucad 'na thir.
Et ar na dei rit-su, airchis dindi, & eirig d'adlucud na n-abach sin do bunadcineoil bodein.’
Et a ndebairt in ingen sin, is ed adrubradar na mna Fregrais Teis daib, & is ed doraid:
‘Ba sidamail trá dofhagbus-sa na Greig antan dochuadus-sa gusan Sceithia,, a Chreoin,’ ar se, ‘cid mo choscar-sa 'dchluintea-sa, nír-bo choir duit an cinnead sin do denam.’
Et cuma adbert sin & doraid ré araid id_est Flegeius:
‘Eirig romat co Teib a ghilla,’ ar se, ‘& abair ré Créón adlaicter leis na Gregaig no fhrithailead cathugud rim-sa.’
Et ger-ba toirrsecha na sluaig, tangadar araen ré Teis da sluagad.
Nir-leigead scailead na scandrad doib acht a mornertad ré Teís dochum na Teibi, & rothinoil fuillead sluag & sochraidi da n-indsaigid id_est fir indsi Barón do muir Thoirrian & indsi Maradón & indsi Piria & na cathrach Melena & Charna & Sermon & Salmis & Eiliusis.
Et dono dorachad Ipoleiti rigan na Cichloiscthi isin tinol sin mina thoirmisced Teiss uimpi, uair fá torrach uad fein Et is e toirrches rouái aici andsin Uirbius mac Ipolite, & is ris atberur Uirbius Uirbibens his, & ni ho athair id_est o Teis mac Eig sloinnter in mac sin acht o mhathair id_est Ipolite.
Et is e tainic a sochraidi Thuirn mic Duin i n-aigid Ainiasa ar cathugud na hEdaille & na Rutulla.
arba do Grecaibh bunadh-cinel Tuirn, conadh aire sin tainic Uirbius mac Teis & Ipolite a cathugud na Rutalla a n-aigid Troighinach & Ainiasa & do chumgnam le Rutallaibh. Et is e sin tindrem genemna Uirbius & is e roatnuighsit na dei fá dó iarna marbad tre fochann a lesmathar.
Et o dariachtadar na sluaigh sin co haeninad, is ed doraid Teiss riú:
‘A firu,’ ar se, ‘comdaingnigid bar n-aigenta, & teindeasnaigi co Teib can anad a llo no a n-aidchi no co roisti da hindsaigid.’
Is andsin roeirgedar an morsochraidIsin co rachrithnaig an talam ré miri na midach ba na milidaib & ré trethan na curad comnart ag comtindinus dochum an catha, cor-ba ród robuan ina criaid chomsuaiti cróderg cach mag reid roglas tara teigdiss an sluag sin, & ba soillsi slesa na sleibteg secha tigdis re taitnem na n-arm loindreach lasamain badar uastu, & ba hadbal a fogar bres isinn aér uastu, re crithgair a n-arm n-examla n-urnochta ag buain ré aroili.
Et robái comtnúth mór acco ag cosnam thosaig do rochtain dochum na Teibi da togail.
Ba suaithnigta an rí romor gasta roalaind 'ma roibi an shochraidIsin id_est Teis, mac Eíg.
Uair is amlaid robái & dealba na n-indsed fair & na n-oilen & na cathrach rochosain, & dealb an muntuirc no an minituir ramarb i n-ínis Creid arna rindad a slesaib an sceith chuanda chobradaig rabai air, cor-bá buaidred da bidbadaib antan concingead cath sillead for an sciath n-ilbrec n-examail sin; & tangadar rompo fan samla sin dochum na Teibi can anad.
Imthusa na Tiabanda risi sin, rugad leo Airgia, ingen Adraist, & Antigoine, ingen Eidip, tar mur an baili amach da marbad.
Et antan rothriallad an gnim sin, is and dosiacht Flegeius, gilla Teiss, da n-indsaigid; & is e in gille sin dothoirmisc na mna do marbad, & ní cet sida doshir acht is cath rofhogair:
‘Ag sin,’ ar se, ‘Teis mac Eigh cona morsochraidi.’
O 'dchualaid immorro Creón an scel sin, is ed doraid:
‘Ba lór am do Gregaib ar-marbsamair-ne chena dib; & gid ed tised anoisi, fagebtha an cetna do denam’ Et ní thairnig dosum sin do rada in uair adchondairc na claicthigi ciach & na neoill coilli comdluithi os na sluagaib tendtalchairda robadar araen re Teis.
Greisis Créon, & tindesnaigis na Tiabanda do chur chatha re Teis mac Eig.
Ba haidleasc amh ré Tiabandaib sin, uair fa ledarthi a lama.
ba tollta a taib, & fa creachtacha a cnís, & ba minaigthi mur a cathrach umpu; & gid ead roeirgedar ré gresacht a rig, & rothrélmaigsed a n-armu co hathlam.
Is andsin immorro rolinsad sluaig athlama echtacha na hAthaine re tosach an laí mag na Teibi tondglaisi 'na timcheall, & ba farrach daib ré fulang an brentatu buaidirthi roeirig dona hapaigib 'can athgluasacht fo a cosaib isin muig.
Et raidis Teis aga faicsin:
‘Ni maith,’ ar se, ‘an anoir dorad Creon dona corpaib-si, & ní huasal dobai riu can a cuirp do loscad no d'adlucad, & ní coimdi duindi cath do chur an bail atad so, & tigid romaib ar inad reid roglan na fuilet apaigi, co laieam gléo and & na Tiabanda.’
Is andsin coimindsaigid na catha ceachtarda dochum aroile.
Tincaid na Tiabanda co tái toirrsech an tres.
Indsaigid immorro na hAaithinnsda co tend tomaithmech an tres.
Et togbais andsin Theis, mac Eig, an sleg Maratonda raibái 'na laim, coma samalta ré foscad fidbaidi firairdi anellchroda comdorcha craind na sleigi sin, & coma samaltha re rind roglan ruithnigthech soillsi slendand na s--leigi sin, consoillsiugad an mag ara rabadar na sluaig.
Et o 'dchondcadar na Tiabanda an tómaithem sin, nir-fhulaing doib anad ris, acht roimpotar a mergedha maithsroill & romebaid raen romadma dib dochum a cathrach.
Nír miad am le Téis lenmain an lochta sin, uair dochind can fer timteitheadach do marbad, & robadar daescursluag athlam Athaine ar chena aga n-oirrlech.
Anais amh Olenius do Thiabandaib & Tamerus trenfer ag eisimal tar eis a mhunntire.
Dibraigis Teiss co hindilldireach iat co torchradar leis.
Is andsin dono roansad tri mic Ailisis do Tiabandaib re munntir Teis id_est Piliius & Elops & Iapix, & fersad comland riu, & fegais Teis an treas sin, & diubraigis can toirisim can toirmisc iad, coma triur tretholl arna tuitim da eis.
Triallais Emon echtach mac Creón Teis d'indsaigid co hairm a roibi, & bertnaigís Téis ant sleig n-agmair n-urbadaig, & dobret urchar d'Emon di, co torchair can anmain an tres gaisgedach na Tiabanda.
Gairmis immorro, & grendaigis Teis Creon, ri na Teibi, o guth mor do chomrag ris ar toitim a mic da laim.
Tincais Creon croda sin, & impais a munnter leis.
Athchuris Teis a munntir bodein uadh, & anais a aenur ar cind Creon cona munntir.
Et raidis Creon ris:
‘A gilla,’ ar se, ‘ca dasacht & ca drochciall dobeir ort mo grendugud-sa do chomlond rit?
an faicend tu Tit, mac Aeniasa, mac rig na Cailidoine, ar toitim lind, & Ipimedon gruadsolus & Capaneius & Partanopeius & maithi Greg archena do thoitim lind?’
Et o raraid-sium sin, tug urchar dochum Theis cor-ben a mbili n-uachtarach a sceith.
Tibis Teis gen gairi imi sin, & raidis:
‘A anmanda na n-Greg,’ ar se, ‘fhoslaigid doirrsi adfhuathmara ifirn, co cuirer Creón chugaib ind.’
Et doteilg an sleig mor Marathonda bái 'na laim do Creon, cur-ben a n-eislind a chuirp tre berna a luirigi, co rug mili arrindi trena chnes.
Tuitid Creon do goin an gaisgedaig sin can atharrach can atheirgi do, & raidis Teis:
‘An tibri anois,’ arse, ‘cedugud comloiscthi ar chorpu na n-Grec & inad adnacail doib?
Et ber-si let sin,’ ar se, ‘ad chintaib fein, & rod-aidlecthar cen cur-dligar a denam.’
Is andsin tra rotimsaigid na tuatha Tiabanda & oirechta na hAithine 'ma Teis, mac Eig, mic Neptuin.
Et rocreidsit do uili & rachindsed a chumthanus andsin, & rashnaimsed sith suthain aterru, & rugsad leó Teiss isin cathraig, & roeirgedar mna & maccaeim an baili d'anorugud & d'admolad an gilla sin, & robai isin Teib re hed na haidchi sin.
tra acht ba hairdri ar gasraid Grec Teis dar eis Adraist o Traicia a tuaigh co muir Repalia bhu dhes & o cind sleibe aird Olimp & o sruth roglan Re? anoir co rind mara hAidhriadh siar.
Na mna immorro rogabad la Creon rofhosclad dibh la Teis id_est Airgia ingen Adraist & Ismene ingen Eidhiph.
Roan immorro ingen Eidhip isin Teibh.
Et docuaidh Airgia co Larisa.
Et ua truagh scith imsnimach a scaradh na mban sin ri aroili.
Et rouai Airgia andsin co cumtach, toirsech, dercaintech.
Et ní airmit scribhenna feis re fer di dar eis a cetmuintire co nd-erbailt fo deoidh do chumaid Poliniceis.
Et rogabh a mac id_est Tesanndrus mac Poliniceis righi na Tiabanda, conadh e in sechtmad righ rouai ag togail Troe maraon re Grecaibh in Tesandorus sin.
Imtusa immorro an bantrachta Gregda risa tainig Teis an turus sin, raadlaicsed co hanorach & co huasal curpu a carad & a caemceilead, & dochuadar da trebaib & da tigib asa haithli co caeinteach easbadach.
Airim thrá ar-marbad andsin do rigaib & da daescursluagh diairmigthi.
Ní chuimnigid na sgribenda & scela discrirthecha deiligthi ar-fagbad beó and.
Ní sud consirther.
Conad ní da ngnimaib & da scelaib & da n-imteachtaib conuigi sin.
